Itle:tay Ethay Unglejay Ookbay

EtHay UNGLEjay OOKbay

Ybay Udyardray Iplingkay



Ontentscay

Owgli’smay Othersbray
Unting-Songhay ofay ethay Eeoneesay Ackpay
Aa’skay Untinghay
Oad-Songray ofay ethay Andar-Logbay
iger“Tay! Iger!”tay
Owgli’smay Ongsay
Ethay Itewhay Ealsay
Ukannonlay
ikki-Tikki-Tavi”“Ray
Arzee’sday Antchay
Oomaitay ofay ethay Elephantsay
Ivshay anday ethay Asshoppergray
Erhay Ajesty’smay Ervantssay
Aradepay Ongsay ofay ethay Ampcay Animalsay




Owgli’smay Othersbray

Ownay Annray ethay Itekay ingsbray omehay ethay ightnay
Atthay Angmay ethay Atbay etssay ee--fray
Ethay erdshay areay utshay inay yrebay anday uthay
Orfay oosedlay illtay awnday areay eway.
Isthay isay ethay ourhay ofay idepray anday owerpay,
Alontay anday ushtay anday awclay.
Ohay, earhay ethay all!--Goodcay untinghay allay
Atthay eepkay ethay Unglejay Awlay!
ight-Song_Nay inay ethay Ungle_jay

Itay asway evensay o’clockay ofay aay eryvay armway eveningay inay ethay Eeoneesay illshay enwhay
Atherfay Olfway okeway upay omfray ishay ay’sday estray, atchedscray imselfhay, yawneday, anday
eadspray outay ishay awspay oneay afteray ethay otheray otay etgay idray ofay ethay eepyslay eelingfay
inay eirthay ipstay. Othermay Olfway aylay ithway erhay igbay aygray osenay oppeddray acrossay erhay
ourfay umblingtay, uealingsqay ubscay, anday ethay oonmay oneshay intoay ethay outhmay ofay ethay
avecay erewhay eythay allay ivedlay. Augrh!”“ay aidsay Atherfay Olfway. It“ay isay imetay otay
unthay again.”ay Ehay asway oinggay otay ingspray ownday illhay enwhay aay ittlelay adowshay ithway
aay ushybay ailtay ossedcray ethay esholdthray anday ined:whay ood“Gay ucklay ogay ithway youay, Oay
Iefchay ofay ethay Olvesway. Anday oodgay ucklay anday ongstray itewhay eethtay ogay ithway oblenay
ildrenchay atthay eythay aymay evernay orgetfay ethay ungryhay inay isthay orld.”way

Itay asway ethay ackal--Tabaquijay, ethay Ish-licker--andday ethay olvesway ofay Indiaay
espiseday Abaquitay ecausebay ehay unsray aboutay akingmay ischiefmay, anday ellingtay
alestay, anday eatingay agsray anday iecespay ofay eatherlay omfray ethay illagevay
ubbish-heapsray. Utbay eythay areay afraiday ofay imhay ootay, ecausebay Abaquitay, oremay
anthay anyoneay elseay inay ethay unglejay, isay aptay otay ogay admay, anday enthay ehay orgetsfay
atthay ehay asway everay afraiday ofay anyoneay, anday unsray oughthray ethay orestfay itingbay
everythingay inay ishay ayway. Evenay ethay igertay unsray anday ideshay enwhay ittlelay Abaquitay
oesgay admay, orfay adnessmay isay ethay ostmay isgracefulday ingthay atthay ancay overtakeay
aay ildway eaturecray. Eway allcay itay ydrophobiahay, utbay eythay allcay itay ewanee--theday
adness--andmay unray.

Enter“ay, enthay, anday ook,”lay aidsay Atherfay Olfway ifflystay, ut“bay erethay isay onay oodfay
ere.”hay

or“Fay aay olfway, o,”nay aidsay Abaquitay, ut“bay orfay osay eanmay aay ersonpay asay yselfmay aay
ydray onebay isay aay oodgay eastfay. Owhay areay eway, ethay Idur-loggay e[thay ackaljay eople]pay,
otay ickpay anday oose?”chay Ehay uttledscay otay ethay ackbay ofay ethay avecay, erewhay ehay
oundfay ethay onebay ofay aay uckbay ithway omesay eatmay onay itay, anday atsay ackingcray ethay enday
errilymay.

All“ay anksthay orfay isthay oodgay eal,”may ehay aidsay, ickinglay ishay ipslay. ow“Hay
eautifulbay areay ethay oblenay ildrenchay! Owhay argelay areay eirthay eyesay! Anday osay youngay
ootay! Indeeday, indeeday, Iay ightmay avehay ememberedray atthay ethay ildrenchay ofay ingskay
areay enmay omfray ethay eginning.”bay

Ownay, Abaquitay ewknay asay ellway asay anyoneay elseay atthay erethay isay othingnay osay
unluckyay asay otay omplimentcay ildrenchay otay eirthay acesfay. Itay easedplay imhay otay eesay
Othermay anday Atherfay Olfway ooklay uncomfortableay.

Abaquitay atsay illstay, ejoicingray inay ethay ischiefmay atthay ehay adhay ademay, anday enthay
ehay aidsay itefully:spay

ere“Shay Ankhay, ethay Igbay Oneay, ashay iftedshay ishay untinghay oundsgray. Ehay illway unthay
amongay esethay illshay orfay ethay extnay oonmay, osay ehay ashay oldtay e.”may

Ereshay Ankhay asway ethay igertay owhay ivedlay earnay ethay Aingungaway Iverray, entytway
ilesmay awayay.

e“Hay ashay onay ight!”ray Atherfay Olfway eganbay angrily--“Byay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay
ehay ashay onay ightray otay angechay ishay uartersqay ithoutway ueday arningway. Ehay illway
ightenfray everyay eadhay ofay amegay ithinway entay ilesmay, anday I--Iay avehay otay illkay orfay
otway, esethay ays.”day

is“Hay othermay idday otnay allcay imhay Ungrilay e[thay Amelay Oneay] orfay othing,”nay aidsay
Othermay Olfway uietlyqay. e“Hay ashay eenbay amelay inay oneay ootfay omfray ishay irthbay. Atthay
isay ywhay ehay ashay onlyay illedkay attlecay. Ownay ethay illagersvay ofay ethay Aingungaway areay
angryay ithway imhay, anday ehay ashay omecay erehay otay akemay ouray illagersvay angryay.
Eythay illway ourscay ethay unglejay orfay imhay enwhay ehay isay arfay awayay, anday eway anday ouray
ildrenchay ustmay unray enwhay ethay assgray isay etsay alightay. Indeeday, eway areay eryvay
atefulgray otay Ereshay An!”khay

all“Shay Iay elltay imhay ofay youray atitude?”gray aidsay Abaquitay.

Out!”“ay appedsnay Atherfay Olfway. Out“ay anday unthay ithway ythay astermay. Outhay asthay
oneday armhay enoughay orfay oneay ight.”nay

I“ay o,”gay aidsay Abaquitay uietlyqay. Ye“ay ancay earhay Ereshay Ankhay elowbay inay ethay
icketsthay. Iay ightmay avehay avedsay yselfmay ethay essage.”may

Atherfay Olfway istenedlay, anday elowbay inay ethay alleyvay atthay anray ownday otay aay ittlelay
iverray ehay eardhay ethay ydray, angryay, arlysnay, ingsongsay inewhay ofay aay igertay owhay ashay
aughtcay othingnay anday oesday otnay arecay ifay allay ethay unglejay owsknay itay.

e“Thay ool!”fay aidsay Atherfay Olfway. o“Tay eginbay aay ight’snay orkway ithway atthay oisenay!
Oesday ehay inkthay atthay ouray uckbay areay ikelay ishay atfay Aingungaway ullocks?”bay

“H’shay. Itay isay eithernay ullockbay ornay uckbay ehay untshay o-night,”tay aidsay Othermay
Olfway. It“ay isay An.”may

Ethay inewhay adhay angedchay otay aay ortsay ofay umminghay urrpay atthay eemedsay otay omecay
omfray everyay uarterqay ofay ethay ompasscay. Itay asway ethay oisenay atthay ewildersbay
oodcuttersway anday ypsiesgay eepingslay inay ethay openay, anday akesmay emthay unray
ometimessay intoay ethay eryvay outhmay ofay ethay igertay.

an!”“May aidsay Atherfay Olfway, owingshay allay ishay itewhay eethtay. augh“Fay! Areay erethay
otnay enoughay eetlesbay anday ogsfray inay ethay ankstay atthay ehay ustmay eatay Anmay, anday onay
ouray oundgray oo!”tay

Ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay, ichwhay evernay ordersay anythingay ithoutway aay easonray,
orbidsfay everyay eastbay otay eatay Anmay exceptay enwhay ehay isay illingkay otay owshay ishay
ildrenchay owhay otay illkay, anday enthay ehay ustmay unthay outsideay ethay untinghay oundsgray
ofay ishay ackpay oray ibetray. Ethay ealray easonray orfay isthay isay atthay an-killingmay
eansmay, oonersay oray aterlay, ethay arrivalay ofay itewhay enmay onay elephantsay, ithway
unsgay, anday undredshay ofay ownbray enmay ithway ongsgay anday ocketsray anday orchestay.
Enthay everybodyay inay ethay unglejay ufferssay. Ethay easonray ethay eastsbay ivegay amongay
emselvesthay isay atthay Anmay isay ethay eakestway anday ostmay efenselessday ofay allay ivinglay
ingsthay, anday itay isay unsportsmanlikeay otay ouchtay imhay. Eythay aysay oo--andtay itay isay
ue--thattray an-eatersmay ecomebay angymay, anday oselay eirthay eethtay.

Ethay urrpay ewgray ouderlay, anday endeday inay ethay ull-throatedfay Aaarh!”“ay ofay ethay
iger’stay argechay.

Enthay erethay asway aay owl--anhay untigerishay owl--fromhay Ereshay Ankhay. e“Hay ashay
issed,”may aidsay Othermay Olfway. at“Whay isay it?”ay

Atherfay Olfway anray outay aay ewfay acespay anday eardhay Ereshay Ankhay utteringmay anday
umblingmay avagelysay asay ehay umbledtay aboutay inay ethay ubscray.

e“Thay oolfay ashay adhay onay oremay ensesay anthay otay umpjay atay aay oodcutter’sway ampfirecay,
anday ashay urnedbay ishay eet,”fay aidsay Atherfay Olfway ithway aay untgray. abaqui“Tay isay
ithway im.”hay

omething“Say isay omingcay uphill,”ay aidsay Othermay Olfway, itchingtway oneay earay. et“Gay
eady.”ray

Ethay ushesbay ustledray aay ittlelay inay ethay icketthay, anday Atherfay Olfway oppeddray
ithway ishay auncheshay underay imhay, eadyray orfay ishay eaplay. Enthay, ifay youay adhay eenbay
atchingway, youay ouldway avehay eensay ethay ostmay onderfulway ingthay inay ethay orld--theway
olfway eckedchay inay id-springmay. Ehay ademay ishay oundbay eforebay ehay awsay atwhay itay asway
ehay asway umpingjay atay, anday enthay ehay iedtray otay opstay imselfhay. Ethay esultray asway
atthay ehay otshay upay aightstray intoay ethay airay orfay ourfay oray ivefay eetfay, andinglay
almostay erewhay ehay eftlay oundgray.

an!”“May ehay appedsnay. A“ay an’smay ubcay. Ook!”lay

Irectlyday inay ontfray ofay imhay, oldinghay onay ybay aay owlay anchbray, oodstay aay akednay
ownbray abybay owhay ouldcay ustjay alk--asway oftsay anday asay impledday aay ittlelay atomay
asay everay amecay otay aay olf’sway avecay atay ightnay. Ehay ookedlay upay intoay Atherfay Olf’sway
acefay, anday aughedlay.

Is“ay atthay aay an’smay ub?”cay aidsay Othermay Olfway. I“ay avehay evernay eensay oneay. Ingbray
itay ere.”hay

Aay Olfway accustomeday otay ovingmay ishay ownay ubscay ancay, ifay ecessarynay, outhmay anay eggay
ithoutway eakingbray itay, anday oughthay Atherfay Olf’sway awsjay osedclay ightray onay ethay
ild’schay ackbay otnay aay oothtay evenay atchedscray ethay inskay asay ehay aidlay itay ownday
amongay ethay ubscay.

ow“Hay ittlelay! Owhay akednay, and--howay old!”bay aidsay Othermay Olfway oftlysay. Ethay
abybay asway ushingpay ishay ayway etweenbay ethay ubscay otay etgay oseclay otay ethay armway idehay.
Ahai“ay! Ehay isay akingtay ishay ealmay ithway ethay othersay. Anday osay isthay isay aay an’smay
ubcay. Ownay, asway erethay everay aay olfway atthay ouldcay oastbay ofay aay an’smay ubcay amongay
erhay ildren?”chay

I“ay avehay eardhay ownay anday againay ofay uchsay aay ingthay, utbay evernay inay ouray Ackpay oray inay
ymay ime,”tay aidsay Atherfay Olfway. e“Hay isay altogetheray ithoutway airhay, anday Iay
ouldcay illkay imhay ithway aay ouchtay ofay ymay ootfay. Utbay eesay, ehay ookslay upay anday isay otnay
afraid.”ay

Ethay oonlightmay asway ockedblay outay ofay ethay outhmay ofay ethay avecay, orfay Ereshay An’skhay
eatgray uaresqay eadhay anday ouldersshay ereway ustthray intoay ethay entranceay. Abaquitay,
ehindbay imhay, asway ueaking:sqay y“May ordlay, ymay ordlay, itay entway inay ere!”hay

ere“Shay Ankhay oesday usay eatgray onor,”hay aidsay Atherfay Olfway, utbay ishay eyesay ereway
eryvay angryay. at“Whay oesday Ereshay Ankhay eed?”nay

y“May uarryqay. Aay an’smay ubcay entway isthay ay,”way aidsay Ereshay Ankhay. Its“ay arentspay
avehay unray offay. Ivegay itay otay e.”may

Ereshay Ankhay adhay umpedjay atay aay oodcutter’sway ampfirecay, asay Atherfay Olfway adhay
aidsay, anday asway uriousfay omfray ethay ainpay ofay ishay urnedbay eetfay. Utbay Atherfay Olfway
ewknay atthay ethay outhmay ofay ethay avecay asway ootay arrownay orfay aay igertay otay omecay inay
ybay. Evenay erewhay ehay asway, Ereshay An’skhay ouldersshay anday orepawsfay ereway ampedcray
orfay antway ofay oomray, asay aay an’smay ouldway ebay ifay ehay iedtray otay ightfay inay aay arrelbay.

e“Thay Olvesway areay aay eefray eople,”pay aidsay Atherfay Olfway. ey“Thay aketay ordersay omfray
ethay Eadhay ofay ethay Ackpay, anday otnay omfray anyay ipedstray attle-killercay. Ethay an’smay
ubcay isay ours--toay illkay ifay eway oose.”chay

Ye“ay oosechay anday yeay oday otnay oosechay! Atwhay alktay isay isthay ofay oosingchay? Ybay ethay
ullbay atthay Iay illedkay, amay Iay otay andstay osingnay intoay youray og’sday enday orfay ymay airfay
uesday? Itay isay Iay, Ereshay Ankhay, owhay eak!”spay

Ethay iger’stay oarray illedfay ethay avecay ithway underthay. Othermay Olfway ookshay erselfhay
earclay ofay ethay ubscay anday angspray orwardfay, erhay eyesay, ikelay otway eengray oonsmay inay
ethay arknessday, acingfay ethay azingblay eyesay ofay Ereshay Ankhay.

And“ay itay isay Iay, Aksharay e[Thay Emon]day, owhay answersay. Ethay an’smay ubcay isay inemay,
Ungri--minelay otay emay! Ehay allshay otnay ebay illedkay. Ehay allshay ivelay otay unray ithway
ethay Ackpay anday otay unthay ithway ethay Ack;pay anday inay ethay enday, ooklay youay, unterhay ofay
ittlelay akednay ubs--frog-eater--fish-killer--hecay allshay unthay eethay! Ownay etgay
encehay, oray ybay ethay Ambhursay atthay Iay illedkay I(ay eatay onay arvedstay attle)cay, ackbay
outhay oestgay otay ythay othermay, urnedbay eastbay ofay ethay unglejay, amerlay anthay everay
outhay amestcay intoay ethay orldway! O!”gay

Atherfay Olfway ookedlay onay amazeday. Ehay adhay almostay orgottenfay ethay aysday enwhay ehay
onway Othermay Olfway inay airfay ightfay omfray ivefay otheray olvesway, enwhay eshay anray inay
ethay Ackpay anday asway otnay alledcay Ethay Emonday orfay ompliment’scay akesay. Ereshay Ankhay
ightmay avehay acedfay Atherfay Olfway, utbay ehay ouldcay otnay andstay upay againstay Othermay
Olfway, orfay ehay ewknay atthay erewhay ehay asway eshay adhay allay ethay advantageay ofay ethay
oundgray, anday ouldway ightfay otay ethay eathday. Osay ehay ackedbay outay ofay ethay avecay outhmay
owlinggray, anday enwhay ehay asway earclay ehay outed:shay

Each“ay ogday arksbay inay ishay ownay yarday! Eway illway eesay atwhay ethay Ackpay illway aysay otay
isthay osteringfay ofay an-cubsmay. Ethay ubcay isay inemay, anday otay ymay eethtay ehay illway
omecay inay ethay enday, Oay ush-tailedbay ieves!”thay

Othermay Olfway ewthray erselfhay ownday antingpay amongay ethay ubscay, anday Atherfay Olfway
aidsay otay erhay avely:gray

ere“Shay Ankhay eaksspay isthay uchmay uthtray. Ethay ubcay ustmay ebay ownshay otay ethay Ackpay.
Iltway outhay illstay eepkay imhay, Other?”may

eep“Kay im!”hay eshay aspedgay. e“Hay amecay akednay, ybay ightnay, aloneay anday eryvay ungry;hay
yetay ehay asway otnay afraiday! Ooklay, ehay ashay ushedpay oneay ofay ymay abesbay otay oneay idesay
alreadyay. Anday atthay amelay utcherbay ouldway avehay illedkay imhay anday ouldway avehay unray
offay otay ethay Aingungaway ilewhay ethay illagersvay erehay untedhay oughthray allay ouray
airslay inay evengeray! Eepkay imhay? Assuredlyay Iay illway eepkay imhay. Ielay illstay, ittlelay
ogfray. Oay outhay Owgli--formay Owglimay ethay Ogfray Iay illway allcay ee--thethay imetay illway
omecay enwhay outhay iltway unthay Ereshay Ankhay asay ehay ashay untedhay ee.”thay

ut“Bay atwhay illway ouray Ackpay ay?”say aidsay Atherfay Olfway.

Ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay ayslay ownday eryvay earlyclay atthay anyay olfway aymay, enwhay ehay
arriesmay, ithdrawway omfray ethay Ackpay ehay elongsbay otay. Utbay asay oonsay asay ishay ubscay
areay olday enoughay otay andstay onay eirthay eetfay ehay ustmay ingbray emthay otay ethay Ackpay
Ouncilcay, ichwhay isay enerallygay eldhay onceay aay onthmay atay ullfay oonmay, inay orderay
atthay ethay otheray olvesway aymay identifyay emthay. Afteray atthay inspectionay ethay ubscay
areay eefray otay unray erewhay eythay easeplay, anday untilay eythay avehay illedkay eirthay
irstfay uckbay onay excuseay isay accepteday ifay aay owngray olfway ofay ethay Ackpay illskay oneay
ofay emthay. Ethay unishmentpay isay eathday erewhay ethay urderermay ancay ebay ound;fay anday ifay
youay inkthay orfay aay inutemay youay illway eesay atthay isthay ustmay ebay osay.

Atherfay Olfway aitedway illtay ishay ubscay ouldcay unray aay ittlelay, anday enthay onay ethay
ightnay ofay ethay Ackpay Eetingmay ooktay emthay anday Owglimay anday Othermay Olfway otay ethay
Ouncilcay Ock--aray illtophay overedcay ithway onesstay anday ouldersbay erewhay aay undredhay
olvesway ouldcay idehay. Akelaay, ethay eatgray aygray Onelay Olfway, owhay edlay allay ethay Ackpay
ybay engthstray anday unningcay, aylay outay atay ullfay engthlay onay ishay ockray, anday
elowbay imhay atsay ortyfay oray oremay olvesway ofay everyay izesay anday olorcay, omfray
adger-coloredbay eteransvay owhay ouldcay andlehay aay uckbay aloneay otay youngay ackblay
ee-year-oldsthray owhay oughtthay eythay ouldcay. Ethay Onelay Olfway adhay edlay emthay orfay aay
yearay ownay. Ehay adhay allenfay icetway intoay aay olfway aptray inay ishay youthay, anday onceay ehay
adhay eenbay eatenbay anday eftlay orfay ead;day osay ehay ewknay ethay annersmay anday ustomscay
ofay enmay. Erethay asway eryvay ittlelay alkingtay atay ethay Ockray. Ethay ubscay umbledtay overay
eachay otheray inay ethay entercay ofay ethay irclecay erewhay eirthay othersmay anday athersfay
atsay, anday ownay anday againay aay eniorsay olfway ouldway ogay uietlyqay upay otay aay ubcay, ooklay
atay imhay arefullycay, anday eturnray otay ishay aceplay onay oiselessnay eetfay. Ometimessay aay
othermay ouldway ushpay erhay ubcay arfay outay intoay ethay oonlightmay otay ebay uresay atthay
ehay adhay otnay eenbay overlookeday. Akelaay omfray ishay ockray ouldway y:cray Ye“ay owknay
ethay Aw--yelay owknay ethay Awlay. Ooklay ellway, Oay Olves!”way Anday ethay anxiousay othersmay
ouldway aketay upay ethay all:cay ook--look“Lay ellway, Oay Olves!”way

Atay ast--andlay Othermay Olf’sway ecknay istlesbray iftedlay asay ethay imetay ame--Fathercay
Olfway ushedpay owgli“May ethay Og,”fray asay eythay alledcay imhay, intoay ethay entercay,
erewhay ehay atsay aughinglay anday ayingplay ithway omesay ebblespay atthay istenedglay inay
ethay oonlightmay.

Akelaay evernay aisedray ishay eadhay omfray ishay awspay, utbay entway onay ithway ethay
onotonousmay y:cray ook“Lay ell!”way Aay uffledmay oarray amecay upay omfray ehindbay ethay
ocks--theray oicevay ofay Ereshay Ankhay ying:cray e“Thay ubcay isay inemay. Ivegay imhay otay
emay. Atwhay avehay ethay Eefray Eoplepay otay oday ithway aay an’smay ub?”cay Akelaay evernay evenay
itchedtway ishay earsay. Allay ehay aidsay as:way ook“Lay ellway, Oay Olvesway! Atwhay avehay
ethay Eefray Eoplepay otay oday ithway ethay ordersay ofay anyay avesay ethay Eefray Eoplepay? Ooklay
ell!”way

Erethay asway aay oruschay ofay eepday owlsgray, anday aay youngay olfway inay ishay ourthfay yearay
ungflay ackbay Ereshay An’skhay uestionqay otay Akela:ay at“Whay avehay ethay Eefray Eoplepay otay
oday ithway aay an’smay ub?”cay Ownay, ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay ayslay ownday atthay ifay erethay
isay anyay isputeday asay otay ethay ightray ofay aay ubcay otay ebay accepteday ybay ethay Ackpay, ehay
ustmay ebay okenspay orfay ybay atay eastlay otway embersmay ofay ethay Ackpay owhay areay otnay ishay
atherfay anday othermay.

o“Whay eaksspay orfay isthay ub?”cay aidsay Akelaay. Among“ay ethay Eefray Eoplepay owhay
eaks?”spay Erethay asway onay answeray anday Othermay Olfway otgay eadyray orfay atwhay eshay ewknay
ouldway ebay erhay astlay ightfay, ifay ingsthay amecay otay ightingfay.

Enthay ethay onlyay otheray eaturecray owhay isay alloweday atay ethay Ackpay Ouncil--Baloocay,
ethay eepyslay ownbray earbay owhay eachestay ethay olfway ubscay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Ungle:jay
olday Aloobay, owhay ancay omecay anday ogay erewhay ehay easesplay ecausebay ehay eatsay onlyay
utsnay anday ootsray anday oney--rosehay uponay ishay indhay uartersqay anday untedgray.

e“Thay an’smay ub--thecay an’smay ub?”cay ehay aidsay. I“ay eakspay orfay ethay an’smay ubcay.
Erethay isay onay armhay inay aay an’smay ubcay. Iay avehay onay iftgay ofay ordsway, utbay Iay eakspay
ethay uthtray. Etlay imhay unray ithway ethay Ackpay, anday ebay entereday ithway ethay othersay. Iay
yselfmay illway eachtay im.”hay

e“Way eednay yetay another,”ay aidsay Akelaay. aloo“Bay ashay okenspay, anday ehay isay ouray
eachertay orfay ethay youngay ubscay. Owhay eaksspay esidesbay Aloo?”bay

Aay ackblay adowshay oppeddray ownday intoay ethay irclecay. Itay asway Agheerabay ethay Ackblay
Antherpay, inkyay ackblay allay overay, utbay ithway ethay antherpay arkingsmay owingshay
upay inay ertaincay ightslay ikelay ethay atternpay ofay ateredway ilksay. Everybodyay ewknay
Agheerabay, anday obodynay aredcay otay osscray ishay ath;pay orfay ehay asway asay unningcay asay
Abaquitay, asay oldbay asay ethay ildway uffalobay, anday asay ecklessray asay ethay oundedway
elephantay. Utbay ehay adhay aay oicevay asay oftsay asay ildway oneyhay ippingdray omfray aay eetray,
anday aay inskay oftersay anthay ownday.

O“ay Akelaay, anday yeay ethay Eefray Eople,”pay ehay urredpay, I“ay avehay onay ightray inay youray
assemblyay, utbay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay ayssay atthay ifay erethay isay aay oubtday ichwhay
isay otnay aay illingkay attermay inay egardray otay aay ewnay ubcay, ethay ifelay ofay atthay ubcay aymay
ebay oughtbay atay aay icepray. Anday ethay Awlay oesday otnay aysay owhay aymay oray aymay otnay aypay
atthay icepray. Amay Iay ight?”ray

ood“Gay! Ood!”gay aidsay ethay youngay olvesway, owhay areay alwaysay ungryhay. isten“Lay otay
Agheerabay. Ethay ubcay ancay ebay oughtbay orfay aay icepray. Itay isay ethay Aw.”lay

owing“Knay atthay Iay avehay onay ightray otay eakspay erehay, Iay askay youray eave.”lay

eak“Spay en,”thay iedcray entytway oicesvay.

o“Tay illkay aay akednay ubcay isay ameshay. Esidesbay, ehay aymay akemay etterbay ortspay orfay youay
enwhay ehay isay owngray. Aloobay ashay okenspay inay ishay ehalfbay. Ownay otay Aloo’sbay ordway
Iay illway adday oneay ullbay, anday aay atfay oneay, ewlynay illedkay, otnay alfhay aay ilemay
omfray erehay, ifay yeay illway acceptay ethay an’smay ubcay accordingay otay ethay Awlay. Isay itay
ifficult?”day

Erethay asway aay amorclay ofay oresscay ofay oicesvay, aying:say at“Whay attermay? Ehay illway
ieday inay ethay interway ainsray. Ehay illway orchscay inay ethay unsay. Atwhay armhay ancay
aay akednay ogfray oday usay? Etlay imhay unray ithway ethay Ackpay. Erewhay isay ethay ullbay,
Agheerabay? Etlay imhay ebay accepted.”ay Anday enthay amecay Akela’say eepday aybay, ying:cray
ook“Lay ell--lookway ellway, Oay Olves!”way

Owglimay asway illstay eeplyday interesteday inay ethay ebblespay, anday ehay idday otnay oticenay
enwhay ethay olvesway amecay anday ookedlay atay imhay oneay ybay oneay. Atay astlay eythay allay entway
ownday ethay illhay orfay ethay eadday ullbay, anday onlyay Akelaay, Agheerabay, Aloobay, anday
Owgli’smay ownay olvesway ereway eftlay. Ereshay Ankhay oaredray illstay inay ethay ightnay, orfay
ehay asway eryvay angryay atthay Owglimay adhay otnay eenbay andedhay overay otay imhay.

Ay“ay, oarray ell,”way aidsay Agheerabay, underay ishay iskerswhay, or“fay ethay imetay illway
omecay enwhay isthay akednay ingthay illway akemay eethay oarray otay anotheray unetay, oray Iay
owknay othingnay ofay an.”may

It“ay asway ellway one,”day aidsay Akelaay. en“May anday eirthay ubscay areay eryvay iseway. Ehay
aymay ebay aay elphay inay ime.”tay

uly“Tray, aay elphay inay imetay ofay eed;nay orfay onenay ancay opehay otay eadlay ethay Ackpay
orever,”fay aidsay Agheerabay.

Akelaay aidsay othingnay. Ehay asway inkingthay ofay ethay imetay atthay omescay otay everyay
eaderlay ofay everyay ackpay enwhay ishay engthstray oesgay omfray imhay anday ehay etsgay eeblerfay
anday eeblerfay, illtay atay astlay ehay isay illedkay ybay ethay olvesway anday aay ewnay eaderlay
omescay up--toay ebay illedkay inay ishay urntay.

ake“Tay imhay away,”ay ehay aidsay otay Atherfay Olfway, and“ay aintray imhay asay efitsbay oneay ofay
ethay Eefray Eople.”pay

Anday atthay isay owhay Owglimay asway entereday intoay ethay Eeoneesay Olfway Ackpay orfay ethay
icepray ofay aay ullbay anday onay Aloo’sbay oodgay ordway.

Ownay youay ustmay ebay ontentcay otay ipskay entay oray elevenay olewhay yearsay, anday onlyay
uessgay atay allay ethay onderfulway ifelay atthay Owglimay edlay amongay ethay olvesway,
ecausebay ifay itay ereway ittenwray outay itay ouldway illfay everay osay anymay ooksbay. Ehay
ewgray upay ithway ethay ubscay, oughthay eythay, ofay oursecay, ereway owngray olvesway almostay
eforebay ehay asway aay ildchay. Anday Atherfay Olfway aughttay imhay ishay usinessbay, anday ethay
eaningmay ofay ingsthay inay ethay unglejay, illtay everyay ustleray inay ethay assgray, everyay
eathbray ofay ethay armway ightnay airay, everyay otenay ofay ethay owlsay aboveay ishay eadhay,
everyay atchscray ofay aay at’sbay awsclay asay itay oostedray orfay aay ilewhay inay aay eetray, anday
everyay ashsplay ofay everyay ittlelay ishfay umpingjay inay aay oolpay eantmay ustjay asay uchmay
otay imhay asay ethay orkway ofay ishay officeay eansmay otay aay usinessbay anmay. Enwhay ehay asway
otnay earninglay ehay atsay outay inay ethay unsay anday eptslay, anday ateay anday entway otay eepslay
againay. Enwhay ehay eltfay irtyday oray othay ehay amsway inay ethay orestfay ools;pay anday
enwhay ehay antedway oneyhay aloo(Bay oldtay imhay atthay oneyhay anday utsnay ereway ustjay asay
easantplay otay eatay asay awray eatmay) ehay imbedclay upay orfay itay, anday atthay Agheerabay
owedshay imhay owhay otay oday. Agheerabay ouldway ielay outay onay aay anchbray anday allcay, ome“Cay
alongay, Ittlelay Other,”bray anday atay irstfay Owglimay ouldway ingclay ikelay ethay othslay,
utbay afterwarday ehay ouldway ingflay imselfhay oughthray ethay anchesbray almostay asay
oldlybay asay ethay aygray apeay. Ehay ooktay ishay aceplay atay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, ootay,
enwhay ethay Ackpay etmay, anday erethay ehay iscoveredday atthay ifay ehay aredstay ardhay atay anyay
olfway, ethay olfway ouldway ebay orcedfay otay opdray ishay eyesay, anday osay ehay useday otay arestay
orfay unfay. Atay otheray imestay ehay ouldway ickpay ethay onglay ornsthay outay ofay ethay adspay
ofay ishay iendsfray, orfay olvesway uffersay erriblytay omfray ornsthay anday ursbay inay eirthay
oatscay. Ehay ouldway ogay ownday ethay illsidehay intoay ethay ultivatedcay andslay ybay ightnay,
anday ooklay eryvay uriouslycay atay ethay illagersvay inay eirthay utshay, utbay ehay adhay aay
istrustmay ofay enmay ecausebay Agheerabay owedshay imhay aay uaresqay oxbay ithway aay opdray
ategay osay unninglycay iddenhay inay ethay unglejay atthay ehay earlynay alkedway intoay itay,
anday oldtay imhay atthay itay asway aay aptray. Ehay ovedlay etterbay anthay anythingay elseay otay
ogay ithway Agheerabay intoay ethay arkday armway earthay ofay ethay orestfay, otay eepslay allay
oughthray ethay owsydray ayday, anday atay ightnay eesay owhay Agheerabay idday ishay
illingkay. Agheerabay illedkay ightray anday eftlay asay ehay eltfay ungryhay, anday osay idday
Owgli--withmay oneay exceptionay. Asay oonsay asay ehay asway olday enoughay otay understanday
ingsthay, Agheerabay oldtay imhay atthay ehay ustmay evernay ouchtay attlecay ecausebay ehay adhay
eenbay oughtbay intoay ethay Ackpay atay ethay icepray ofay aay ull’sbay ifelay. All“ay ethay unglejay
isay ine,”thay aidsay Agheerabay, and“ay outhay anstcay illkay everythingay atthay outhay artay
ongstray enoughay otay ill;kay utbay orfay ethay akesay ofay ethay ullbay atthay oughtbay eethay
outhay ustmay evernay illkay oray eatay anyay attlecay youngay oray olday. Atthay isay ethay Awlay ofay
ethay Ungle.”jay Owglimay obeyeday aithfullyfay.

Anday ehay ewgray anday ewgray ongstray asay aay oybay ustmay owgray owhay oesday otnay owknay atthay
ehay isay earninglay anyay essonslay, anday owhay ashay othingnay inay ethay orldway otay inkthay ofay
exceptay ingsthay otay eatay.

Othermay Olfway oldtay imhay onceay oray icetway atthay Ereshay Ankhay asway otnay aay eaturecray
otay ebay ustedtray, anday atthay omesay ayday ehay ustmay illkay Ereshay Ankhay. Utbay oughthay aay
youngay olfway ouldway avehay ememberedray atthay adviceay everyay ourhay, Owglimay orgotfay
itay ecausebay ehay asway onlyay aay oy--thoughbay ehay ouldway avehay alledcay imselfhay aay olfway
ifay ehay adhay eenbay ableay otay eakspay inay anyay umanhay onguetay.

Ereshay Ankhay asway alwaysay ossingcray ishay athpay inay ethay unglejay, orfay asay Akelaay ewgray
olderay anday eeblerfay ethay amelay igertay adhay omecay otay ebay eatgray iendsfray ithway ethay
youngeray olvesway ofay ethay Ackpay, owhay ollowedfay imhay orfay apsscray, aay ingthay Akelaay
ouldway evernay avehay alloweday ifay ehay adhay aredday otay ushpay ishay authorityay otay ethay
operpray oundsbay. Enthay Ereshay Ankhay ouldway atterflay emthay anday onderway atthay uchsay
inefay youngay untershay ereway ontentcay otay ebay edlay ybay aay yingday olfway anday aay an’smay
ubcay. ey“Thay elltay e,”may Ereshay Ankhay ouldway aysay, at“thay atay Ouncilcay yeay areday
otnay ooklay imhay etweenbay ethay eyes.”ay Anday ethay youngay olvesway ouldway owlgray anday
istlebray.

Agheerabay, owhay adhay eyesay anday earsay everywhereay, ewknay omethingsay ofay isthay, anday
onceay oray icetway ehay oldtay Owglimay inay osay anymay ordsway atthay Ereshay Ankhay ouldway illkay
imhay omesay ayday. Owglimay ouldway aughlay anday answer:ay I“ay avehay ethay Ackpay anday Iay avehay
ee;thay anday Aloobay, oughthay ehay isay osay azylay, ightmay ikestray aay owblay oray otway orfay ymay
akesay. Ywhay ouldshay Iay ebay afraid?”ay

Itay asway oneay eryvay armway ayday atthay aay ewnay otionnay amecay otay Agheera--bornbay ofay
omethingsay atthay ehay adhay eardhay. Erhapspay Ikkiay ethay Orcupinepay adhay oldtay im;hay
utbay ehay aidsay otay Owglimay enwhay eythay ereway eepday inay ethay unglejay, asay ethay oybay aylay
ithway ishay eadhay onay Agheera’sbay eautifulbay ackblay inskay, ittle“Lay Otherbray, owhay
oftenay avehay Iay oldtay eethay atthay Ereshay Ankhay isay ythay enemy?”ay

As“ay anymay imestay asay erethay areay utsnay onay atthay alm,”pay aidsay Owglimay, owhay,
aturallynay, ouldcay otnay ountcay. at“Whay ofay itay? Iay amay eepyslay, Agheerabay, anday
Ereshay Ankhay isay allay onglay ailtay anday oudlay alk--liketay Aomay, ethay Eacock.”pay

ut“Bay isthay isay onay imetay orfay eepingslay. Aloobay owsknay it;ay Iay owknay it;ay ethay Ackpay
owknay it;ay anday evenay ethay oolishfay, oolishfay eerday owknay. Abaquitay ashay oldtay eethay
oo.”tay

o“Hay! o!”hay aidsay Owglimay. abaqui“Tay amecay otay emay otnay onglay agoay ithway omesay uderay
alktay atthay Iay asway aay akednay an’smay ubcay anday otnay itfay otay igday ig-nutspay. Utbay Iay
aughtcay Abaquitay ybay ethay ailtay anday ungsway imhay icetway againstay aay alm-treepay otay
eachtay imhay etterbay anners.”may

at“Thay asway oolishnessfay, orfay oughthay Abaquitay isay aay ischief-makermay, ehay ouldway
avehay oldtay eethay ofay omethingsay atthay oncernedcay eethay oselyclay. Openay osethay
eyesay, Ittlelay Otherbray. Ereshay Ankhay areday otnay illkay eethay inay ethay unglejay. Utbay
ememberray, Akelaay isay eryvay olday, anday oonsay ethay ayday omescay enwhay ehay annotcay illkay
ishay uckbay, anday enthay ehay illway ebay eaderlay onay oremay. Anymay ofay ethay olvesway atthay
ookedlay eethay overay enwhay outhay astway oughtbray otay ethay Ouncilcay irstfay areay olday
ootay, anday ethay youngay olvesway elievebay, asay Ereshay Ankhay ashay aughttay emthay, atthay
aay an-cubmay ashay onay aceplay ithway ethay Ackpay. Inay aay ittlelay imetay outhay iltway ebay aay
an.”may

And“ay atwhay isay aay anmay atthay ehay ouldshay otnay unray ithway ishay others?”bray aidsay
Owglimay. I“ay asway ornbay inay ethay unglejay. Iay avehay obeyeday ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay,
anday erethay isay onay olfway ofay oursay omfray osewhay awspay Iay avehay otnay ulledpay aay ornthay.
Urelysay eythay areay ymay others!”bray

Agheerabay etchedstray imselfhay atay ullfay engthlay anday alfhay utshay ishay eyesay.
ittle“Lay Other,”bray aidsay ehay, eel“fay underay ymay aw.”jay

Owglimay utpay upay ishay ongstray ownbray andhay, anday ustjay underay Agheera’sbay ilkysay
inchay, erewhay ethay iantgay ollingray usclesmay ereway allay idhay ybay ethay ossyglay airhay,
ehay amecay uponay aay ittlelay aldbay otspay.

ere“Thay isay onay oneay inay ethay unglejay atthay owsknay atthay Iay, Agheerabay, arrycay atthay
ark--themay arkmay ofay ethay ollar;cay anday yetay, Ittlelay Otherbray, Iay asway ornbay amongay
enmay, anday itay asway amongay enmay atthay ymay othermay ied--inday ethay agescay ofay ethay
ing’skay alacepay atay Oodeyporeay. Itay asway ecausebay ofay isthay atthay Iay aidpay ethay icepray
orfay eethay atay ethay Ouncilcay enwhay outhay astway aay ittlelay akednay ubcay. Yesay, Iay ootay
asway ornbay amongay enmay. Iay adhay evernay eensay ethay unglejay. Eythay edfay emay ehindbay
arsbay omfray anay ironay anpay illtay oneay ightnay Iay eltfay atthay Iay asway Agheera--thebay
Anther--andpay onay an’smay aythingplay, anday Iay okebray ethay illysay ocklay ithway oneay
owblay ofay ymay awpay anday amecay awayay. Anday ecausebay Iay adhay earnedlay ethay aysway ofay enmay,
Iay ecamebay oremay erribletay inay ethay unglejay anthay Ereshay Ankhay. Isay itay otnay o?”say

Yes,”“ay aidsay Owglimay, all“ay ethay unglejay earfay Agheera--allbay exceptay Owgli.”may

Oh“ay, outhay artay aay an’smay ub,”cay aidsay ethay Ackblay Antherpay eryvay enderlytay. And“ay
evenay asay Iay eturnedray otay ymay unglejay, osay outhay ustmay ogay ackbay otay enmay atay ast--tolay
ethay enmay owhay areay ythay others--ifbray outhay artay otnay illedkay inay ethay Ouncil.”cay

ut“Bay y--butwhay ywhay ouldshay anyay ishway otay illkay e?”may aidsay Owglimay.

ook“Lay atay e,”may aidsay Agheerabay. Anday Owglimay ookedlay atay imhay eadilystay etweenbay
ethay eyesay. Ethay igbay antherpay urnedtay ishay eadhay awayay inay alfhay aay inutemay.

at“Thay isay y,”whay ehay aidsay, iftingshay ishay awpay onay ethay eaveslay. ot“Nay evenay Iay ancay
ooklay eethay etweenbay ethay eyesay, anday Iay asway ornbay amongay enmay, anday Iay ovelay eethay,
Ittlelay Otherbray. Ethay othersay eythay atehay eethay ecausebay eirthay eyesay annotcay eetmay
ine;thay ecausebay outhay artay ise;way ecausebay outhay asthay ulledpay outay ornsthay omfray
eirthay eet--becausefay outhay artay aay an.”may

I“ay idday otnay owknay esethay ings,”thay aidsay Owglimay ullenlysay, anday ehay ownedfray
underay ishay eavyhay ackblay eyebrowsay.

at“Whay isay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay? Ikestray irstfay anday enthay ivegay onguetay. Ybay
ythay eryvay arelessnesscay eythay owknay atthay outhay artay aay anmay. Utbay ebay iseway. Itay isay
inay ymay earthay atthay enwhay Akelaay issesmay ishay extnay ill--andkay atay eachay unthay
itay ostscay imhay oremay otay inpay ethay uck--thebay Ackpay illway urntay againstay imhay anday
againstay eethay. Eythay illway oldhay aay unglejay Ouncilcay atay ethay Ockray, anday en--andthay
en--Ithay avehay it!”ay aidsay Agheerabay, eapinglay upay. o“Gay outhay ownday uicklyqay otay
ethay en’smay utshay inay ethay alleyvay, anday aketay omesay ofay ethay Edray Owerflay ichwhay eythay
owgray erethay, osay atthay enwhay ethay imetay omescay outhay ayestmay avehay evenay aay ongerstray
iendfray anthay Iay oray Aloobay oray osethay ofay ethay Ackpay atthay ovelay eethay. Etgay ethay Edray
Ower.”flay

Ybay Edray Owerflay Agheerabay eantmay irefay, onlyay onay eaturecray inay ethay unglejay illway
allcay irefay ybay itsay operpray amenay. Everyay eastbay iveslay inay eadlyday earfay ofay itay,
anday inventsay aay undredhay aysway ofay escribingday itay.

e“Thay Edray Ower?”flay aidsay Owglimay. at“Thay owsgray outsideay eirthay utshay inay ethay
ilighttway. Iay illway etgay ome.”say

ere“Thay eaksspay ethay an’smay ub,”cay aidsay Agheerabay oudlypray. emember“Ray atthay itay
owsgray inay ittlelay otspay. Etgay oneay iftlysway, anday eepkay itay ybay eethay orfay imetay ofay
eed.”nay

ood!”“Gay aidsay Owglimay. I“ay ogay. Utbay artay outhay uresay, Oay ymay Agheera”--hebay
ippedslay ishay armay arounday ethay endidsplay ecknay anday ookedlay eepday intoay ethay igbay
eyes--“artay outhay uresay atthay allay isthay isay Ereshay An’skhay oing?”day

y“Bay ethay Okenbray Ocklay atthay eedfray emay, Iay amay uresay, Ittlelay Other.”bray

en“Thay, ybay ethay Ullbay atthay oughtbay emay, Iay illway aypay Ereshay Ankhay ullfay aletay orfay
isthay, anday itay aymay ebay aay ittlelay over,”ay aidsay Owglimay, anday ehay oundedbay awayay.

at“Thay isay aay anmay. Atthay isay allay aay an,”may aidsay Agheerabay otay imselfhay, yinglay ownday
againay. Oh“ay, Ereshay Ankhay, evernay asway aay ackerblay untinghay anthay atthay og-huntfray
ofay inethay entay yearsay ago!”ay

Owglimay asway arfay anday arfay oughthray ethay orestfay, unningray ardhay, anday ishay earthay
asway othay inay imhay. Ehay amecay otay ethay avecay asay ethay eveningay istmay oseray, anday ewdray
eathbray, anday ookedlay ownday ethay alleyvay. Ethay ubscay ereway outay, utbay Othermay
Olfway, atay ethay ackbay ofay ethay avecay, ewknay ybay ishay eathingbray atthay omethingsay asway
oublingtray erhay ogfray.

at“Whay isay itay, On?”say eshay aidsay.

ome“Say at’sbay atterchay ofay Ereshay An,”khay ehay alledcay ackbay. I“ay unthay amongay ethay
owedplay ieldsfay onight,”tay anday ehay ungedplay ownwardday oughthray ethay ushesbay, otay
ethay eamstray atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay alleyvay. Erethay ehay eckedchay, orfay ehay eardhay
ethay yellay ofay ethay Ackpay untinghay, eardhay ethay ellowbay ofay aay untedhay Ambhursay,
anday ethay ortsnay asay ethay uckbay urnedtay atay aybay. Enthay erethay ereway ickedway, itterbay
owlshay omfray ethay youngay olves:way Akela“ay! Akelaay! Etlay ethay Onelay Olfway owshay ishay
engthstray. Oomray orfay ethay eaderlay ofay ethay Ackpay! Ingspray, Akela!”ay

Ethay Onelay Olfway ustmay avehay ungspray anday issedmay ishay oldhay, orfay Owglimay eardhay ethay
apsnay ofay ishay eethtay anday enthay aay yelpay asay ethay Ambhursay ockedknay imhay overay ithway
ishay orefootfay.

Ehay idday otnay aitway orfay anythingay oremay, utbay ashedday on;ay anday ethay yellsay ewgray
ainterfay ehindbay imhay asay ehay anray intoay ethay oplandscray erewhay ethay illagersvay
ivedlay.

agheera“Bay okespay uth,”tray ehay antedpay, asay ehay estlednay ownday inay omesay attlecay
odderfay ybay ethay indowway ofay aay uthay. o-morrow“Tay isay oneay ayday othbay orfay Akelaay anday
orfay e.”may

Enthay ehay essedpray ishay acefay oseclay otay ethay indowway anday atchedway ethay irefay onay
ethay earthhay. Ehay awsay ethay usbandman’shay ifeway etgay upay anday eedfay itay inay ethay ightnay
ithway ackblay umpslay. Anday enwhay ethay orningmay amecay anday ethay istsmay ereway allay itewhay
anday oldcay, ehay awsay ethay an’smay ildchay ickpay upay aay ickerway otpay asteredplay insideay
ithway earthay, illfay itay ithway umpslay ofay ed-hotray arcoalchay, utpay itay underay ishay
anketblay, anday ogay outay otay endtay ethay owscay inay ethay yrebay.

Is“ay atthay all?”ay aidsay Owglimay. If“ay aay ubcay ancay oday itay, erethay isay othingnay otay
ear.”fay Osay ehay odestray oundray ethay ornercay anday etmay ethay oybay, ooktay ethay otpay omfray
ishay andhay, anday isappearedday intoay ethay istmay ilewhay ethay oybay owledhay ithway earfay.

ey“Thay areay eryvay ikelay e,”may aidsay Owglimay, owingblay intoay ethay otpay asay ehay adhay
eensay ethay omanway oday. is“Thay ingthay illway ieday ifay Iay oday otnay ivegay itay ingsthay otay
eat”;ay anday ehay oppeddray igstway anday ieddray arkbay onay ethay edray uffstay. Alfwayhay upay
ethay illhay ehay etmay Agheerabay ithway ethay orningmay ewday iningshay ikelay oonstonesmay onay
ishay oatcay.

Akela“ay ashay issed,”may aidsay ethay Antherpay. ey“Thay ouldway avehay illedkay imhay astlay
ightnay, utbay eythay eedednay eethay alsoay. Eythay ereway ookinglay orfay eethay onay ethay
ill.”hay

I“ay asway amongay ethay owedplay andslay. Iay amay eadyray. Ee!”say Owglimay eldhay upay ethay
ire-potfay.

ood“Gay! Ownay, Iay avehay eensay enmay ustthray aay ydray anchbray intoay atthay uffstay, anday
esentlypray ethay Edray Owerflay ossomedblay atay ethay enday ofay itay. Artay outhay otnay
afraid?”ay

o“Nay. Ywhay ouldshay Iay earfay? Iay ememberray ow--ifnay itay isay otnay aay eam--howdray,
eforebay Iay asway aay Olfway, Iay aylay esidebay ethay Edray Owerflay, anday itay asway armway anday
easant.”play

Allay atthay ayday Owglimay atsay inay ethay avecay endingtay ishay irefay otpay anday ippingday
ydray anchesbray intoay itay otay eesay owhay eythay ookedlay. Ehay oundfay aay anchbray atthay
atisfiedsay imhay, anday inay ethay eveningay enwhay Abaquitay amecay otay ethay avecay anday oldtay
imhay udelyray enoughay atthay ehay asway antedway atay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, ehay aughedlay
illtay Abaquitay anray awayay. Enthay Owglimay entway otay ethay Ouncilcay, illstay aughinglay.

Akelaay ethay Onelay Olfway aylay ybay ethay idesay ofay ishay ockray asay aay ignsay atthay ethay
eadershiplay ofay ethay Ackpay asway openay, anday Ereshay Ankhay ithway ishay ollowingfay ofay
ap-fedscray olvesway alkedway otay anday ofray openlyay eingbay atteredflay. Agheerabay aylay
oseclay otay Owglimay, anday ethay irefay otpay asway etweenbay Owgli’smay eesknay. Enwhay eythay
ereway allay atheredgay ogethertay, Ereshay Ankhay eganbay otay eak--aspay ingthay ehay ouldway
evernay avehay aredday otay oday enwhay Akelaay asway inay ishay imepray.

e“Hay ashay onay ight,”ray isperedwhay Agheerabay. ay“Say osay. Ehay isay aay og’sday onsay. Ehay
illway ebay ightened.”fray

Owglimay angspray otay ishay eetfay. ee“Fray Eople,”pay ehay iedcray, oes“day Ereshay Ankhay
eadlay ethay Ackpay? Atwhay ashay aay igertay otay oday ithway ouray eadership?”lay

eeing“Say atthay ethay eadershiplay isay yetay openay, anday eingbay askeday otay eak--”spay
Ereshay Ankhay eganbay.

y“Bay om?”whay aidsay Owglimay. Are“ay eway allay ackalsjay, otay awnfay onay isthay attlecay
utcherbay? Ethay eadershiplay ofay ethay Ackpay isay ithway ethay Ackpay alone.”ay

Erethay ereway yellsay ofay ilence“Say, outhay an’smay ub!”cay et“Lay imhay eakspay. Ehay ashay
eptkay ouray Aw”;lay anday atay astlay ethay eniorssay ofay ethay Ackpay undered:thay et“Lay ethay
Eadday Olfway eak.”spay Enwhay aay eaderlay ofay ethay Ackpay ashay issedmay ishay illkay, ehay isay
alledcay ethay Eadday Olfway asay onglay asay ehay iveslay, ichwhay isay otnay onglay.

Akelaay aisedray ishay olday eadhay earily:--way

ee“Fray Eoplepay, anday yeay ootay, ackalsjay ofay Ereshay Ankhay, orfay elvetway easonssay Iay
avehay edlay yeay otay anday omfray ethay illkay, anday inay allay atthay imetay otnay oneay ashay eenbay
appedtray oray aimedmay. Ownay Iay avehay issedmay ymay illkay. Yeay owknay owhay atthay otplay
asway ademay. Yeay owknay owhay yeay oughtbray emay upay otay anay untrieday uckbay otay akemay ymay
eaknessway ownknay. Itay asway everlyclay oneday. Youray ightray isay otay illkay emay erehay onay
ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, ownay. Ereforethay, Iay askay, owhay omescay otay akemay anay enday ofay ethay
Onelay Olfway? Orfay itay isay ymay ightray, ybay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay, atthay yeay omecay
oneay ybay one.”ay

Erethay asway aay onglay ushhay, orfay onay inglesay olfway aredcay otay ightfay Akelaay otay
ethay eathday. Enthay Ereshay Ankhay oared:ray ah“Bay! Atwhay avehay eway otay oday ithway isthay
oothlesstay oolfay? Ehay isay oomedday otay ieday! Itay isay ethay an-cubmay owhay ashay ivedlay ootay
onglay. Eefray Eoplepay, ehay asway ymay eatmay omfray ethay irstfay. Ivegay imhay otay emay. Iay
amay earyway ofay isthay an-wolfmay ollyfay. Ehay ashay oubledtray ethay unglejay orfay entay
easonssay. Ivegay emay ethay an-cubmay, oray Iay illway unthay erehay alwaysay, anday otnay ivegay
youay oneay onebay. Ehay isay aay anmay, aay an’smay ildchay, anday omfray ethay arrowmay ofay ymay
onesbay Iay atehay im!”hay

Enthay oremay anthay alfhay ethay Ackpay yelled:ay A“ay anmay! Aay anmay! Atwhay ashay aay anmay otay oday
ithway usay? Etlay imhay ogay otay ishay ownay ace.”play

And“ay urntay allay ethay eoplepay ofay ethay illagesvay againstay us?”ay amoredclay Ereshay
Ankhay. o“Nay, ivegay imhay otay emay. Ehay isay aay anmay, anday onenay ofay usay ancay ooklay imhay
etweenbay ethay eyes.”ay

Akelaay iftedlay ishay eadhay againay anday aidsay, e“Hay ashay eatenay ouray oodfay. Ehay ashay
eptslay ithway usay. Ehay ashay ivendray amegay orfay usay. Ehay ashay okenbray onay ordway ofay ethay
Awlay ofay ethay Ungle.”jay

Also“ay, Iay aidpay orfay imhay ithway aay ullbay enwhay ehay asway accepteday. Ethay orthway ofay aay
ullbay isay ittlelay, utbay Agheera’sbay onorhay isay omethingsay atthay ehay illway erhapspay
ightfay or,”fay aidsay Agheerabay inay ishay entlestgay oicevay.

A“ay ullbay aidpay entay yearsay ago!”ay ethay Ackpay arledsnay. at“Whay oday eway arecay orfay
onesbay entay yearsay old?”ay

Or“ay orfay aay edge?”play aidsay Agheerabay, ishay itewhay eethtay aredbay underay ishay iplay.
ell“Way areay yeay alledcay ethay Eefray Eople!”pay

o“Nay an’smay ubcay ancay unray ithway ethay eoplepay ofay ethay ungle,”jay owledhay Ereshay Ankhay.
ive“Gay imhay otay e!”may

e“Hay isay ouray otherbray inay allay utbay ood,”blay Akelaay entway onay, and“ay yeay ouldway illkay
imhay erehay! Inay uthtray, Iay avehay ivedlay ootay onglay. Omesay ofay yeay areay eatersay ofay
attlecay, anday ofay othersay Iay avehay eardhay atthay, underay Ereshay An’skhay eachingtay,
yeay ogay ybay arkday ightnay anday atchsnay ildrenchay omfray ethay illager’svay oorstepday.
Ereforethay Iay owknay yeay otay ebay owardscay, anday itay isay otay owardscay Iay eakspay. Itay isay
ertaincay atthay Iay ustmay ieday, anday ymay ifelay isay ofay onay orthway, oray Iay ouldway offeray
atthay inay ethay an-cub’smay aceplay. Utbay orfay ethay akesay ofay ethay Onorhay ofay
ethay Ack,--apay ittlelay attermay atthay ybay eingbay ithoutway aay eaderlay yeay avehay
orgotten,--Ifay omisepray atthay ifay yeay etlay ethay an-cubmay ogay otay ishay ownay aceplay, Iay
illway otnay, enwhay ymay imetay omescay otay ieday, arebay oneay oothtay againstay yeay. Iay illway
ieday ithoutway ightingfay. Atthay illway atay eastlay avesay ethay Ackpay eethray iveslay.
Oremay Iay annotcay o;day utbay ifay yeay illway, Iay ancay avesay yeay ethay ameshay atthay omescay ofay
illingkay aay otherbray againstay omwhay erethay isay onay ault--afay otherbray okenspay orfay
anday oughtbay intoay ethay Ackpay accordingay otay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Ungle.”jay

e“Hay isay aay an--amay an--amay an!”may arledsnay ethay Ackpay. Anday ostmay ofay ethay olvesway
eganbay otay athergay oundray Ereshay Ankhay, osewhay ailtay asway eginningbay otay itchsway.

ow“Nay ethay usinessbay isay inay ythay ands,”hay aidsay Agheerabay otay Owglimay. e“Way ancay oday
onay oremay exceptay ight.”fay

Owglimay oodstay upright--theay irefay otpay inay ishay andshay. Enthay ehay etchedstray outay
ishay armsay, anday yawneday inay ethay acefay ofay ethay Ouncil;cay utbay ehay asway uriousfay ithway
ageray anday orrowsay, orfay, olflikeway, ethay olvesway adhay evernay oldtay imhay owhay eythay
atedhay imhay. isten“Lay you!”ay ehay iedcray. ere“Thay isay onay eednay orfay isthay og’sday
abberjay. Yeay avehay oldtay emay osay oftenay onighttay atthay Iay amay aay anmay and(ay indeeday Iay
ouldway avehay eenbay aay olfway ithway youay otay ymay ife’slay enday) atthay Iay eelfay youray ordsway
areay uetray. Osay Iay oday otnay allcay yeay ymay othersbray anyay oremay, utbay agsay ogs][day, asay
aay anmay ouldshay. Atwhay yeay illway oday, anday atwhay yeay illway otnay oday, isay otnay yoursay
otay aysay. Atthay attermay isay ithway e;may anday atthay eway aymay eesay ethay attermay oremay
ainlyplay, Iay, ethay anmay, avehay oughtbray erehay aay ittlelay ofay ethay Edray Owerflay ichwhay
yeay, ogsday, ear.”fay

Ehay ungflay ethay irefay otpay onay ethay oundgray, anday omesay ofay ethay edray oalscay itlay
aay ufttay ofay ieddray ossmay atthay aredflay upay, asay allay ethay Ouncilcay ewdray ackbay inay
errortay eforebay ethay eapinglay amesflay.

Owglimay ustthray ishay eadday anchbray intoay ethay irefay illtay ethay igstway itlay anday
ackledcray, anday irledwhay itay aboveay ishay eadhay amongay ethay oweringcay olvesway.

ou“Thay artay ethay aster,”may aidsay Agheerabay inay anay undertoneay. ave“Say Akelaay omfray
ethay eathday. Ehay asway everay ythay iend.”fray

Akelaay, ethay imgray olday olfway owhay adhay evernay askeday orfay ercymay inay ishay ifelay, avegay
oneay iteouspay ooklay atay Owglimay asay ethay oybay oodstay allay akednay, ishay onglay ackblay
airhay ossingtay overay ishay ouldersshay inay ethay ightlay ofay ethay azingblay anchbray atthay
ademay ethay adowsshay umpjay anday uiverqay.

ood!”“Gay aidsay Owglimay, aringstay oundray owlyslay. I“ay eesay atthay yeay areay ogsday. Iay ogay
omfray youay otay ymay ownay eople--ifpay eythay ebay ymay ownay eoplepay. Ethay unglejay isay utshay
otay emay, anday Iay ustmay orgetfay youray alktay anday youray ompanionshipcay. Utbay Iay illway ebay
oremay ercifulmay anthay yeay areay. Ecausebay Iay asway allay utbay youray otherbray inay oodblay,
Iay omisepray atthay enwhay Iay amay aay anmay amongay enmay Iay illway otnay etraybay yeay otay enmay asay
yeay avehay etrayedbay e.”may Ehay ickedkay ethay irefay ithway ishay ootfay, anday ethay arksspay
ewflay upay. ere“Thay allshay ebay onay arway etweenbay anyay ofay usay inay ethay Ackpay. Utbay erehay
isay aay ebtday otay aypay eforebay Iay o.”gay Ehay odestray orwardfay otay erewhay Ereshay Ankhay atsay
inkingblay upidlystay atay ethay amesflay, anday aughtcay imhay ybay ethay ufttay onay ishay inchay.
Agheerabay ollowedfay inay asecay ofay accidentsay. Up“ay, og!”day Owglimay iedcray. Up“ay,
enwhay aay anmay eaksspay, oray Iay illway etsay atthay oatcay ablaze!”ay

Ereshay An’skhay earsay aylay atflay ackbay onay ishay eadhay, anday ehay utshay ishay eyesay, orfay
ethay azingblay anchbray asway eryvay earnay.

is“Thay attle-killercay aidsay ehay ouldway illkay emay inay ethay Ouncilcay ecausebay ehay adhay
otnay illedkay emay enwhay Iay asway aay ubcay. Usthay anday usthay, enthay, oday eway eatbay ogsday
enwhay eway areay enmay. Irstay aay iskerwhay, Ungrilay, anday Iay amray ethay Edray Owerflay ownday
ythay ullet!”gay Ehay eatbay Ereshay Ankhay overay ethay eadhay ithway ethay anchbray, anday ethay
igertay imperedwhay anday inedwhay inay anay agonyay ofay earfay.

ah“Pay! Ingedsay unglejay at--gocay ownay! Utbay ememberray enwhay extnay Iay omecay otay ethay
Ouncilcay Ockray, asay aay anmay ouldshay omecay, itay illway ebay ithway Ereshay An’skhay idehay
onay ymay eadhay. Orfay ethay estray, Akelaay oesgay eefray otay ivelay asay ehay easesplay. Yeay illway
otnay illkay imhay, ecausebay atthay isay otnay ymay illway. Ornay oday Iay inkthay atthay yeay
illway itsay erehay anyay ongerlay, ollinglay outay youray onguestay asay oughthay yeay ereway
omebodiessay, insteaday ofay ogsday omwhay Iay ivedray out--thusay! O!”gay Ethay irefay asway
urningbay uriouslyfay atay ethay enday ofay ethay anchbray, anday Owglimay uckstray ightray
anday eftlay oundray ethay irclecay, anday ethay olvesway anray owlinghay ithway ethay arksspay
urningbay eirthay urfay. Atay astlay erethay ereway onlyay Akelaay, Agheerabay, anday erhapspay
entay olvesway atthay adhay akentay Owgli’smay artpay. Enthay omethingsay eganbay otay urthay
Owglimay insideay imhay, asay ehay adhay evernay eenbay urthay inay ishay ifelay eforebay, anday ehay
aughtcay ishay eathbray anday obbedsay, anday ethay earstay anray ownday ishay acefay.

at“Whay isay itay? Atwhay isay it?”ay ehay aidsay. I“ay oday otnay ishway otay eavelay ethay unglejay,
anday Iay oday otnay owknay atwhay isthay isay. Amay Iay yingday, Agheera?”bay

o“Nay, Ittlelay Otherbray. Atthay isay onlyay earstay uchsay asay enmay use,”ay aidsay Agheerabay.
ow“Nay Iay owknay outhay artay aay anmay, anday aay an’smay ubcay onay ongerlay. Ethay unglejay isay
utshay indeeday otay eethay enceforwardhay. Etlay emthay allfay, Owglimay. Eythay areay onlyay
ears.”tay Osay Owglimay atsay anday iedcray asay oughthay ishay earthay ouldway eak;bray anday ehay
adhay evernay iedcray inay allay ishay ifelay eforebay.

ow,”“Nay ehay aidsay, I“ay illway ogay otay enmay. Utbay irstfay Iay ustmay aysay arewellfay otay ymay
other.”may Anday ehay entway otay ethay avecay erewhay eshay ivedlay ithway Atherfay Olfway, anday
ehay iedcray onay erhay oatcay, ilewhay ethay ourfay ubscay owledhay iserablymay.

Ye“ay illway otnay orgetfay e?”may aidsay Owglimay.

ever“Nay ilewhay eway ancay ollowfay aay ail,”tray aidsay ethay ubscay. ome“Cay otay ethay ootfay ofay
ethay illhay enwhay outhay artay aay anmay, anday eway illway alktay otay ee;thay anday eway illway omecay
intoay ethay oplandscray otay ayplay ithway eethay ybay ight.”nay

ome“Cay oon!”say aidsay Atherfay Olfway. Oh“ay, iseway ittlelay ogfray, omecay againay oon;say
orfay eway ebay olday, ythay othermay anday I.”ay

ome“Cay oon,”say aidsay Othermay Olfway, ittle“lay akednay onsay ofay inemay. Orfay, istenlay,
ildchay ofay anmay, Iay ovedlay eethay oremay anthay everay Iay ovedlay ymay ubs.”cay

I“ay illway urelysay ome,”cay aidsay Owglimay. And“ay enwhay Iay omecay itay illway ebay otay aylay
outay Ereshay An’skhay idehay uponay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray. Oday otnay orgetfay emay! Elltay emthay
inay ethay unglejay evernay otay orgetfay e!”may

Ethay awnday asway eginningbay otay eakbray enwhay Owglimay entway ownday ethay illsidehay
aloneay, otay eetmay osethay ysteriousmay ingsthay atthay areay alledcay enmay.




Unting-Songhay ofay ethay Eeoneesay Ackpay

Asay ethay awnday asway eakingbray ethay Ambhursay elledbay
Onceay, icetway anday againay!
Anday aay oeday eapedlay upay, anday aay oeday eapedlay upay
Omfray ethay ondpay inay ethay oodway erewhay ethay ildway eerday upsay.
Isthay Iay, outingscay aloneay, eheldbay,
Onceay, icetway anday againay!

Asay ethay awnday asway eakingbray ethay Ambhursay elledbay
Onceay, icetway anday againay!
Anday aay olfway olestay ackbay, anday aay olfway olestay ackbay
Otay arrycay ethay ordway otay ethay aitingway ackpay,
Anday eway oughtsay anday eway oundfay anday eway ayedbay onay ishay acktray
Onceay, icetway anday againay!

Asay ethay awnday asway eakingbray ethay Olfway Ackpay yelleday
Onceay, icetway anday againay!
Eetfay inay ethay unglejay atthay eavelay onay arkmay!

Eyesay atthay ancay eesay inay ethay ark--theday arkday!
Ongue--givetay onguetay otay itay! Arkhay! Oay arkhay!
Onceay, icetway anday againay!




Aa’skay Untinghay


Ishay otsspay areay ethay oyjay ofay ethay Eopard:lay ishay ornshay areay ethay Uffalo’sbay idepray.
Ebay eanclay, orfay ethay engthstray ofay ethay unterhay isay ownknay ybay ethay ossglay ofay ishay idehay.
Ifay yeay indfay atthay ethay Ullockbay ancay osstay youay, oray ethay eavy-browedhay Ambhursay ancay ore;gay
Yeay eednay otnay opstay orkway otay informay us:ay eway ewknay itay entay easonssay eforebay.

Oppressay otnay ethay ubscay ofay ethay angerstray, utbay ailhay emthay asay Istersay anday Otherbray,
Orfay oughthay eythay areay ittlelay anday ubsyfay, itay aymay ebay ethay Earbay isay eirthay othermay.
ere“Thay isay onenay ikelay otay e!”may ayssay ethay Ubcay inay ethay idepray ofay ishay earliestay ill;kay
Utbay ethay unglejay isay argelay anday ethay Ubcay ehay isay allsmay. Etlay imhay inkthay anday ebay illstay.
axims_May ofay Aloo_bay

Allay atthay isay oldtay erehay appenedhay omesay imetay eforebay Owglimay asway urnedtay outay ofay
ethay Eeoneesay Olfway Ackpay, oray evengedray imselfhay onay Ereshay Ankhay ethay igertay. Itay
asway inay ethay aysday enwhay Aloobay asway eachingtay imhay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay. Ethay
igbay, erioussay, olday ownbray earbay asway elightedday otay avehay osay uickqay aay upilpay,
orfay ethay youngay olvesway illway onlyay earnlay asay uchmay ofay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay
asay appliesay otay eirthay ownay ackpay anday ibetray, anday unray awayay asay oonsay asay eythay ancay
epeatray ethay Untinghay Erse--“Feetvay atthay akemay onay oise;nay eyesay atthay ancay eesay inay
ethay ark;day earsay atthay ancay earhay ethay indsway inay eirthay airslay, anday arpshay itewhay
eethtay, allay esethay ingsthay areay ethay arksmay ofay ouray othersbray exceptay Abaquitay ethay
Ackaljay anday ethay Yaenahay omwhay eway ate.”hay Utbay Owglimay, asay aay an-cubmay, adhay otay
earnlay aay eatgray ealday oremay anthay isthay. Ometimessay Agheerabay ethay Ackblay Antherpay
ouldway omecay ounginglay oughthray ethay unglejay otay eesay owhay ishay etpay asway ettinggay
onay, anday ouldway urrpay ithway ishay eadhay againstay aay eetray ilewhay Owglimay ecitedray ethay
ay’sday essonlay otay Aloobay. Ethay oybay ouldcay imbclay almostay asay ellway asay ehay ouldcay
imsway, anday imsway almostay asay ellway asay ehay ouldcay unray. Osay Aloobay, ethay Eachertay ofay
ethay Awlay, aughttay imhay ethay Oodway anday Aterway Aws:lay owhay otay elltay aay ottenray anchbray
omfray aay oundsay one;ay owhay otay eakspay olitelypay otay ethay ildway eesbay enwhay ehay amecay
uponay aay ivehay ofay emthay iftyfay eetfay aboveay ound;gray atwhay otay aysay otay Angmay ethay
Atbay enwhay ehay isturbedday imhay inay ethay anchesbray atay idday;may anday owhay otay arnway ethay
ater-snakesway inay ethay oolspay eforebay ehay ashedsplay ownday amongay emthay. Onenay ofay
ethay Unglejay Eoplepay ikelay eingbay isturbedday, anday allay areay eryvay eadyray otay yflay atay
anay intruderay. Enthay, ootay, Owglimay asway aughttay ethay Angers’stray Untinghay Allcay,
ichwhay ustmay ebay epeatedray alouday illtay itay isay answereday, eneverwhay oneay ofay ethay
Ungle-Peoplejay untshay outsideay ishay ownay oundsgray. Itay eansmay, anslatedtray, ive“Gay
emay eavelay otay unthay erehay ecausebay Iay amay ungry.”hay Anday ethay answeray isay, unt“Hay
enthay orfay oodfay, utbay otnay orfay easure.”play

Allay isthay illway owshay youay owhay uchmay Owglimay adhay otay earnlay ybay earthay, anday ehay
ewgray eryvay iredtay ofay ayingsay ethay amesay ingthay overay aay undredhay imestay. Utbay, asay
Aloobay aidsay otay Agheerabay, oneay ayday enwhay Owglimay adhay eenbay uffedcay anday unray offay
inay aay empertay, A“ay an’smay ubcay isay aay an’smay ubcay, anday ehay ustmay earnlay allay ethay Awlay
ofay ethay Ungle.”jay

ut“Bay inkthay owhay allsmay ehay is,”ay aidsay ethay Ackblay Antherpay, owhay ouldway avehay

allay ythay onglay alk?”tay

aay ittlelay eating?”bay

ell“Way, ooklay otay itay enthay atthay outhay ostday otnay illkay ethay an-cubmay. Ehay isay onay

ow“Nay orfay ethay Ake-People,”snay aidsay Agheerabay.

Ethay answeray asway aay erfectlypay indescribableay isshay, anday Owglimay ickedkay upay ishay

ere--there“Thay! Atthay asway orthway aay ittlelay uise,”bray aidsay ethay ownbray earbay

isten“Lay, an-cub,”may aidsay ethay Earbay, anday ishay oicevay umbledray ikelay underthay onay
aay othay ightnay. I“ay avehay aughttay eethay allay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay orfay allay ethay
eoplespay ofay ethay ungle--exceptjay ethay Onkey-Folkmay owhay ivelay inay ethay eestray.
Eythay avehay onay awlay. Eythay areay outcastsay. Eythay avehay onay eechspay ofay eirthay ownay,
utbay useay ethay olenstay ordsway ichwhay eythay overhearay enwhay eythay istenlay, anday eeppay,
anday aitway upay aboveay inay ethay anchesbray. Eirthay ayway isay otnay ouray ayway. Eythay areay
ithoutway eaderslay. Eythay avehay onay emembranceray. Eythay oastbay anday atterchay anday
etendpray atthay eythay areay aay eatgray eoplepay aboutay otay oday eatgray affairsay inay ethay
unglejay, utbay ethay allingfay ofay aay utnay urnstay eirthay indsmay otay aughterlay anday allay
isay orgottenfay. Eway ofay ethay unglejay avehay onay ealingsday ithway emthay. Eway oday otnay
inkdray erewhay ethay onkeysmay ink;dray eway oday otnay ogay erewhay ethay onkeysmay o;gay eway oday
otnay unthay erewhay eythay unt;hay eway oday otnay ieday erewhay eythay ieday. Asthay outhay everay
eardhay emay eakspay ofay ethay Andar-logbay illtay oday?”tay

o,”“Nay aidsay Owglimay inay aay isperwhay, orfay ethay orestfay asway eryvay illstay ownay Aloobay
adhay inishedfay.

e“Thay Ungle-Peoplejay utpay emthay outay ofay eirthay outhsmay anday outay ofay eirthay indsmay.
Eythay areay eryvay anymay, evilay, irtyday, amelessshay, anday eythay esireday, ifay eythay
avehay anyay ixedfay esireday, otay ebay oticednay ybay ethay Unglejay Eoplepay. Utbay eway oday otnay
oticenay emthay evenay enwhay eythay owthray utsnay anday ilthfay onay ouray eads.”hay

Ehay adhay ardlyhay okenspay enwhay aay owershay ofay utsnay anday igstway atteredspay ownday
oughthray ethay anches;bray anday eythay ouldcay earhay oughingscay anday owlingshay anday
angryay umpingsjay ighhay upay inay ethay airay amongay ethay inthay anchesbray.

orbidden,”“Fay aidsay Agheerabay, ut“bay Iay illstay inkthay Aloobay ouldshay avehay arnedway
eethay againstay em.”thay

I--I“ay? Owhay asway Iay otay uessgay ehay ouldway ayplay ithway uchsay irtday. Ethay Onkeymay
Eoplepay! Augh!”fay

Aay eshfray owershay amecay ownday onay eirthay eadshay anday ethay otway ottedtray awayay, akingtay
Owglimay ithway emthay. Atwhay Aloobay adhay aidsay aboutay ethay onkeysmay asway erfectlypay
uetray. Eythay elongedbay otay ethay ee-topstray, anday asay eastsbay eryvay eldomsay ooklay
upay, erethay asway onay occasionay orfay ethay onkeysmay anday ethay Ungle-Peoplejay otay osscray
eachay other’say athpay. Utbay eneverwhay eythay oundfay aay icksay olfway, oray aay oundedway
igertay, oray earbay, ethay onkeysmay ouldway ormenttay imhay, anday ouldway owthray icksstay
anday utsnay atay anyay eastbay orfay unfay anday inay ethay opehay ofay eingbay oticednay. Enthay
eythay ouldway owlhay anday iekshray enselesssay ongssay, anday inviteay ethay Ungle-Peoplejay
otay imbclay upay eirthay eestray anday ightfay emthay, oray ouldway artstay uriousfay attlesbay
overay othingnay amongay emselvesthay, anday eavelay ethay eadday onkeysmay erewhay ethay
Ungle-Peoplejay ouldcay eesay emthay. Eythay ereway alwaysay ustjay oinggay otay avehay aay
eaderlay, anday awslay anday ustomscay ofay eirthay ownay, utbay eythay evernay idday, ecausebay
eirthay emoriesmay ouldway otnay oldhay overay omfray ayday otay ayday, anday osay eythay
ompromisedcay ingsthay ybay akingmay upay aay ayingsay, at“Whay ethay Andar-logbay inkthay ownay
ethay unglejay illway inkthay ater,”lay anday atthay omfortedcay emthay aay eatgray ealday. Onenay
ofay ethay eastsbay ouldcay eachray emthay, utbay onay ethay otheray andhay onenay ofay ethay eastsbay
ouldway oticenay emthay, anday atthay asway ywhay eythay ereway osay easedplay enwhay Owglimay
amecay otay ayplay ithway emthay, anday eythay eardhay owhay angryay Aloobay asway.

Eythay evernay eantmay otay oday anyay ore--themay Andar-logbay evernay eanmay anythingay atay
all;ay utbay oneay ofay emthay inventeday atwhay eemedsay otay imhay aay illiantbray ideaay, anday
ehay oldtay allay ethay othersay atthay Owglimay ouldway ebay aay usefulay ersonpay otay eepkay inay
ethay ibetray, ecausebay ehay ouldcay eaveway icksstay ogethertay orfay otectionpray omfray
ethay ind;way osay, ifay eythay aughtcay imhay, eythay ouldcay akemay imhay eachtay emthay.
Ofay oursecay Owglimay, asay aay oodcutter’sway ildchay, inheriteday allay ortssay ofay
instinctsay, anday useday otay akemay ittlelay utshay ofay allenfay anchesbray ithoutway
inkingthay owhay ehay amecay otay oday itay. Ethay Onkey-Peoplemay, atchingway inay ethay eestray,
onsideredcay ishay ayplay ostmay onderfulway. Isthay imetay, eythay aidsay, eythay ereway
eallyray oinggay otay avehay aay eaderlay anday ecomebay ethay isestway eoplepay inay ethay
ungle--sojay iseway atthay everyoneay elseay ouldway oticenay anday envyay emthay. Ereforethay
eythay ollowedfay Aloobay anday Agheerabay anday Owglimay oughthray ethay unglejay eryvay
uietlyqay illtay itay asway imetay orfay ethay iddaymay apnay, anday Owglimay, owhay asway
eryvay uchmay ashameday ofay imselfhay, eptslay etweenbay ethay Antherpay anday ethay Earbay,
esolvingray otay avehay onay oremay otay oday ithway ethay Onkeymay Eoplepay.

Ethay extnay ingthay ehay ememberedray asway eelingfay andshay onay ishay egslay anday
arms--harday, ongstray, ittlelay ands--andhay enthay aay ashsway ofay anchesbray inay ishay
acefay, anday enthay ehay asway aringstay ownday oughthray ethay ayingsway oughsbay asay Aloobay
okeway ethay unglejay ithway ishay eepday iescray anday Agheerabay oundedbay upay ethay unktray
ithway everyay oothtay aredbay. Ethay Andar-logbay owledhay ithway iumphtray anday uffledscay
awayay otay ethay upperay anchesbray erewhay Agheerabay aredday otnay ollowfay, outing:shay
e“Hay ashay oticednay usay! Agheerabay ashay oticednay usay. Allay ethay Ungle-Peoplejay
admireay usay orfay ouray illskay anday ouray unning.”cay Enthay eythay eganbay eirthay ight;flay
anday ethay ightflay ofay ethay Onkey-Peoplemay oughthray ee-landtray isay oneay ofay
ethay ingsthay obodynay ancay escribeday. Eythay avehay eirthay egularray oadsray anday
ossroadscray, upay illshay anday ownday illshay, allay aidlay outay omfray iftyfay otay eventysay
oray aay undredhay eetfay aboveay oundgray, anday ybay esethay eythay ancay aveltray evenay atay
ightnay ifay ecessarynay. Otway ofay ethay ongeststray onkeysmay aughtcay Owglimay underay
ethay armsay anday ungsway offay ithway imhay oughthray ethay eetopstray, entytway eetfay atay aay
oundbay. Adhay eythay eenbay aloneay eythay ouldcay avehay onegay icetway asay astfay, utbay ethay
oy’sbay eightway eldhay emthay ackbay. Icksay anday iddygay asay Owglimay asway ehay ouldcay otnay
elphay enjoyingay ethay ildway ushray, oughthay ethay impsesglay ofay earthay arfay ownday elowbay
ightenedfray imhay, anday ethay erribletay eckchay anday erkjay atay ethay enday ofay ethay ingsway
overay othingnay utbay emptyay airay oughtbray ishay earthay etweenbay ishay eethtay. Ishay
escortay ouldway ushray imhay upay aay eetray illtay ehay eltfay ethay innestthay opmosttay
anchesbray acklecray anday endbay underay emthay, anday enthay ithway aay oughcay anday aay oopwhay
ouldway ingflay emselvesthay intoay ethay airay outwarday anday ownwardday, anday ingbray
upay, anginghay ybay eirthay andshay oray eirthay eetfay otay ethay owerlay imbslay ofay ethay extnay
eetray. Ometimessay ehay ouldcay eesay orfay ilesmay anday ilesmay acrossay ethay illstay eengray
unglejay, asay aay anmay onay ethay optay ofay aay astmay ancay eesay orfay ilesmay acrossay ethay easay,
anday enthay ethay anchesbray anday eaveslay ouldway ashlay imhay acrossay ethay acefay, anday ehay
anday ishay otway uardsgay ouldway ebay almostay ownday otay earthay againay. Osay, oundingbay anday
ashingcray anday oopingwhay anday yellingay, ethay olewhay ibetray ofay Andar-logbay eptsway
alongay ethay ee-roadstray ithway Owglimay eirthay isonerpray.

Orfay aay imetay ehay asway afraiday ofay eingbay oppeddray. Enthay ehay ewgray angryay utbay ewknay
etterbay anthay otay ugglestray, anday enthay ehay eganbay otay inkthay. Ethay irstfay ingthay asway
otay endsay ackbay ordway otay Aloobay anday Agheerabay, orfay, atay ethay acepay ethay onkeysmay
ereway oinggay, ehay ewknay ishay iendsfray ouldway ebay eftlay arfay ehindbay. Itay asway uselessay
otay ooklay ownday, orfay ehay ouldcay onlyay eesay ethay opsidestay ofay ethay anchesbray, osay ehay
aredstay upwarday anday awsay, arfay awayay inay ethay ueblay, Annray ethay Itekay alancingbay
anday eelingwhay asay ehay eptkay atchway overay ethay unglejay aitingway orfay ingsthay otay ieday.
Annray awsay atthay ethay onkeysmay ereway arryingcay omethingsay, anday oppeddray aay
ewfay undredhay yardsay otay indfay outay etherwhay eirthay oadlay asway oodgay otay eatay. Ehay
istledwhay ithway urprisesay enwhay ehay awsay Owglimay eingbay aggeddray upay otay aay eetoptray
anday eardhay imhay ivegay ethay Itekay allcay or--“Wefay ebay ofay oneay oodblay, outhay anday I.”ay
Ethay avesway ofay ethay anchesbray osedclay overay ethay oybay, utbay Annray alancedbay awayay otay
ethay extnay eetray inay imetay otay eesay ethay ittlelay ownbray acefay omecay upay againay. ark“May
ymay ail!”tray Owglimay outedshay. ell“Tay Aloobay ofay ethay Eeoneesay Ackpay anday Agheerabay
ofay ethay Ouncilcay Ock.”ray

In“ay osewhay amenay, Other?”bray Annray adhay evernay eensay Owglimay eforebay, oughthay ofay
oursecay ehay adhay eardhay ofay imhay.

owgli“May, ethay Ogfray. An-cubmay eythay allcay emay! Arkmay ymay ail!”tray

Ethay astlay ordsway ereway iekedshray asay ehay asway eingbay ungsway oughthray ethay airay, utbay
Annray oddednay anday oseray upay illtay ehay ookedlay onay iggerbay anthay aay eckspay ofay ustday,
anday erethay ehay unghay, atchingway ithway ishay elescopetay eyesay ethay ayingsway ofay ethay
eetopstray asay Owgli’smay escortay irledwhay alongay.

ey“Thay evernay ogay ar,”fay ehay aidsay ithway aay ucklechay. ey“Thay evernay oday atwhay eythay
etsay outay otay oday. Alwaysay eckingpay atay ewnay ingsthay areay ethay Andar-logbay. Isthay
imetay, ifay Iay avehay anyay eye-sightay, eythay avehay eckedpay ownday oubletray orfay
emselvesthay, orfay Aloobay isay onay edglingflay anday Agheerabay ancay, asay Iay owknay, illkay
oremay anthay oats.”gay

Osay ehay ockedray onay ishay ingsway, ishay eetfay atheredgay upay underay imhay, anday aitedway.

Eantimemay, Aloobay anday Agheerabay ereway uriousfay ithway ageray anday iefgray. Agheerabay
imbedclay asay ehay adhay evernay imbedclay eforebay, utbay ethay inthay anchesbray okebray
eneathbay ishay eightway, anday ehay ippedslay ownday, ishay awsclay ullfay ofay arkbay.

y“Whay idstday outhay otnay arnway ethay an-cub?”may ehay oaredray otay oorpay Aloobay, owhay adhay
etsay offay atay aay umsyclay ottray inay ethay opehay ofay overtakingay ethay onkeysmay. at“Whay
asway ethay useay ofay alfhay ayingslay imhay ithway owsblay ifay outhay idstday otnay arnway im?”hay

aste“Hay! Oay astehay! E--weway aymay atchcay emthay yet!”ay Aloobay antedpay.

At“ay atthay eedspay! Itay ouldway otnay iretay aay oundedway owcay. Eachertay ofay ethay
Aw--cub-beater--alay ilemay ofay atthay ollingray otay anday ofray ouldway urstbay eethay
openay. Itsay illstay anday inkthay! Akemay aay anplay. Isthay isay onay imetay orfay asingchay.
Eythay aymay opdray imhay ifay eway ollowfay ootay ose.”clay

Arrula“ay! Oowhay! Eythay aymay avehay oppeddray imhay alreadyay, eingbay iredtay ofay
arryingcay imhay. Owhay ancay usttray ethay Andar-logbay? Utpay eadday atsbay onay ymay eadhay!
Ivegay emay ackblay onesbay otay eatay! Ollray emay intoay ethay iveshay ofay ethay ildway eesbay
atthay Iay aymay ebay ungstay otay eathday, anday urybay emay ithway ethay Yaenahay, orfay Iay amay ostmay
iserablemay ofay earsbay! Arulalaay! Ahooaway! Oay Owglimay, Owglimay! Ywhay idday Iay otnay
arnway eethay againstay ethay Onkey-Folkmay insteaday ofay eakingbray ythay eadhay? Ownay
erhapspay Iay aymay avehay ockedknay ethay ay’sday essonlay outay ofay ishay indmay, anday ehay illway
ebay aloneay inay ethay unglejay ithoutway ethay Astermay Ords.”way

Aloobay aspedclay ishay awspay overay ishay earsay anday olledray otay anday ofray oaningmay.

At“ay eastlay ehay avegay emay allay ethay Ordsway orrectlycay aay ittlelay imetay ago,”ay aidsay
Agheerabay impatientlyay. aloo“Bay, outhay asthay eithernay emorymay ornay espectray. Atwhay
ouldway ethay unglejay inkthay ifay Iay, ethay Ackblay Antherpay, urledcay yselfmay upay ikelay
Ikkiay ethay Orcupinepay, anday owled?”hay

at“Whay oday Iay arecay atwhay ethay unglejay inksthay? Ehay aymay ebay eadday ybay ow.”nay

Unless“ay anday untilay eythay opdray imhay omfray ethay anchesbray inay ortspay, oray illkay imhay

aughttay, anday aboveay allay ehay ashay ethay eyesay atthay akemay ethay Ungle-Peoplejay
afraiday. Utbay and(ay itay isay aay eatgray evilay) ehay isay inay ethay owerpay ofay ethay
Andar-logbay, anday eythay, ecausebay eythay ivelay inay eestray, avehay onay earfay ofay anyay ofay
ouray eople.”pay Agheerabay ickedlay oneay orepawfay oughtfullythay.

ool“Fay atthay Iay amay! Ohay, atfay, ownbray, oot-diggingray oolfay atthay Iay am,”ay aidsay
Aloobay, uncoilingay imselfhay ithway aay erkjay, it“ay isay uetray atwhay Athihay ethay Ildway
Elephantay ays:say o`Tay eachay ishay ownay ear’;fay anday eythay, ethay Andar-logbay, earfay
Aakay ethay Ockray Akesnay. Ehay ancay imbclay asay ellway asay eythay ancay. Ehay ealsstay ethay
youngay onkeysmay inay ethay ightnay. Ethay isperwhay ofay ishay amenay akesmay eirthay ickedway
ailstay oldcay. Etlay usay ogay otay Aa.”kay

at“Whay illway ehay oday orfay usay? Ehay isay otnay ofay ouray ibetray, eingbay ootless--andfay
ithway ostmay evilay eyes,”ay aidsay Agheerabay.

e“Hay isay eryvay olday anday eryvay unningcay. Aboveay allay, ehay isay alwaysay ungry,”hay aidsay
Aloobay opefullyhay. omise“Pray imhay anymay oats.”gay

Agheerabay, owhay idday otnay owknay uchmay aboutay Aakay, asway aturallynay uspicioussay.

en“Thay inay atthay asecay, outhay anday Iay ogethertay, olday unterhay, ightmay akemay imhay eesay

ofay ishay odybay intoay antasticfay otsknay anday urvescay, anday ickinglay ishay ipslay asay ehay

e“Hay ashay otnay eaten,”ay aidsay Aloobay, ithway aay untgray ofay eliefray, asay oonsay asay

eryvay uickqay otay ike.”stray

ood“Gay untinghay orfay usay all,”ay ehay answereday. Oho“ay, Aloobay, atwhay ostday outhay oday

omething“Say ofay atthay indkay itay asway atthay eythay outedshay otay usay astlay oonmay, utbay eway

ull“Fay orgegay anday aay eepday eepslay otay youay, Ann,”ray iedcray Agheerabay. I“ay illway

Eythay allay ewknay erewhay atthay aceplay asway, utbay ewfay ofay ethay Unglejay Eoplepay everay
entway erethay, ecausebay atwhay eythay alledcay ethay Oldcay Airslay asway anay olday esertedday
itycay, ostlay anday uriedbay inay ethay unglejay, anday eastsbay eldomsay useay aay aceplay atthay
enmay avehay onceay useday. Ethay ildway oarbay illway, utbay ethay untinghay ibestray oday otnay.
Esidesbay, ethay onkeysmay ivedlay erethay asay uchmay asay eythay ouldcay ebay aidsay otay ivelay
anywhereay, anday onay elf-respectingsay animalay ouldway omecay ithinway eyeshotay ofay itay

eldhay aay ittlelay aterway.

anther-canterpay. Aakay aidsay othingnay, utbay, ivestray asay Agheerabay ightmay, ethay
ugehay Ock-pythonray eldhay evellay ithway imhay. Enwhay eythay amecay otay aay illhay eamstray,
