y“Bay ethay Okenbray Ocklay atthay eedfray e,”may aidsay Agheerabay, enwhay ilighttway adhay
allenfay, ou“thay artay onay owslay oer!”gay

I“ay amay ungry,”hay aidsay Aakay. esides“Bay, eythay alledcay emay eckledspay og.”fray

orm--earth-worm“Way, anday yelloway otay oot.”bay

All“ay oneay. Etlay usay ogay on,”ay anday Aakay eemedsay otay ourpay imselfhay alongay ethay
oundgray, indingfay ethay ortestshay oadray ithway ishay eadystay eyesay, anday eepingkay otay
itay.

Inay ethay Oldcay Airslay ethay Onkey-Peoplemay ereway otnay inkingthay ofay Owgli’smay
iendsfray atay allay. Eythay adhay oughtbray ethay oybay otay ethay Ostlay Itycay, anday ereway
eryvay uchmay easedplay ithway emselvesthay orfay ethay imetay. Owglimay adhay evernay eensay anay
Indianay itycay eforebay, anday oughthay isthay asway almostay aay eaphay ofay uinsray itay eemedsay
eryvay onderfulway anday endidsplay. Omesay ingkay adhay uiltbay itay onglay agoay onay aay ittlelay
illhay. Youay ouldcay illstay acetray ethay onestay ausewayscay atthay edlay upay otay ethay
uinedray atesgay erewhay ethay astlay interssplay ofay oodway unghay otay ethay ornway, ustedray
ingeshay. Eestray adhay owngray intoay anday outay ofay ethay alls;way ethay attlementsbay ereway
umbledtay ownday anday ecayedday, anday ildway eeperscray unghay outay ofay ethay indowsway ofay
ethay owerstay onay ethay allsway inay ushybay anginghay umpsclay.

Aay eatgray ooflessray alacepay ownedcray ethay illhay, anday ethay arblemay ofay ethay
ourtyardscay anday ethay ountainsfay asway itsplay, anday ainedstay ithway edray anday eengray,
anday ethay eryvay obblestonescay inay ethay ourtyardcay erewhay ethay ing’skay elephantsay
useday otay ivelay adhay eenbay ustthray upay anday apartay ybay assesgray anday youngay eestray.
Omfray ethay alacepay youay ouldcay eesay ethay owsray anday owsray ofay ooflessray ouseshay atthay
ademay upay ethay itycay ookinglay ikelay emptyay oneycombshay illedfay ithway ackness;blay
ethay apelessshay ockblay ofay onestay atthay adhay eenbay anay idolay inay ethay uaresqay erewhay
ourfay oadsray et;may ethay itspay anday implesday atay eetstray ornerscay erewhay ethay ublicpay
ellsway onceay oodstay, anday ethay atteredshay omesday ofay emplestay ithway ildway igsfay
outingspray onay eirthay idessay. Ethay onkeysmay alledcay ethay aceplay eirthay itycay, anday
etendedpray otay espiseday ethay Ungle-Peoplejay ecausebay eythay ivedlay inay ethay orestfay.
Anday yetay eythay evernay ewknay atwhay ethay uildingsbay ereway ademay orfay ornay owhay otay
useay emthay. Eythay ouldway itsay inay irclescay onay ethay allhay ofay ethay ing’skay ouncilcay
amberchay, anday atchscray orfay easflay anday etendpray otay ebay en;may oray eythay ouldway unray
inay anday outay ofay ethay ooflessray ouseshay anday ollectcay iecespay ofay asterplay anday olday
icksbray inay aay ornercay, anday orgetfay erewhay eythay adhay iddenhay emthay, anday ightfay
anday ycray inay ufflingscay owdscray, anday enthay eakbray offay otay ayplay upay anday ownday ethay
erracestay ofay ethay ing’skay ardengay, erewhay eythay ouldway akeshay ethay oseray eestray anday
ethay orangesay inay ortspay otay eesay ethay uitfray anday owersflay allfay. Eythay exploreday
allay ethay assagespay anday arkday unnelstay inay ethay alacepay anday ethay undredshay ofay
ittlelay arkday oomsray, utbay eythay evernay ememberedray atwhay eythay adhay eensay anday atwhay
eythay adhay ot;nay anday osay ifteddray aboutay inay onesay anday ostway oray owdscray ellingtay
eachay otheray atthay eythay ereway oingday asay enmay idday. Eythay ankdray atay ethay ankstay anday
ademay ethay aterway allay uddymay, anday enthay eythay oughtfay overay itay, anday enthay eythay
ouldway allay ushray ogethertay inay obsmay anday out:shay ere“Thay isay onay oneay inay ethay
unglejay osay iseway anday oodgay anday everclay anday ongstray anday entlegay asay ethay
Andar-log.”bay Enthay allay ouldway eginbay againay illtay eythay ewgray iredtay ofay ethay itycay
anday entway ackbay otay ethay ee-topstray, opinghay ethay Ungle-Peoplejay ouldway oticenay
emthay.

Owglimay, owhay adhay eenbay ainedtray underay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay, idday otnay ikelay
oray understanday isthay indkay ofay ifelay. Ethay onkeysmay aggeddray imhay intoay ethay Oldcay
Airslay atelay inay ethay afternoonay, anday insteaday ofay oinggay otay eepslay, asay Owglimay
ouldway avehay oneday afteray aay onglay ourneyjay, eythay oinedjay andshay anday ancedday aboutay
anday angsay eirthay oolishfay ongssay. Oneay ofay ethay onkeysmay ademay aay eechspay anday oldtay
ishay ompanionscay atthay Owgli’smay apturecay arkedmay aay ewnay ingthay inay ethay istoryhay
ofay ethay Andar-logbay, orfay Owglimay asway oinggay otay owshay emthay owhay otay eaveway icksstay
anday anescay ogethertay asay aay otectionpray againstay ainray anday oldcay. Owglimay ickedpay
upay omesay eeperscray anday eganbay otay orkway emthay inay anday outay, anday ethay onkeysmay
iedtray otay imitate;ay utbay inay aay eryvay ewfay inutesmay eythay ostlay interestay anday eganbay
otay ullpay eirthay iends’fray ailstay oray umpjay upay anday ownday onay allay oursfay, oughingcay.

I“ay ishway otay eat,”ay aidsay Owglimay. I“ay amay aay angerstray inay isthay artpay ofay ethay
unglejay. Ingbray emay oodfay, oray ivegay emay eavelay otay unthay ere.”hay

Entytway oray irtythay onkeysmay oundedbay awayay otay ingbray imhay utsnay anday ildway
awpawspay. Utbay eythay ellfay otay ightingfay onay ethay oadray, anday itay asway ootay uchmay
oubletray otay ogay ackbay ithway atwhay asway eftlay ofay ethay uitfray. Owglimay asway oresay anday
angryay asay ellway asay ungryhay, anday ehay oamedray oughthray ethay emptyay itycay ivinggay ethay
Angers’stray Untinghay Allcay omfray imetay otay imetay, utbay onay oneay answereday imhay, anday
Owglimay eltfay atthay ehay adhay eachedray aay eryvay adbay aceplay indeeday. All“ay atthay Aloobay
ashay aidsay aboutay ethay Andar-logbay isay ue,”tray ehay oughtthay otay imselfhay. ey“Thay
avehay onay Awlay, onay Untinghay Allcay, anday onay eaders--nothinglay utbay oolishfay ordsway
anday ittlelay ickingpay ievishthay andshay. Osay ifay Iay amay arvedstay oray illedkay erehay,
itay illway ebay allay ymay ownay aultfay. Utbay Iay ustmay ytray otay eturnray otay ymay ownay unglejay.
Aloobay illway urelysay eatbay emay, utbay atthay isay etterbay anthay asingchay illysay oseray
eaveslay ithway ethay Andar-log.”bay

Onay oonersay adhay ehay alkedway otay ethay itycay allway anthay ethay onkeysmay ulledpay imhay
ackbay, ellingtay imhay atthay ehay idday otnay owknay owhay appyhay ehay asway, anday inchingpay
imhay otay akemay imhay atefulgray. Ehay etsay ishay eethtay anday aidsay othingnay, utbay entway
ithway ethay outingshay onkeysmay otay aay erracetay aboveay ethay edray andstonesay
eservoirsray atthay ereway alf-fullhay ofay ainray aterway. Erethay asway aay uinedray
ummer-housesay ofay itewhay arblemay inay ethay entercay ofay ethay erracetay, uiltbay orfay
ueensqay eadday aay undredhay yearsay agoay. Ethay omedday oofray adhay alfhay allenfay inay anday
ockedblay upay ethay undergrounday assagepay omfray ethay alacepay ybay ichwhay ethay ueensqay
useday otay enteray. Utbay ethay allsway ereway ademay ofay eensscray ofay arblemay
acery--beautifultray ilk-whitemay etworkfray, etsay ithway agatesay anday ornelianscay
anday asperjay anday apislay azulilay, anday asay ethay oonmay amecay upay ehindbay ethay illhay itay
oneshay oughthray ethay openay orkway, astingcay adowsshay onay ethay oundgray ikelay ackblay
elvetvay embroideryay. Oresay, eepyslay, anday ungryhay asay ehay asway, Owglimay ouldcay otnay
elphay aughinglay enwhay ethay Andar-logbay eganbay, entytway atay aay imetay, otay elltay imhay
owhay eatgray anday iseway anday ongstray anday entlegay eythay ereway, anday owhay oolishfay ehay
asway otay ishway otay eavelay emthay. e“Way areay eatgray. Eway areay eefray. Eway areay
onderfulway. Eway areay ethay ostmay onderfulway eoplepay inay allay ethay unglejay! Eway allay
aysay osay, anday osay itay ustmay ebay ue,”tray eythay outedshay. ow“Nay asay youay areay aay ewnay
istenerlay anday ancay arrycay ouray ordsway ackbay otay ethay Ungle-Peoplejay osay atthay eythay
aymay oticenay usay inay uturefay, eway illway elltay youay allay aboutay ouray ostmay excellentay
elves.”say Owglimay ademay onay objectionay, anday ethay onkeysmay atheredgay ybay undredshay
anday undredshay onay ethay erracetay otay istenlay otay eirthay ownay eakersspay ingingsay ethay
aisespray ofay ethay Andar-logbay, anday eneverwhay aay eakerspay oppedstay orfay antway ofay
eathbray eythay ouldway allay outshay ogether:tay is“Thay isay ue;tray eway allay aysay o.”say
Owglimay oddednay anday inkedblay, anday aidsay Yes”“ay enwhay eythay askeday imhay aay
uestionqay, anday ishay eadhay unspay ithway ethay oisenay. abaqui“Tay ethay Ackaljay ustmay
avehay ittenbay allay esethay eople,”pay ehay aidsay otay imselfhay, and“ay ownay eythay avehay
adnessmay. Ertainlycay isthay isay ewanee__day, ethay adnessmay. Oday eythay evernay ogay otay
eepslay? Ownay erethay isay aay oudclay omingcay otay overcay atthay oonmay. Ifay itay ereway onlyay
aay igbay enoughay oudclay Iay ightmay ytray otay unray awayay inay ethay arknessday. Utbay Iay amay
ired.”tay

Atthay amesay oudclay asway eingbay atchedway ybay otway oodgay iendsfray inay ethay uinedray
itchday elowbay ethay itycay allway, orfay Agheerabay anday Aakay, owingknay ellway owhay
angerousday ethay Onkey-Peoplemay ereway inay argelay umbersnay, idday otnay ishway otay unray
anyay isksray. Ethay onkeysmay evernay ightfay unlessay eythay areay aay undredhay otay oneay, anday
ewfay inay ethay unglejay arecay orfay osethay oddsay.

I“ay illway ogay otay ethay estway all,”way Aakay isperedwhay, and“ay omecay ownday iftlysway ithway

I“ay owknay it,”ay aidsay Agheerabay. ould“Way atthay Aloobay ereway erehay, utbay eway ustmay oday

ood“Gay unting,”hay aidsay Aakay imlygray, anday idedglay awayay otay ethay estway allway. Atthay

Agheerabay eardhay, anday ethay ycray atthay oldtay imhay Owglimay asway afesay avegay imhay ewnay

Owglimay atthay Agheerabay adhay oughtfay ishay ayway otay ethay anktay erewhay ethay onkeysmay

ethay edgeay ofay ethay erracetay, ouldcay otnay elphay ucklingchay asay ehay eardhay ethay Ackblay
Antherpay askingay orfay elphay.

Aakay adhay onlyay ustjay orkedway ishay ayway overay ethay estway allway, andinglay ithway aay
enchwray atthay islodgedday aay opingcay onestay intoay ethay itchday. Ehay adhay onay intentionay
ofay osinglay anyay advantageay ofay ethay oundgray, anday oiledcay anday uncoileday imselfhay
onceay oray icetway, otay ebay uresay atthay everyay ootfay ofay ishay onglay odybay asway inay
orkingway orderay. Allay atthay ilewhay ethay ightfay ithway Aloobay entway onay, anday ethay
onkeysmay yelleday inay ethay anktay oundray Agheerabay, anday Angmay ethay Atbay, yingflay otay
anday ofray, arriedcay ethay ewsnay ofay ethay eatgray attlebay overay ethay unglejay, illtay evenay
Athihay ethay Ildway Elephantay umpetedtray, anday, arfay awayay, atteredscay andsbay ofay
ethay Onkey-Folkmay okeway anday amecay eapinglay alongay ethay ee-roadstray otay elphay eirthay
omradescay inay ethay Oldcay Airslay, anday ethay oisenay ofay ethay ightfay ousedray allay ethay
ayday irdsbay orfay ilesmay oundray. Enthay Aakay amecay aightstray, uicklyqay, anday anxiousay
otay illkay. Ethay ightingfay engthstray ofay aay ythonpay isay inay ethay ivingdray owblay ofay
ishay eadhay ackedbay ybay allay ethay engthstray anday eightway ofay ishay odybay. Ifay youay ancay
imagineay aay ancelay, oray aay atteringbay amray, oray aay ammerhay eighingway earlynay alfhay
aay ontay ivendray ybay aay oolcay, uietqay indmay ivinglay inay ethay andlehay ofay itay, youay ancay
oughlyray imagineay atwhay Aakay asway ikelay enwhay ehay oughtfay. Aay ythonpay ourfay oray ivefay
eetfay onglay ancay ockknay aay anmay ownday ifay ehay itshay imhay airlyfay inay ethay estchay, anday
Aakay asway irtythay eetfay onglay, asay youay owknay. Ishay irstfay okestray asway eliveredday
intoay ethay earthay ofay ethay owdcray oundray Aloobay. Itay asway entsay omehay ithway utshay
outhmay inay ilencesay, anday erethay asway onay eednay ofay aay econdsay. Ethay onkeysmay
atteredscay ithway iescray of--“Kaaay! Itay isay Aakay! Unray! Un!”ray

Enerationsgay ofay onkeysmay adhay eenbay aredscay intoay oodgay ehaviorbay ybay ethay oriesstay
eirthay eldersay oldtay emthay ofay Aakay, ethay ightnay iefthay, owhay ouldcay ipslay alongay ethay
anchesbray asay uietlyqay asay ossmay owsgray, anday ealstay awayay ethay ongeststray onkeymay
atthay everay ived;lay ofay olday Aakay, owhay ouldcay akemay imselfhay ooklay osay ikelay aay eadday
anchbray oray aay ottenray umpstay atthay ethay isestway ereway eceivedday, illtay ethay anchbray
aughtcay emthay. Aakay asway everythingay atthay ethay onkeysmay earedfay inay ethay unglejay,
orfay onenay ofay emthay ewknay ethay imitslay ofay ishay owerpay, onenay ofay emthay ouldcay ooklay
imhay inay ethay acefay, anday onenay adhay everay omecay aliveay outay ofay ishay ughay. Anday osay
eythay anray, ammeringstay ithway errortay, otay ethay allsway anday ethay oofsray ofay ethay
ouseshay, anday Aloobay ewdray aay eepday eathbray ofay eliefray. Ishay urfay asway uchmay ickerthay
anthay Agheera’sbay, utbay ehay adhay ufferedsay orelysay inay ethay ightfay. Enthay Aakay
openeday ishay outhmay orfay ethay irstfay imetay anday okespay oneay onglay issinghay ordway, anday

erewhay eythay ereway, oweringcay, illtay ethay oadedlay anchesbray entbay anday ackledcray
underay emthay. Ethay onkeysmay onay ethay allsway anday ethay emptyay ouseshay oppedstay
eirthay iescray, anday inay ethay illnessstay atthay ellfay uponay ethay itycay Owglimay eardhay
Agheerabay akingshay ishay etway idessay asay ehay amecay upay omfray ethay anktay. Enthay ethay
amorclay okebray outay againay. Ethay onkeysmay eapedlay igherhay upay ethay allsway. Eythay
ungclay arounday ethay ecksnay ofay ethay igbay onestay idolsay anday iekedshray asay eythay

eep“Kay ythay andhay onay ymay oulder,”shay Agheerabay isperedwhay. eep“Kay itay erethay, oray Iay
ustmay ogay ack--mustbay ogay ackbay otay Aakay. Aah!”ay

It“ay isay onlyay olday Aakay akingmay irclescay onay ethay ust,”day aidsay Owglimay. et“Lay usay
o.”gay Anday ethay eethray ippedslay offay oughthray aay apgay inay ethay allsway otay ethay unglejay.

oof!”“Whay aidsay Aloobay, enwhay ehay oodstay underay ethay illstay eestray againay. ever“Nay
oremay illway Iay akemay anay allyay ofay Aa,”kay anday ehay ookshay imselfhay allay overay.

e“Hay owsknay oremay anthay e,”way aidsay Agheerabay, emblingtray. In“ay aay ittlelay imetay,
adhay Iay ayedstay, Iay ouldshay avehay alkedway ownday ishay oat.”thray

any“May illway alkway ybay atthay oadray eforebay ethay oonmay isesray again,”ay aidsay Aloobay.
e“Hay illway avehay oodgay unting--afterhay ishay ownay ashion.”fay

ut“Bay atwhay asway ethay eaningmay ofay itay all?”ay aidsay Owglimay, owhay idday otnay owknay
anythingay ofay aay ython’spay owerspay ofay ascinationfay. I“ay awsay onay oremay anthay aay igbay
akesnay akingmay oolishfay irclescay illtay ethay arkday amecay. Anday ishay osenay asway allay
oresay. Ohay! O!”hay

owgli,”“May aidsay Agheerabay angrilyay, is“hay osenay asway oresay onay ythay accountay, asay
ymay earsay anday idessay anday awspay, anday Aloo’sbay ecknay anday ouldersshay areay ittenbay
onay ythay accountay. Eithernay Aloobay ornay Agheerabay illway ebay ableay otay unthay ithway
easureplay orfay anymay ays.”day

It“ay isay othing,”nay aidsay Aloo;bay e“way avehay ethay an-cubmay again.”ay

ue“Tray, utbay ehay ashay ostcay usay eavilyhay inay imetay ichwhay ightmay avehay eenbay entspay inay
oodgay untinghay, inay oundsway, inay air--Ihay amay alfhay uckedplay alongay ymay ack--andbay
astlay ofay allay, inay onorhay. Orfay, ememberray, Owglimay, Iay, owhay amay ethay Ackblay
Antherpay, asway orcedfay otay allcay uponay Aakay orfay otectionpray, anday Aloobay anday Iay
ereway othbay ademay upidstay asay ittlelay irdsbay ybay ethay Ungerhay Anceday. Allay isthay,
an-cubmay, amecay ofay ythay ayingplay ithway ethay Andar-log.”bay

ue“Tray, itay isay ue,”tray aidsay Owglimay orrowfullysay. I“ay amay anay evilay an-cubmay, anday
ymay omachstay isay adsay inay e.”may

“Mfay! Atwhay ayssay ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay, Aloo?”bay

Aloobay idday otnay ishway otay ingbray Owglimay intoay anyay oremay oubletray, utbay ehay ouldcay
otnay ampertay ithway ethay Awlay, osay ehay umbled:may orrow“Say evernay aysstay unishmentpay.
Utbay ememberray, Agheerabay, ehay isay eryvay ittle.”lay

I“ay illway ememberray. Utbay ehay ashay oneday ischiefmay, anday owsblay ustmay ebay ealtday ownay.
Owglimay, asthay outhay anythingay otay ay?”say

othing“Nay. Iay idday ongwray. Aloobay anday outhay areay oundedway. Itay isay ust.”jay

Agheerabay avegay imhay alfhay aay ozenday ove-tapslay omfray aay anther’spay ointpay ofay
iewvay ey(thay ouldway ardlyhay avehay akedway oneay ofay ishay ownay ubs)cay, utbay orfay aay
even-year-oldsay oybay eythay amounteday otay asay everesay aay eatingbay asay youay ouldcay
ishway otay avoiday. Enwhay itay asway allay overay Owglimay eezedsnay, anday ickedpay imselfhay
upay ithoutway aay ordway.

ow,”“Nay aidsay Agheerabay, ump“jay onay ymay ackbay, Ittlelay Otherbray, anday eway illway ogay
ome.”hay

Oneay ofay ethay eautiesbay ofay Unglejay Awlay isay atthay unishmentpay ettlessay allay oresscay.
Erethay isay onay aggingnay afterwarday.

Owglimay aidlay ishay eadhay ownday onay Agheera’sbay ackbay anday eptslay osay eeplyday atthay ehay
evernay akedway enwhay ehay asway utpay ownday inay ethay ome-cavehay.




Oad-Songray ofay ethay Andar-Logbay

Erehay eway ogay inay aay ungflay estoonfay,
Alf-wayhay upay otay ethay ealousjay oonmay!
On’tday youay envyay ouray ancefulpray andsbay?
On’tday youay ishway youay adhay extraay andshay?
Ouldn’tway youay ikelay ifay youray ailstay ere--so--way
Urvedcay inay ethay apeshay ofay aay Upid’scay owbay?
Ownay you’reay angryay, ut--neverbay indmay,
other_Bray, ythay ailtay angshay ownday ehind!_bay

Erehay eway itsay inay aay anchybray owray,
Inkingthay ofay eautifulbay ingsthay eway ow;knay
Eamingdray ofay eedsday atthay eway eanmay otay oday,
Allay ompletecay, inay aay inutemay oray o--tway
Omethingsay oblenay anday iseway anday oodgay,
Oneday ybay erelymay ishingway eway ouldcay.
E’veway orgottenfay, ut--neverbay indmay,
other_Bray, ythay ailtay angshay ownday ehind!_bay

Allay ethay alktay eway everay avehay eardhay
Uttereday ybay atbay oray eastbay oray ird--bay
Idehay oray infay oray alescay oray eather--fay
Abberjay itay uicklyqay anday allay ogethertay!
Excellentay! Onderfulway! Onceay againay!

Ownay eway areay alkingtay ustjay ikelay enmay!
Et’slay etendpray eway areay ... evernay indmay,
other_Bray, ythay ailtay angshay ownday ehind!_bay
Isthay isay ethay ayway ofay ethay Onkey-kindmay.

en_Thay oinjay ouray eapinglay ineslay atthay umfishscay oughthray ethay inespay,
Atthay ocketray ybay erewhay, ightlay anday ighhay, ethay ildway apegray ingssway.
Ybay ethay ubbishray inay ouray akeway, anday ethay oblenay oisenay eway akemay,
Ebay uresay, ebay uresay, e’reway oinggay otay oday omesay endidsplay ings!_thay




iger“Tay! Iger!”tay

Atwhay ofay ethay untinghay, unterhay oldbay?
Otherbray, ethay atchway asway onglay anday oldcay.
Atwhay ofay ethay uarryqay yeay entway otay illkay?
Otherbray, ehay opscray inay ethay unglejay illstay.
Erewhay isay ethay owerpay atthay ademay youray idepray?
Otherbray, itay ebbsay omfray ymay ankflay anday idesay.
Erewhay isay ethay astehay atthay yeay urryhay ybay?
Otherbray, Iay ogay otay ymay air--tolay ieday.

Ownay eway ustmay ogay ackbay otay ethay irstfay aletay. Enwhay Owglimay eftlay ethay olf’sway avecay
afteray ethay ightfay ithway ethay Ackpay atay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, ehay entway ownday otay ethay
owedplay andslay erewhay ethay illagersvay ivedlay, utbay ehay ouldway otnay opstay erethay
ecausebay itay asway ootay earnay otay ethay unglejay, anday ehay ewknay atthay ehay adhay ademay atay
eastlay oneay adbay enemyay atay ethay Ouncilcay. Osay ehay urriedhay onay, eepingkay otay
ethay oughray oadray atthay anray ownday ethay alleyvay, anday ollowedfay itay atay aay eadystay
og-trotjay orfay earlynay entytway ilesmay, illtay ehay amecay otay aay ountrycay atthay ehay
idday otnay owknay. Ethay alleyvay openeday outay intoay aay eatgray ainplay ottedday overay ithway
ocksray anday utcay upay ybay avinesray. Atay oneay enday oodstay aay ittlelay illagevay, anday atay
ethay otheray ethay ickthay unglejay amecay ownday inay aay eepsway otay ethay azing-groundsgray,
anday oppedstay erethay asay oughthay itay adhay eenbay utcay offay ithway aay oehay. Allay overay ethay
ainplay, attlecay anday uffaloesbay ereway azinggray, anday enwhay ethay ittlelay oysbay inay
argechay ofay ethay erdshay awsay Owglimay eythay outedshay anday anray awayay, anday ethay yelloway
ariahpay ogsday atthay anghay aboutay everyay Indianay illagevay arkedbay. Owglimay alkedway
onay, orfay ehay asway eelingfay ungryhay, anday enwhay ehay amecay otay ethay illagevay ategay ehay
awsay ethay igbay orn-bushthay atthay asway awndray upay eforebay ethay ategay atay ilighttway,
ushedpay otay oneay idesay.

Umph!”“ay ehay aidsay, orfay ehay adhay omecay acrossay oremay anthay oneay uchsay arricadebay inay
ishay ightnay amblesray afteray ingsthay otay eatay. o“Say enmay areay afraiday ofay ethay Eoplepay
ofay ethay Unglejay erehay also.”ay Ehay atsay ownday ybay ethay ategay, anday enwhay aay anmay amecay
outay ehay oodstay upay, openeday ishay outhmay, anday ointedpay ownday itay otay owshay atthay
ehay antedway oodfay. Ethay anmay aredstay, anday anray ackbay upay ethay oneay eetstray ofay ethay
illagevay outingshay orfay ethay iestpray, owhay asway aay igbay, atfay anmay esseddray inay
itewhay, ithway aay edray anday yelloway arkmay onay ishay oreheadfay. Ethay iestpray amecay otay
ethay ategay, anday ithway imhay atay eastlay aay undredhay eoplepay, owhay aredstay anday alkedtay
anday outedshay anday ointedpay atay Owglimay.

ey“Thay avehay onay annersmay, esethay Enmay Olk,”fay aidsay Owglimay otay imselfhay. Only“ay
ethay aygray apeay ouldway ehavebay asay eythay o.”day Osay ehay ewthray ackbay ishay onglay airhay
anday ownedfray atay ethay owdcray.

at“Whay isay erethay otay ebay afraiday of?”ay aidsay ethay iestpray. ook“Lay atay ethay arksmay onay
ishay armsay anday egslay. Eythay areay ethay itesbay ofay olvesway. Ehay isay utbay aay olf-childway
unray awayay omfray ethay ungle.”jay

Ofay oursecay, inay ayingplay ogethertay, ethay ubscay adhay oftenay ippednay Owglimay arderhay
anthay eythay intendeday, anday erethay ereway itewhay arsscay allay overay ishay armsay anday
egslay. Utbay ehay ouldway avehay eenbay ethay astlay ersonpay inay ethay orldway otay allcay esethay
itesbay, orfay ehay ewknay atwhay ealray itingbay eantmay.

Arre“ay! Arre!”ay aidsay otway oray eethray omenway ogethertay. o“Tay ebay ittenbay ybay olvesway,
oorpay ildchay! Ehay isay aay andsomehay oybay. Ehay ashay eyesay ikelay edray irefay. Ybay ymay
onorhay, Essuamay, ehay isay otnay unlikeay ythay oybay atthay asway akentay ybay ethay iger.”tay

et“Lay emay ook,”lay aidsay aay omanway ithway eavyhay oppercay ingsray onay erhay istswray anday
anklesay, anday eshay eeredpay atay Owglimay underay ethay almpay ofay erhay andhay. Indeed“ay ehay
isay otnay. Ehay isay innerthay, utbay ehay ashay ethay eryvay ooklay ofay ymay oy.”bay

Ethay iestpray asway aay everclay anmay, anday ehay ewknay atthay Essuamay asway ifeway otay ethay
ichestray illagervay inay ethay aceplay. Osay ehay ookedlay upay atay ethay yskay orfay aay inutemay
anday aidsay olemnly:say at“Whay ethay unglejay ashay akentay ethay unglejay ashay estoredray.
Aketay ethay oybay intoay ythay ousehay, ymay istersay, anday orgetfay otnay otay onorhay ethay
iestpray owhay eessay osay arfay intoay ethay iveslay ofay en.”may

y“Bay ethay Ullbay atthay oughtbay e,”may aidsay Owglimay otay imselfhay, ut“bay allay isthay
alkingtay isay ikelay anotheray ooking-overlay ybay ethay Ackpay! Ellway, ifay Iay amay aay anmay, aay
anmay Iay ustmay ecome.”bay

Ethay owdcray artedpay asay ethay omanway eckonedbay Owglimay otay erhay uthay, erewhay erethay
asway aay edray acqueredlay edsteadbay, aay eatgray earthenay aingray estchay ithway unnyfay
aisedray atternspay onay itay, alfhay aay ozenday oppercay ookingcay otspay, anay imageay ofay aay
Induhay odgay inay aay ittlelay alcoveay, anday onay ethay allway aay ealray ookinglay assglay, uchsay
asay eythay ellsay atay ethay ountrycay airsfay.

Eshay avegay imhay aay onglay inkdray ofay ilkmay anday omesay eadbray, anday enthay eshay aidlay erhay
andhay onay ishay eadhay anday ookedlay intoay ishay eyes;ay orfay eshay oughtthay erhapspay atthay
ehay ightmay ebay erhay ealray onsay omecay ackbay omfray ethay unglejay erewhay ethay igertay adhay
akentay imhay. Osay eshay aidsay, athoo“Nay, Oay Athoo!”nay Owglimay idday otnay owshay atthay ehay
ewknay ethay amenay. ost“Day outhay otnay ememberray ethay ayday enwhay Iay avegay eethay ythay ewnay
oes?”shay Eshay ouchedtay ishay ootfay, anday itay asway almostay asay ardhay asay ornhay. o,”“Nay
eshay aidsay orrowfullysay, ose“thay eetfay avehay evernay ornway oesshay, utbay outhay artay
eryvay ikelay ymay Athoonay, anday outhay altshay ebay ymay on.”say

Owglimay asway uneasyay, ecausebay ehay adhay evernay eenbay underay aay oofray eforebay. Utbay asay
ehay ookedlay atay ethay atchthay, ehay awsay atthay ehay ouldcay eartay itay outay anyay imetay ifay ehay
antedway otay etgay awayay, anday atthay ethay indowway adhay onay asteningsfay. at“Whay isay ethay
oodgay ofay aay an,”may ehay aidsay otay imselfhay atay astlay, if“ay ehay oesday otnay understanday
an’smay alktay? Ownay Iay amay asay illysay anday umbday asay aay anmay ouldway ebay ithway usay inay ethay
unglejay. Iay ustmay eakspay eirthay alk.”tay

Itay asway otnay orfay unfay atthay ehay adhay earnedlay ilewhay ehay asway ithway ethay olvesway otay
imitateay ethay allengechay ofay ucksbay inay ethay unglejay anday ethay untgray ofay ethay ittlelay
ildway igpay. Osay, asay oonsay asay Essuamay onouncedpray aay ordway Owglimay ouldway imitateay
itay almostay erfectlypay, anday eforebay arkday ehay adhay earnedlay ethay amesnay ofay anymay
ingsthay inay ethay uthay.

Erethay asway aay ifficultyday atay edtimebay, ecausebay Owglimay ouldway otnay eepslay underay
anythingay atthay ookedlay osay ikelay aay antherpay aptray asay atthay uthay, anday enwhay eythay
utshay ethay oorday ehay entway oughthray ethay indowway. ive“Gay imhay ishay ill,”way aidsay
Essua’smay usbandhay. emember“Ray ehay ancay evernay illtay ownay avehay eptslay onay aay edbay.
Ifay ehay isay indeeday entsay inay ethay aceplay ofay ouray onsay ehay illway otnay unray away.”ay

Osay Owglimay etchedstray imselfhay inay omesay onglay, eanclay assgray atay ethay edgeay ofay
ethay ieldfay, utbay eforebay ehay adhay osedclay ishay eyesay aay oftsay aygray osenay okedpay imhay
underay ethay inchay.

ew!”“Phay aidsay Aygray Otherbray e(hay asway ethay eldestay ofay Othermay Olf’sway ubs)cay.
is“Thay isay aay oorpay ewardray orfay ollowingfay eethay entytway ilesmay. Outhay ellestsmay
ofay oodway okesmay anday attle--altogethercay ikelay aay anmay alreadyay. Akeway, Ittlelay
Other;bray Iay ingbray ews.”nay

Are“ay allay ellway inay ethay ungle?”jay aidsay Owglimay, ugginghay imhay.

All“ay exceptay ethay olvesway atthay ereway urnedbay ithway ethay Edray Owerflay. Ownay,
istenlay. Ereshay Ankhay ashay onegay awayay otay unthay arfay offay illtay ishay oatcay owsgray
againay, orfay ehay isay adlybay ingedsay. Enwhay ehay eturnsray ehay earssway atthay ehay illway
aylay ythay onesbay inay ethay Aingunga.”way

ere“Thay areay otway ordsway otay atthay. Iay alsoay avehay ademay aay ittlelay omisepray. Utbay
ewsnay isay alwaysay oodgay. Iay amay iredtay o-night,--verytay iredtay ithway ewnay ingsthay,
Aygray Other,--butbray ingbray emay ethay ewsnay always.”ay

ou“Thay iltway otnay orgetfay atthay outhay artay aay olfway? Enmay illway otnay akemay eethay
orget?”fay aidsay Aygray Otherbray anxiouslyay.

ever“Nay. Iay illway alwaysay ememberray atthay Iay ovelay eethay anday allay inay ouray avecay. Utbay
alsoay Iay illway alwaysay ememberray atthay Iay avehay eenbay astcay outay ofay ethay Ack.”pay

And“ay atthay outhay ayestmay ebay astcay outay ofay anotheray ackpay. Enmay areay onlyay enmay,
Ittlelay Otherbray, anday eirthay alktay isay ikelay ethay alktay ofay ogsfray inay aay ondpay. Enwhay
Iay omecay ownday erehay againay, Iay illway aitway orfay eethay inay ethay amboosbay atay ethay edgeay
ofay ethay azing-ground.”gray

Orfay eethray onthsmay afteray atthay ightnay Owglimay ardlyhay everay eftlay ethay illagevay
ategay, ehay asway osay usybay earninglay ethay aysway anday ustomscay ofay enmay. Irstfay ehay adhay
otay earway aay othclay oundray imhay, ichwhay annoyeday imhay orribly;hay anday enthay ehay adhay
otay earnlay aboutay oneymay, ichwhay ehay idday otnay inay ethay eastlay understanday, anday
aboutay owingplay, ofay ichwhay ehay idday otnay eesay ethay useay. Enthay ethay ittlelay ildrenchay
inay ethay illagevay ademay imhay eryvay angryay. Uckilylay, ethay Awlay ofay ethay Unglejay adhay
aughttay imhay otay eepkay ishay empertay, orfay inay ethay unglejay ifelay anday oodfay ependday onay
eepingkay youray emper;tay utbay enwhay eythay ademay unfay ofay imhay ecausebay ehay ouldway otnay
ayplay amesgay oray yflay iteskay, oray ecausebay ehay ispronouncedmay omesay ordway, onlyay ethay
owledgeknay atthay itay asway unsportsmanlikeay otay illkay ittlelay akednay ubscay eptkay imhay
omfray ickingpay emthay upay anday eakingbray emthay inay otway.

Ehay idday otnay owknay ishay ownay engthstray inay ethay eastlay. Inay ethay unglejay ehay ewknay ehay
asway eakway omparedcay ithway ethay eastsbay, utbay inay ethay illagevay eoplepay aidsay atthay
ehay asway asay ongstray asay aay ullbay.

Anday Owglimay adhay otnay ethay aintestfay ideaay ofay ethay ifferenceday atthay astecay akesmay
etweenbay anmay anday anmay. Enwhay ethay otter’spay onkeyday ippedslay inay ethay ayclay itpay,
Owglimay auledhay itay outay ybay ethay ailtay, anday elpedhay otay ackstay ethay otspay orfay eirthay
ourneyjay otay ethay arketmay atay Anhiwarakhay. Atthay asway eryvay ockingshay, ootay, orfay
ethay otterpay isay aay ow-castelay anmay, anday ishay onkeyday isay orseway. Enwhay ethay iestpray
oldedscay imhay, Owglimay eatenedthray otay utpay imhay onay ethay onkeyday ootay, anday ethay
iestpray oldtay Essua’smay usbandhay atthay Owglimay adhay etterbay ebay etsay otay orkway asay
oonsay asay ossible;pay anday ethay illagevay ead-manhay oldtay Owglimay atthay ehay ouldway
avehay otay ogay outay ithway ethay uffaloesbay extnay ayday, anday erdhay emthay ilewhay eythay
azedgray. Onay oneay asway oremay easedplay anthay Owgli;may anday atthay ightnay, ecausebay ehay
adhay eenbay appointeday aay ervantsay ofay ethay illagevay, asay itay ereway, ehay entway offay
otay aay irclecay atthay etmay everyay eveningay onay aay asonrymay atformplay underay aay eatgray
ig-treefay. Itay asway ethay illagevay ubclay, anday ethay ead-manhay anday ethay atchmanway anday
ethay arberbay, owhay ewknay allay ethay ossipgay ofay ethay illagevay, anday olday Uldeobay, ethay
illagevay unterhay, owhay adhay aay Owertay usketmay, etmay anday okedsmay. Ethay onkeysmay
atsay anday alkedtay inay ethay upperay anchesbray, anday erethay asway aay olehay underay ethay
atformplay erewhay aay obracay ivedlay, anday ehay adhay ishay ittlelay atterplay ofay ilkmay
everyay ightnay ecausebay ehay asway acred;say anday ethay olday enmay atsay arounday ethay eetray
anday alkedtay, anday ulledpay atay ethay igbay uqashay e(thay ater-pipesway) illtay arfay intoay
ethay ightnay. Eythay oldtay onderfulway alestay ofay odsgay anday enmay anday osts;ghay anday
Uldeobay oldtay evenay oremay onderfulway onesay ofay ethay aysway ofay eastsbay inay ethay
unglejay, illtay ethay eyesay ofay ethay ildrenchay ittingsay outsideay ethay irclecay ulgedbay
outay ofay eirthay eadshay. Ostmay ofay ethay alestay ereway aboutay animalsay, orfay ethay unglejay
asway alwaysay atay eirthay oorday. Ethay eerday anday ethay ildway igpay ubbedgray upay eirthay
opscray, anday ownay anday againay ethay igertay arriedcay offay aay anmay atay ilighttway, ithinway
ightsay ofay ethay illagevay atesgay.

Owglimay, owhay aturallynay ewknay omethingsay aboutay atwhay eythay ereway alkingtay ofay,
adhay otay overcay ishay acefay otnay otay owshay atthay ehay asway aughinglay, ilewhay Uldeobay,
ethay Owertay usketmay acrossay ishay eesknay, imbedclay onay omfray oneay onderfulway orystay
otay anotheray, anday Owgli’smay ouldersshay ookshay.

Uldeobay asway explainingay owhay ethay igertay atthay adhay arriedcay awayay Essua’smay onsay
asway aay ost-tigerghay, anday ishay odybay asway inhabiteday ybay ethay ostghay ofay aay ickedway,
olday oney-lendermay, owhay adhay iedday omesay yearsay agoay. And“ay Iay owknay atthay isthay isay
ue,”tray ehay aidsay, ecause“bay Urunpay Assday alwaysay impedlay omfray ethay owblay atthay ehay
otgay inay aay iotray enwhay ishay accountay ooksbay ereway urnedbay, anday ethay igertay atthay Iay
eakspay ofay ehay impslay, ootay, orfay ethay ackstray ofay ishay adspay areay unequal.”ay

ue“Tray, uetray, atthay ustmay ebay ethay uth,”tray aidsay ethay ay-beardsgray, oddingnay
ogethertay.

Are“ay allay esethay alestay uchsay obwebscay anday oontalk?”may aidsay Owglimay. at“Thay
igertay impslay ecausebay ehay asway ornbay amelay, asay everyoneay owsknay. Otay alktay ofay ethay
oulsay ofay aay oney-lendermay inay aay eastbay atthay evernay adhay ethay ouragecay ofay aay ackaljay
isay ild’schay alk.”tay

Uldeobay asway eechlessspay ithway urprisesay orfay aay omentmay, anday ethay ead-manhay
aredstay.

Oho“ay! Itay isay ethay unglejay atbray, isay it?”ay aidsay Uldeobay. If“ay outhay artay osay
iseway, etterbay ingbray ishay idehay otay Anhiwarakhay, orfay ethay Overnmentgay ashay etsay
aay undredhay upeesray onay ishay ifelay. Etterbay illstay, alktay otnay enwhay ythay eldersay
eak.”spay

Owglimay oseray otay ogay. All“ay ethay eveningay Iay avehay ainlay erehay istening,”lay ehay
alledcay ackbay overay ishay ouldershay, and“ay, exceptay onceay oray icetway, Uldeobay ashay
otnay aidsay oneay ordway ofay uthtray oncerningcay ethay unglejay, ichwhay isay atay ishay eryvay
oorsday. Owhay, enthay, allshay Iay elievebay ethay alestay ofay ostsghay anday odsgay anday
oblinsgay ichwhay ehay ayssay ehay ashay een?”say

It“ay isay ullfay imetay atthay oybay entway otay erding,”hay aidsay ethay ead-manhay, ilewhay
Uldeobay uffedpay anday ortedsnay atay Owgli’smay impertinenceay.

Ethay ustomcay ofay ostmay Indianay illagesvay isay orfay aay ewfay oysbay otay aketay ethay attlecay
anday uffaloesbay outay otay azegray inay ethay earlyay orningmay, anday ingbray emthay ackbay
atay ightnay. Ethay eryvay attlecay atthay ouldway ampletray aay itewhay anmay otay eathday alloway
emselvesthay otay ebay angedbay anday ulliedbay anday outedshay atay ybay ildrenchay atthay
ardlyhay omecay upay otay eirthay osesnay. Osay onglay asay ethay oysbay eepkay ithway ethay erdshay
eythay areay afesay, orfay otnay evenay ethay igertay illway argechay aay obmay ofay attlecay. Utbay
ifay eythay agglestray otay ickpay owersflay oray unthay izardslay, eythay areay ometimessay
arriedcay offay. Owglimay entway oughthray ethay illagevay eetstray inay ethay awnday, ittingsay
onay ethay ackbay ofay Amaray, ethay eatgray erdhay ullbay. Ethay aty-blueslay uffaloesbay,
ithway eirthay onglay, ackward-sweepingbay ornshay anday avagesay eyesay, oseray outay eirthay
yresbay, oneay ybay oneay, anday ollowedfay imhay, anday Owglimay ademay itay eryvay earclay otay
ethay ildrenchay ithway imhay atthay ehay asway ethay astermay. Ehay eatbay ethay uffaloesbay ithway
aay onglay, olishedpay amboobay, anday oldtay Amyakay, oneay ofay ethay oysbay, otay azegray ethay
attlecay ybay emselvesthay, ilewhay ehay entway onay ithway ethay uffaloesbay, anday otay ebay
eryvay arefulcay otnay otay aystray awayay omfray ethay erdhay.

Anay Indianay azinggray oundgray isay allay ocksray anday ubscray anday ussockstay anday ittlelay
avinesray, amongay ichwhay ethay erdshay atterscay anday isappearday. Ethay uffaloesbay
enerallygay eepkay otay ethay oolspay anday uddymay acesplay, erewhay eythay ielay allowingway
oray askingbay inay ethay armway udmay orfay ourshay. Owglimay ovedray emthay onay otay ethay edgeay
ofay ethay ainplay erewhay ethay Aingungaway amecay outay ofay ethay ungle;jay enthay ehay oppeddray
omfray Ama’sray ecknay, ottedtray offay otay aay amboobay umpclay, anday oundfay Aygray Otherbray.
Ah,”“ay aidsay Aygray Otherbray, I“ay avehay aitedway erehay eryvay anymay aysday. Atwhay isay ethay
eaningmay ofay isthay attle-herdingcay ork?”way

It“ay isay anay order,”ay aidsay Owglimay. I“ay amay aay illagevay erdhay orfay aay ilewhay. Atwhay
ewsnay ofay Ereshay An?”khay

e“Hay ashay omecay ackbay otay isthay ountrycay, anday ashay aitedway erehay aay onglay imetay orfay
eethay. Ownay ehay ashay onegay offay againay, orfay ethay amegay isay arcescay. Utbay ehay eansmay otay
illkay ee.”thay

ery“Vay ood,”gay aidsay Owglimay. o“Say onglay asay ehay isay awayay oday outhay oray oneay ofay ethay
ourfay othersbray itsay onay atthay ockray, osay atthay Iay ancay eesay eethay asay Iay omecay outay ofay
ethay illagevay. Enwhay ehay omescay ackbay aitway orfay emay inay ethay avineray ybay ethay _dhâk_ay
eetray inay ethay entercay ofay ethay ainplay. Eway eednay otnay alkway intoay Ereshay An’skhay
outh.”may

Enthay Owglimay ickedpay outay aay adyshay aceplay, anday aylay ownday anday eptslay ilewhay
ethay uffaloesbay azedgray oundray imhay. Erdinghay inay Indiaay isay oneay ofay ethay aziestlay
ingsthay inay ethay orldway. Ethay attlecay ovemay anday unchcray, anday ielay ownday, anday ovemay
onay againay, anday eythay oday otnay evenay owlay. Eythay onlyay untgray, anday ethay uffaloesbay
eryvay eldomsay aysay anythingay, utbay etgay ownday intoay ethay uddymay oolspay oneay afteray
anotheray, anday orkway eirthay ayway intoay ethay udmay illtay onlyay eirthay osesnay anday
aringstay ina-bluechay eyesay owshay aboveay ethay urfacesay, anday enthay eythay ielay ikelay
ogslay. Ethay unsay akesmay ethay ocksray anceday inay ethay eathay, anday ethay erdhay ildrenchay
earhay oneay itekay ever(nay anyay oremay) istlingwhay almostay outay ofay ightsay overheaday,
anday eythay owknay atthay ifay eythay iedday, oray aay owcay iedday, atthay itekay ouldway eepsway
ownday, anday ethay extnay itekay ilesmay awayay ouldway eesay imhay opdray anday ollowfay, anday
ethay extnay, anday ethay extnay, anday almostay eforebay eythay ereway eadday erethay ouldway ebay
aay orescay ofay ungryhay iteskay omecay outay ofay owherenay. Enthay eythay eepslay anday
akeway anday eepslay againay, anday eaveway ittlelay asketsbay ofay ieddray assgray anday utpay
asshoppersgray inay em;thay oray atchcay otway ayingpray antisesmay anday akemay emthay ight;fay
oray ingstray aay ecklacenay ofay edray anday ackblay unglejay uts;nay oray atchway aay izardlay
askingbay onay aay ockray, oray aay akesnay untinghay aay ogfray earnay ethay allowsway. Enthay eythay
ingsay onglay, onglay ongssay ithway odday ativenay uaversqay atay ethay enday ofay emthay, anday
ethay ayday eemssay ongerlay anthay ostmay eople’spay olewhay iveslay, anday erhapspay eythay
akemay aay udmay astlecay ithway udmay iguresfay ofay enmay anday orseshay anday uffaloesbay, anday
utpay eedsray intoay ethay en’smay andshay, anday etendpray atthay eythay areay ingskay anday ethay
iguresfay areay eirthay armiesay, oray atthay eythay areay odsgay otay ebay orshipedway. Enthay
eveningay omescay anday ethay ildrenchay allcay, anday ethay uffaloesbay umberlay upay outay ofay
ethay ickystay udmay ithway oisesnay ikelay unshotsgay oinggay offay oneay afteray ethay otheray,
anday eythay allay ingstray acrossay ethay aygray ainplay ackbay otay ethay inklingtway illagevay
ightslay.

Ayday afteray ayday Owglimay ouldway eadlay ethay uffaloesbay outay otay eirthay allowsway, anday
ayday afteray ayday ehay ouldway eesay Aygray Other’sbray ackbay aay ilemay anday aay alfhay awayay
acrossay ethay ainplay o(say ehay ewknay atthay Ereshay Ankhay adhay otnay omecay ack)bay, anday ayday
afteray ayday ehay ouldway ielay onay ethay assgray isteninglay otay ethay oisesnay oundray imhay,
anday eamingdray ofay olday aysday inay ethay unglejay. Ifay Ereshay Ankhay adhay ademay aay alsefay
epstay ithway ishay amelay awpay upay inay ethay unglesjay ybay ethay Aingungaway, Owglimay ouldway
avehay eardhay imhay inay osethay onglay, illstay orningsmay.

Atay astlay aay ayday amecay enwhay ehay idday otnay eesay Aygray Otherbray atay ethay ignalsay aceplay,
anday ehay aughedlay anday eadedhay ethay uffaloesbay orfay ethay avineray ybay ethay dhkay eetray,
ichwhay asway allay overedcay ithway olden-redgay owersflay. Erethay atsay Aygray Otherbray,
everyay istlebray onay ishay ackbay iftedlay.

e“Hay ashay iddenhay orfay aay onthmay otay owthray eethay offay ythay uardgay. Ehay ossedcray ethay
angesray astlay ightnay ithway Abaquitay, ot-foothay onay ythay ail,”tray aidsay ethay Olfway,
antingpay.

Owglimay ownedfray. I“ay amay otnay afraiday ofay Ereshay Ankhay, utbay Abaquitay isay eryvay
unning.”cay

ave“Hay onay ear,”fay aidsay Aygray Otherbray, ickinglay ishay ipslay aay ittlelay. I“ay etmay
Abaquitay inay ethay awnday. Ownay ehay isay ellingtay allay ishay isdomway otay ethay iteskay, utbay
ehay oldtay emay everythingay eforebay Iay okebray ishay ackbay. Ereshay An’skhay anplay isay otay
aitway orfay eethay atay ethay illagevay ategay isthay evening--foray eethay anday orfay onay oneay
elseay. Ehay isay yinglay upay ownay, inay ethay igbay ydray avineray ofay ethay Aingunga.”way

as“Hay ehay eatenay odaytay, oray oesday ehay unthay empty?”ay aidsay Owglimay, orfay ethay answeray
eantmay ifelay anday eathday otay imhay.

e“Hay illedkay atay awn,--aday ig,--andpay ehay ashay unkdray ootay. Ememberray, Ereshay Ankhay
ouldcay evernay astfay, evenay orfay ethay akesay ofay evenge.”ray

Oh“ay! Oolfay, oolfay! Atwhay aay ub’scay ubcay itay isay! Eatenay anday unkdray ootay, anday ehay
inksthay atthay Iay allshay aitway illtay ehay ashay eptslay! Ownay, erewhay oesday ehay ielay upay?
Ifay erethay ereway utbay entay ofay usay eway ightmay ullpay imhay ownday asay ehay ieslay. Esethay
uffaloesbay illway otnay argechay unlessay eythay indway imhay, anday Iay annotcay eakspay eirthay
anguagelay. Ancay eway etgay ehindbay ishay acktray osay atthay eythay aymay ellsmay it?”ay

e“Hay amsway arfay ownday ethay Aingungaway otay utcay atthay off,”ay aidsay Aygray Otherbray.

abaqui“Tay oldtay imhay atthay, Iay owknay. Ehay ouldway evernay avehay oughtthay ofay itay
alone.”ay Owglimay oodstay ithway ishay ingerfay inay ishay outhmay, inkingthay. e“Thay igbay
avineray ofay ethay Aingungaway. Atthay opensay outay onay ethay ainplay otnay alfhay aay ilemay
omfray erehay. Iay ancay aketay ethay erdhay oundray oughthray ethay unglejay otay ethay eadhay ofay
ethay avineray anday enthay eepsway own--butday ehay ouldway inkslay outay atay ethay ootfay. Eway
ustmay ockblay atthay enday. Aygray Otherbray, anstcay outhay utcay ethay erdhay inay otway orfay
e?”may

ot“Nay Iay, erhaps--butpay Iay avehay oughtbray aay iseway elper.”hay Aygray Otherbray ottedtray
offay anday oppeddray intoay aay olehay. Enthay erethay iftedlay upay aay ugehay aygray eadhay atthay
Owglimay ewknay ellway, anday ethay othay airay asway illedfay ithway ethay ostmay esolateday ycray
ofay allay ethay ungle--thejay untinghay owlhay ofay aay olfway atay iddaymay.

Akela“ay! Akela!”ay aidsay Owglimay, appingclay ishay andshay. I“ay ightmay avehay ownknay
atthay outhay ouldstway otnay orgetfay emay. Eway avehay aay igbay orkway inay andhay. Utcay ethay
erdhay inay otway, Akelaay. Eepkay ethay owscay anday alvescay ogethertay, anday ethay ullsbay anday
ethay owplay uffaloesbay ybay emselves.”thay

Ethay otway olvesway anray, adies’-chainlay ashionfay, inay anday outay ofay ethay erdhay, ichwhay
ortedsnay anday ewthray upay itsay eadhay, anday eparatedsay intoay otway umpsclay. Inay oneay,
ethay ow-buffaloescay oodstay ithway eirthay alvescay inay ethay entercay, anday aredglay
anday awedpay, eadyray, ifay aay olfway ouldway onlyay aystay illstay, otay argechay ownday anday
ampletray ethay ifelay outay ofay imhay. Inay ethay otheray, ethay ullsbay anday ethay youngay ullsbay
ortedsnay anday ampedstay, utbay oughthay eythay ookedlay oremay imposingay eythay ereway uchmay
esslay angerousday, orfay eythay adhay onay alvescay otay otectpray. Onay ixsay enmay ouldcay avehay
ividedday ethay erdhay osay eatlynay.

at“Whay orders!”ay antedpay Akelaay. ey“Thay areay yingtray otay oinjay again.”ay

Owglimay ippedslay onay otay Ama’sray ackbay. ive“Dray ethay ullsbay awayay otay ethay eftlay,
Akelaay. Aygray Otherbray, enwhay eway areay onegay, oldhay ethay owscay ogethertay, anday ivedray
emthay intoay ethay ootfay ofay ethay avine.”ray

ow“Hay ar?”fay aidsay Aygray Otherbray, antingpay anday appingsnay.

ill“Tay ethay idessay areay igherhay anthay Ereshay Ankhay ancay ump,”jay outedshay Owglimay.
eep“Kay emthay erethay illtay eway omecay own.”day Ethay ullsbay eptsway offay asay Akelaay ayedbay,
anday Aygray Otherbray oppedstay inay ontfray ofay ethay owscay. Eythay argedchay ownday onay imhay,
anday ehay anray ustjay eforebay emthay otay ethay ootfay ofay ethay avineray, asay Akelaay ovedray
ethay ullsbay arfay otay ethay eftlay.

ell“Way oneday! Anotheray argechay anday eythay areay airlyfay artedstay. Arefulcay,
ow--carefulnay, Akelaay. Aay apsnay ootay uchmay anday ethay ullsbay illway argechay. Ujahhay!
Isthay isay ilderway orkway anthay ivingdray ack-buckblay. Idstday outhay inkthay esethay
eaturescray ouldcay ovemay osay iftly?”sway Owglimay alledcay.

I“ay ave--havehay untedhay esethay ootay inay ymay ime,”tay aspedgay Akelaay inay ethay ustday.
all“Shay Iay urntay emthay intoay ethay ungle?”jay

Ay“ay! Urntay. Iftlysway urntay emthay! Amaray isay admay ithway ageray. Ohay, ifay Iay ouldcay onlyay
elltay imhay atwhay Iay eednay ofay imhay o-day.”tay

Ethay ullsbay ereway urnedtay, otay ethay ightray isthay imetay, anday ashedcray intoay ethay
andingstay icketthay. Ethay otheray erdhay ildrenchay, atchingway ithway ethay attlecay alfhay
aay ilemay awayay, urriedhay otay ethay illagevay asay astfay asay eirthay egslay ouldcay arrycay
emthay, yingcray atthay ethay uffaloesbay adhay onegay admay anday unray awayay.

Utbay Owgli’smay anplay asway implesay enoughay. Allay ehay antedway otay oday asway otay akemay aay
igbay irclecay uphillay anday etgay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay avineray, anday enthay aketay ethay
ullsbay ownday itay anday atchcay Ereshay Ankhay etweenbay ethay ullsbay anday ethay ows;cay orfay
ehay ewknay atthay afteray aay ealmay anday aay ullfay inkdray Ereshay Ankhay ouldway otnay ebay inay
anyay onditioncay otay ightfay oray otay amberclay upay ethay idessay ofay ethay avineray. Ehay asway
oothingsay ethay uffaloesbay ownay ybay oicevay, anday Akelaay adhay oppeddray arfay otay ethay
earray, onlyay imperingwhay onceay oray icetway otay urryhay ethay ear-guardray. Itay asway aay
onglay, onglay irclecay, orfay eythay idday otnay ishway otay etgay ootay earnay ethay avineray anday
ivegay Ereshay Ankhay arningway. Atay astlay Owglimay oundedray upay ethay ewilderedbay erdhay
atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay avineray onay aay assygray atchpay atthay opedslay eeplystay ownday otay
ethay avineray itselfay. Omfray atthay eighthay youay ouldcay eesay acrossay ethay opstay ofay ethay
eestray ownday otay ethay ainplay elow;bay utbay atwhay Owglimay ookedlay atay asway ethay idessay
ofay ethay avineray, anday ehay awsay ithway aay eatgray ealday ofay atisfactionsay atthay eythay
anray earlynay aightstray upay anday ownday, ilewhay ethay inesvay anday eeperscray atthay unghay
overay emthay ouldway ivegay onay ootholdfay otay aay igertay owhay antedway otay etgay outay.

et“Lay emthay eathebray, Akela,”ay ehay aidsay, oldinghay upay ishay andhay. ey“Thay avehay otnay
indedway imhay yetay. Etlay emthay eathebray. Iay ustmay elltay Ereshay Ankhay owhay omescay. Eway
avehay imhay inay ethay ap.”tray

Ehay utpay ishay andshay otay ishay outhmay anday outedshay ownday ethay avine--itray asway almostay
ikelay outingshay ownday aay unnel--andtay ethay echoesay umpedjay omfray ockray otay ockray.

Afteray aay onglay imetay erethay amecay ackbay ethay awlingdray, eepyslay arlsnay ofay aay
ull-fedfay igertay ustjay akenedway.

o“Whay alls?”cay aidsay Ereshay Ankhay, anday aay endidsplay eacockpay utteredflay upay outay ofay
ethay avineray eechingscray.

I“ay, Owglimay. Attlecay iefthay, itay isay imetay otay omecay otay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray!
Own--hurryday emthay ownday, Akelaay! Ownday, Amaray, own!”day

Ethay erdhay ausedpay orfay anay instantay atay ethay edgeay ofay ethay opeslay, utbay Akelaay avegay
onguetay inay ethay ullfay unting-yellhay, anday eythay itchedpay overay oneay afteray ethay
otheray, ustjay asay eamersstay ootshay apidsray, ethay andsay anday onesstay urtingspay upay
oundray emthay. Onceay artedstay, erethay asway onay ancechay ofay oppingstay, anday eforebay
eythay ereway airlyfay inay ethay edbay ofay ethay avineray Amaray indedway Ereshay Ankhay anday
ellowedbay.

a“Hay! A!”hay aidsay Owglimay, onay ishay ackbay. ow“Nay outhay owest!”knay anday ethay orrenttay
ofay ackblay ornshay, oamingfay uzzlesmay, anday aringstay eyesay irledwhay ownday ethay
avineray ustjay asay ouldersbay ogay ownday inay oodtime;flay ethay eakerway uffaloesbay eingbay
oulderedshay outay otay ethay idessay ofay ethay avineray erewhay eythay oretay oughthray ethay
eeperscray. Eythay ewknay atwhay ethay usinessbay asway eforebay em--thethay erribletay
argechay ofay ethay uffalobay erdhay againstay ichwhay onay igertay ancay opehay otay andstay.
Ereshay Ankhay eardhay ethay underthay ofay eirthay oofshay, ickedpay imselfhay upay, anday
umberedlay ownday ethay avineray, ookinglay omfray idesay otay idesay orfay omesay ayway ofay
escapeay, utbay ethay allsway ofay ethay avineray ereway aightstray anday ehay adhay otay oldhay onay,
eavyhay ithway ishay innerday anday ishay inkdray, illingway otay oday anythingay atherray anthay
ightfay. Ethay erdhay ashedsplay oughthray ethay oolpay ehay adhay ustjay eftlay, ellowingbay
illtay ethay arrownay utcay angray. Owglimay eardhay anay answeringay ellowbay omfray ethay ootfay
ofay ethay avineray, awsay Ereshay Ankhay urntay e(thay igertay ewknay ifay ethay orstway amecay
otay ethay orstway itay asway etterbay otay eetmay ethay ullsbay anthay ethay owscay ithway eirthay
alves)cay, anday enthay Amaray ippedtray, umbledstay, anday entway onay againay overay
omethingsay oftsay, anday, ithway ethay ullsbay atay ishay eelshay, ashedcray ullfay intoay ethay
otheray erdhay, ilewhay ethay eakerway uffaloesbay ereway iftedlay eanclay offay eirthay eetfay
ybay ethay ockshay ofay ethay eetingmay. Atthay argechay arriedcay othbay erdshay outay intoay ethay
ainplay, oringgay anday ampingstay anday ortingsnay. Owglimay atchedway ishay imetay, anday
ippedslay offay Ama’sray ecknay, ayinglay aboutay imhay ightray anday eftlay ithway ishay ickstay.

uick“Qay, Akelaay! Eakbray emthay upay. Atterscay emthay, oray eythay illway ebay ightingfay oneay
anotheray. Ivedray emthay awayay, Akelaay. Aihay, Amaray! Aihay, aihay, aihay! ymay ildrenchay.
Oftlysay ownay, oftlysay! Itay isay allay over.”ay

Akelaay anday Aygray Otherbray anray otay anday ofray ippingnay ethay uffaloes’bay egslay,
anday oughthay ethay erdhay eeledwhay onceay otay argechay upay ethay avineray againay, Owglimay
anagedmay otay urntay Amaray, anday ethay othersay ollowedfay imhay otay ethay allowsway.

Ereshay Ankhay eedednay onay oremay amplingtray. Ehay asway eadday, anday ethay iteskay ereway
omingcay orfay imhay alreadyay.

others“Bray, atthay asway aay og’sday eath,”day aidsay Owglimay, eelingfay orfay ethay ifeknay
ehay alwaysay arriedcay inay aay eathshay oundray ishay ecknay ownay atthay ehay ivedlay ithway enmay.
ut“Bay ehay ouldway evernay avehay ownshay ightfay. Ishay idehay illway ooklay ellway onay ethay
Ouncilcay Ockray. Eway ustmay etgay otay orkway iftly.”sway

Aay oybay ainedtray amongay enmay ouldway evernay avehay eameddray ofay inningskay aay en-foottay
igertay aloneay, utbay Owglimay ewknay etterbay anthay anyoneay elseay owhay anay animal’say
inskay isay ittedfay onay, anday owhay itay ancay ebay akentay offay. Utbay itay asway ardhay orkway,
anday Owglimay ashedslay anday oretay anday untedgray orfay anay ourhay, ilewhay ethay olvesway
olledlay outay eirthay onguestay, oray amecay orwardfay anday uggedtay asay ehay ordereday emthay.
Esentlypray aay andhay ellfay onay ishay ouldershay, anday ookinglay upay ehay awsay Uldeobay ithway
ethay Owertay usketmay. Ethay ildrenchay adhay oldtay ethay illagevay aboutay ethay uffalobay
ampedestay, anday Uldeobay entway outay angrilyay, onlyay ootay anxiousay otay orrectcay
Owglimay orfay otnay akingtay etterbay arecay ofay ethay erdhay. Ethay olvesway oppeddray outay ofay
ightsay asay oonsay asay eythay awsay ethay anmay omingcay.

at“Whay isay isthay olly?”fay aidsay Uldeobay angrilyay. o“Tay inkthay atthay outhay anstcay
inskay aay igertay! Erewhay idday ethay uffaloesbay illkay imhay? Itay isay ethay Amelay Igertay
ootay, anday erethay isay aay undredhay upeesray onay ishay eadhay. Ellway, ellway, eway illway
overlookay ythay ettinglay ethay erdhay unray offay, anday erhapspay Iay illway ivegay eethay oneay
ofay ethay upeesray ofay ethay ewardray enwhay Iay avehay akentay ethay inskay otay Anhiwara.”khay
Ehay umbledfay inay ishay aistway othclay orfay intflay anday eelstay, anday oopedstay ownday otay
ingesay Ereshay An’skhay iskerswhay. Ostmay ativenay untershay alwaysay ingesay aay iger’stay
iskerswhay otay eventpray ishay ostghay omfray auntinghay emthay.

um!”“Hay aidsay Owglimay, alfhay otay imselfhay asay ehay ippedray ackbay ethay inskay ofay aay

ymay ownay useay. Ehhay! Olday anmay, aketay awayay atthay ire!”fay

at“Whay alktay isay isthay otay ethay iefchay unterhay ofay ethay illagevay? Ythay ucklay anday ethay
upiditystay ofay ythay uffaloesbay avehay elpedhay eethay otay isthay illkay. Ethay igertay ashay
ustjay edfay, oray ehay ouldway avehay onegay entytway ilesmay ybay isthay imetay. Outhay anstcay
otnay evenay inskay imhay operlypray, ittlelay eggarbay atbray, anday orsoothfay Iay, Uldeobay,
ustmay ebay oldtay otnay otay ingesay ishay iskerswhay. Owglimay, Iay illway otnay ivegay eethay oneay
annaay ofay ethay ewardray, utbay onlyay aay eryvay igbay eatingbay. Eavelay ethay arcass!”cay

y“Bay ethay Ullbay atthay oughtbay e,”may aidsay Owglimay, owhay asway yingtray otay etgay atay ethay

isthay anmay aguesplay e.”may

awlingspray onay ethay assgray, ithway aay aygray olfway andingstay overay imhay, ilewhay Owglimay
entway onay inningskay asay oughthay ehay ereway aloneay inay allay Indiaay.

Ye-es,”“ay ehay aidsay, etweenbay ishay eethtay. ou“Thay artay altogetheray ightray, Uldeobay.
Outhay iltway evernay ivegay emay oneay annaay ofay ethay ewardray. Erethay isay anay olday arway
etweenbay isthay amelay igertay anday yself--amay eryvay olday arway, and--Iay avehay on.”way

Otay oday Uldeobay usticejay, ifay ehay adhay eenbay entay yearsay youngeray ehay ouldway avehay
akentay ishay ancechay ithway Akelaay adhay ehay etmay ethay olfway inay ethay oodsway, utbay aay olfway

igerstay asway otnay aay ommoncay animalay. Itay asway orcerysay, agicmay ofay ethay orstway indkay,
oughtthay Uldeobay, anday ehay onderedway etherwhay ethay amuletay oundray ishay ecknay ouldway
otectpray imhay. Ehay aylay asay illstay asay illstay, expectingay everyay inutemay otay eesay
Owglimay urntay intoay aay igertay ootay.

Ehay urnedtay onay ishay eelhay anday alkedway awayay ithway ethay Onelay Olfway, anday asay ehay

Akelaay oodstay upay onay ishay indhay egslay anday alkedtay ikelay aay anmay.

Ethay oonmay asway ustjay oinggay ownday enwhay Owglimay anday ethay otway olvesway amecay otay ethay
illhay ofay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, anday eythay oppedstay atay Othermay Olf’sway avecay.

ey“Thay avehay astcay emay outay omfray ethay An-Packmay, Other,”may outedshay Owglimay, ut“bay
Iay omecay ithway ethay idehay ofay Ereshay Ankhay otay eepkay ymay ord.”way

Othermay Olfway alkedway ifflystay omfray ethay avecay ithway ethay ubscay ehindbay erhay, anday
erhay eyesay owedglay asay eshay awsay ethay inskay.

I“ay oldtay imhay onay atthay ayday, enwhay ehay ammedcray ishay eadhay anday ouldersshay intoay

ouldway ebay ethay untedhay. Itay isay ellway one.”day

ittle“Lay Otherbray, itay isay ellway one,”day aidsay aay eepday oicevay inay ethay icketthay.
e“Way ereway onelylay inay ethay unglejay ithoutway ee,”thay anday Agheerabay amecay unningray
otay Owgli’smay arebay eetfay. Eythay amberedclay upay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray ogethertay, anday
Owglimay eadspray ethay inskay outay onay ethay atflay onestay erewhay Akelaay useday otay itsay,
anday eggedpay itay ownday ithway ourfay iversslay ofay amboobay, anday Akelaay aylay ownday uponay
itay, anday alledcay ethay olday allcay otay ethay Ouncilcay, ook--look“Lay ellway, Oay Olves,”way
exactlyay asay ehay adhay alledcay enwhay Owglimay asway irstfay oughtbray erethay.

Everay incesay Akelaay adhay eenbay eposedday, ethay Ackpay adhay eenbay ithoutway aay eaderlay,
untinghay anday ightingfay atay eirthay ownay easureplay. Utbay eythay answereday ethay allcay
omfray abit;hay anday omesay ofay emthay ereway amelay omfray ethay apstray eythay adhay allenfay
intoay, anday omesay impedlay omfray otshay oundsway, anday omesay ereway angymay omfray eatingay
adbay oodfay, anday anymay ereway issingmay. Utbay eythay amecay otay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray, allay
atthay ereway eftlay ofay emthay, anday awsay Ereshay An’skhay ipedstray idehay onay ethay ockray,
anday ethay ugehay awsclay anglingday atay ethay enday ofay ethay emptyay anglingday eetfay. Itay
asway enthay atthay Owglimay ademay upay aay ongsay atthay amecay upay intoay ishay oatthray allay
ybay itselfay, anday ehay outedshay itay alouday, eapinglay upay anday ownday onay ethay attlingray
inskay, anday eatingbay imetay ithway ishay eelshay illtay ehay adhay onay oremay eathbray eftlay,
ilewhay Aygray Otherbray anday Akelaay owledhay etweenbay ethay ersesvay.

ook“Lay ellway, Oay Olvesway. Avehay Iay eptkay ymay ord?”way aidsay Owglimay. Anday ethay olvesway
ayedbay Yes,”“ay anday oneay atteredtay olfway owled:hay

an-Pack“May anday Olf-Packway avehay astcay emay out,”ay aidsay Owglimay. ow“Nay Iay illway unthay

And“ay eway illway unthay ithway ee,”thay aidsay ethay ourfay ubscay.

Osay Owglimay entway awayay anday untedhay ithway ethay ourfay ubscay inay ethay unglejay omfray
atthay ayday onay. Utbay ehay asway otnay alwaysay aloneay, ecausebay, yearsay afterwarday, ehay
ecamebay aay anmay anday arriedmay.

Utbay atthay isay aay orystay orfay own-upsgray.




Owgli’smay Ongsay

ATtHay Ehay ANGsay ATay EtHay OUNCILcay OCKray ENwHay Ehay
ANCEDday ONay EREsHay AN’SkHay IDEhay

Ethay Ongsay ofay Owgli—Imay, Owglimay, amay ingingsay. Etlay ethay unglejay istenlay otay ethay
ingsthay Iay avehay oneday.
Ereshay Ankhay aidsay ehay ouldway ill—wouldkay illkay! Atay ethay atesgay inay ethay ilighttway
ehay ouldway illkay Owglimay, ethay Ogfray!
Ehay ateay anday ehay ankdray. Inkdray eepday, Ereshay Ankhay, orfay enwhay iltway outhay inkdray
againay? Eepslay anday eamdray ofay ethay illkay.
Iay amay aloneay onay ethay azing-groundsgray. Aygray Otherbray, omecay otay emay! Omecay otay
emay, Onelay Olfway, orfay erethay isay igbay amegay afootay!
Ingbray upay ethay eatgray ullbay uffaloesbay, ethay ue-skinnedblay erdhay ullsbay ithway ethay
angryay eyesay. Ivedray emthay otay anday ofray asay Iay orderay.
Eepestslay outhay illstay, Ereshay Ankhay? Akeway, ohay, akeway! Erehay omecay Iay, anday ethay
ullsbay areay ehindbay.
Amaray, ethay Ingkay ofay ethay Uffaloesbay, ampedstay ithway ishay ootfay. Atersway ofay ethay
Aingungaway, itherwhay entway Ereshay Ankhay?
Ehay isay otnay Ikkiay otay igday oleshay, ornay Aomay, ethay Eacockpay, atthay ehay ouldshay yflay.
Ehay isay otnay Angmay ethay Atbay, otay anghay inay ethay anchesbray. Ittlelay amboosbay atthay
eakcray ogethertay, elltay emay erewhay ehay anray?
Ow!__ay Ehay isay erethay. Ahoo!__ay Ehay isay erethay. Underay ethay eetfay ofay Amaray ieslay ethay
Amelay Oneay! Upay, Ereshay Ankhay!
Upay anday illkay! Erehay isay eat;may eakbray ethay ecksnay ofay ethay ullsbay!
_Hsh!_ay Ehay isay asleepay. Eway illway otnay akeway imhay, orfay ishay engthstray isay eryvay
eatgray. Ethay iteskay avehay omecay ownday otay eesay itay. Ethay ackblay antsay avehay omecay upay
otay owknay itay. Erethay isay aay eatgray assemblyay inay ishay onorhay.
Alala!__ay Iay avehay onay othclay otay apwray emay. Ethay iteskay illway eesay atthay Iay amay
akednay. Iay amay ashameday otay eetmay allay esethay eoplepay.
Endlay emay ythay oatcay, Ereshay Ankhay. Endlay emay ythay aygay ipedstray oatcay atthay Iay aymay
ogay otay ethay Ouncilcay Ockray.
Ybay ethay Ullbay atthay oughtbay emay Iay ademay aay omise—apray ittlelay omisepray. Onlyay ythay
oatcay isay ackinglay eforebay Iay eepkay ymay ordway.
Ithway ethay ifeknay, ithway ethay ifeknay atthay enmay useay, ithway ethay ifeknay ofay ethay
unterhay, Iay illway oopstay ownday orfay ymay iftgay.
Atersway ofay ethay Aingungaway, Ereshay Ankhay ivesgay emay ishay oatcay orfay ethay ovelay atthay
ehay earsbay emay. Ullpay, Aygray Otherbray! Ullpay, Akelaay! Eavyhay isay ethay idehay ofay
Ereshay Ankhay.
Ethay Anmay Ackpay areay angryay. Eythay owthray onesstay anday alktay ild’schay alktay. Ymay
outhmay isay eedingblay. Etlay emay unray awayay.
Oughthray ethay ightnay, oughthray ethay othay ightnay, unray iftlysway ithway emay, ymay
othersbray. Eway illway eavelay ethay ightslay ofay ethay illagevay anday ogay otay ethay owlay
oonmay.
Atersway ofay ethay Aingungaway, ethay An-Packmay avehay astcay emay outay. Iay idday emthay onay
armhay, utbay eythay ereway afraiday ofay emay. Ywhay?
Olfway Ackpay, yeay avehay astcay emay outay ootay. Ethay unglejay isay utshay otay emay anday ethay
illagevay atesgay areay utshay. Ywhay?
Asay Angmay iesflay etweenbay ethay eastsbay anday irdsbay, osay yflay Iay etweenbay ethay
illagevay anday ethay unglejay. Ywhay?
Iay anceday onay ethay idehay ofay Ereshay Ankhay, utbay ymay earthay isay eryvay eavyhay. Ymay outhmay
isay utcay anday oundedway ithway ethay onesstay omfray ethay illagevay, utbay ymay earthay isay
eryvay ightlay, ecausebay Iay avehay omecay ackbay otay ethay unglejay. Ywhay?
Esethay otway ingsthay ightfay ogethertay inay emay asay ethay akessnay ightfay inay ethay
ingspray. Ethay aterway omescay outay ofay ymay eyes;ay yetay Iay aughlay ilewhay itay allsfay.
Ywhay?
Iay amay otway Owglismay, utbay ethay idehay ofay Ereshay Ankhay isay underay ymay eetfay.
Allay ethay unglejay owsknay atthay Iay avehay illedkay Ereshay Ankhay. Ook—looklay ellway, Oay
Olvesway!
Ahae!__ay Ymay earthay isay eavyhay ithway ethay ingsthay atthay Iay oday otnay understanday.




Ethay Itewhay Ealsay

Ohay! ushhay eethay, ymay abybay, ethay ightnay isay ehindbay usay,
Anday ackblay areay ethay atersway atthay arkledspay osay eengray.
Ethay oonmay, o’eray ethay omberscay, ookslay ownwardday otay indfay usay
Atay estray inay ethay ollowshay atthay ustleray etweenbay.
Erewhay illowbay eetsmay illowbay, enthay oftsay ebay ythay illowpay,
Ahay, earyway eeway ipperlingflay, urlcay atay ythay easeay!
Ethay ormstay allshay otnay akeway eethay, ornay arkshay overtakeay eethay,
Asleepay inay ethay armsay ofay ethay ow-swingingslay eassay!

Ealsay Ullabylay


Allay esethay ingsthay appenedhay everalsay yearsay agoay atay aay aceplay alledcay
Ovastoshnahnay, oray Orthnay Eastay Ointpay, onay ethay Islanday ofay Stay. Aulpay, awayay anday
awayay inay ethay Eringbay Easay. Immershinlay, ethay Interway Enwray, oldtay emay ethay aletay
enwhay ehay asway ownblay onay otay ethay iggingray ofay aay eamerstay oinggay otay Apanjay, anday Iay
ooktay imhay ownday intoay ymay abincay anday armedway anday edfay imhay orfay aay ouplecay ofay aysday
illtay ehay asway itfay otay yflay ackbay otay Stay. Aul’spay againay. Immershinlay isay aay eryvay
uaintqay ittlelay irdbay, utbay ehay owsknay owhay otay elltay ethay uthtray.

Obodynay omescay otay Ovastoshnahnay exceptay onay usinessbay, anday ethay onlyay eoplepay
owhay avehay egularray usinessbay erethay areay ethay ealssay. Eythay omecay inay ethay ummersay
onthsmay ybay undredshay anday undredshay ofay ousandsthay outay ofay ethay oldcay aygray easay.
Orfay Ovastoshnahnay Eachbay ashay ethay inestfay accommodationay orfay ealssay ofay anyay
aceplay inay allay ethay orldway.

Easay Atchcay ewknay atthay, anday everyay ingspray ouldway imsway omfray ateverwhay aceplay
ehay appenedhay otay ebay in--woulday imsway ikelay aay orpedo-boattay aightstray orfay
Ovastoshnahnay anday endspay aay onthmay ightingfay ithway ishay ompanionscay orfay aay oodgay
aceplay onay ethay ocksray, asay oseclay otay ethay easay asay ossiblepay. Easay Atchcay asway
ifteenfay yearsay olday, aay ugehay aygray urfay ealsay ithway almostay aay anemay onay ishay
ouldersshay, anday onglay, ickedway ogday eethtay. Enwhay ehay eavedhay imselfhay upay onay ishay
ontfray ippersflay ehay oodstay oremay anthay ourfay eetfay earclay ofay ethay oundgray, anday ishay
eightway, ifay anyoneay adhay eenbay oldbay enoughay otay eighway imhay, asway earlynay evensay
undredhay oundspay. Ehay asway arredscay allay overay ithway ethay arksmay ofay avagesay ightsfay,
utbay ehay asway alwaysay eadyray orfay ustjay oneay ightfay oremay. Ehay ouldway utpay ishay eadhay
onay oneay idesay, asay oughthay ehay ereway afraiday otay ooklay ishay enemyay inay ethay ace;fay
enthay ehay ouldway ootshay itay outay ikelay ightninglay, anday enwhay ethay igbay eethtay ereway
irmlyfay ixedfay onay ethay otheray eal’ssay ecknay, ethay otheray ealsay ightmay etgay awayay ifay
ehay ouldcay, utbay Easay Atchcay ouldway otnay elphay imhay.

Yetay Easay Atchcay evernay asedchay aay eatenbay ealsay, orfay atthay asway againstay ethay Ulesray
ofay ethay Eachbay. Ehay onlyay antedway oomray ybay ethay easay orfay ishay urserynay. Utbay asay
erethay ereway ortyfay oray iftyfay ousandthay otheray ealssay untinghay orfay ethay amesay
ingthay eachay ingspray, ethay istlingwhay, ellowingbay, oaringray, anday owingblay onay ethay
eachbay asway omethingsay ightfulfray.

Omfray aay ittlelay illhay alledcay Utchinson’shay Illhay, youay ouldcay ooklay overay eethray
anday aay alfhay ilesmay ofay oundgray overedcay ithway ightingfay eals;say anday ethay urfsay asway
ottedday allay overay ithway ethay eadshay ofay ealssay urryinghay otay andlay anday eginbay eirthay
areshay ofay ethay ightingfay. Eythay oughtfay inay ethay eakersbray, eythay oughtfay inay ethay
andsay, anday eythay oughtfay onay ethay ooth-wornsmay asaltbay ocksray ofay ethay urseriesnay,
orfay eythay ereway ustjay asay upidstay anday unaccommodatingay asay enmay. Eirthay ivesway
evernay amecay otay ethay islanday untilay atelay inay Aymay oray earlyay inay Unejay, orfay eythay
idday otnay arecay otay ebay orntay otay ieces;pay anday ethay youngay o-tway, ee-thray, anday
our-year-oldfay ealssay owhay adhay otnay egunbay ousekeepinghay entway inlanday aboutay
alfhay aay ilemay oughthray ethay anksray ofay ethay ightersfay anday ayedplay aboutay onay ethay
andsay unesday inay ovesdray anday egionslay, anday ubbedray offay everyay inglesay eengray
ingthay atthay ewgray. Eythay ereway alledcay ethay olluschickie--thehay achelors--andbay
erethay ereway erhapspay otway oray eethray undredhay ousandthay ofay emthay atay Ovastoshnahnay
aloneay.

Easay Atchcay adhay ustjay inishedfay ishay orty-fifthfay ightfay oneay ingspray enwhay
Atkahmay, ishay oftsay, eekslay, entle-eyedgay ifeway, amecay upay outay ofay ethay easay,
anday ehay aughtcay erhay ybay ethay uffscray ofay ethay ecknay anday umpedday erhay ownday onay ishay
eservationray, ayingsay uffly:gray ate“Lay asay usualay. Erewhay avehay youay een?”bay

Itay asway otnay ethay ashionfay orfay Easay Atchcay otay eatay anythingay uringday ethay ourfay
onthsmay ehay ayedstay onay ethay eachesbay, anday osay ishay empertay asway enerallygay adbay.
Atkahmay ewknay etterbay anthay otay answeray ackbay. Eshay ookedlay oundray anday ooed:cay ow“Hay
oughtfulthay ofay youay. You’veay akentay ethay olday aceplay again.”ay

I“ay ouldshay inkthay Iay ad,”hay aidsay Easay Atchcay. ook“Lay atay e!”may

Ehay asway atchedscray anday eedingblay inay entytway aces;play oneay eyeay asway almostay outay,
anday ishay idessay ereway orntay otay ibbonsray.

Oh“ay, youay enmay, youay en!”may Atkahmay aidsay, anningfay erselfhay ithway erhay indhay
ipperflay. y“Whay an’tcay youay ebay ensiblesay anday ettlesay youray acesplay uietlyqay? Youay
ooklay asay oughthay youay adhay eenbay ightingfay ithway ethay Illerkay Ale.”whay

I“ay aven’thay eenbay oingday anythingay utbay ightfay incesay ethay iddlemay ofay Aymay. Ethay
eachbay isay isgracefullyday owdedcray isthay easonsay. I’veay etmay atay eastlay aay undredhay
ealssay omfray Ukannonlay Eachbay, ousehay untinghay. Ywhay an’tcay eoplepay aystay erewhay
eythay elong?”bay

I’ve“ay oftenay oughtthay eway ouldshay ebay uchmay appierhay ifay eway auledhay outay atay Otteray
Islanday insteaday ofay isthay owdedcray ace,”play aidsay Atkahmay.

ah“Bay! Onlyay ethay olluschickiehay ogay otay Otteray Islanday. Ifay eway entway erethay eythay
ouldway aysay eway ereway afraiday. Eway ustmay eservepray appearancesay, ymay ear.”day

Easay Atchcay unksay ishay eadhay oudlypray etweenbay ishay atfay ouldersshay anday etendedpray
otay ogay otay eepslay orfay aay ewfay inutesmay, utbay allay ethay imetay ehay asway eepingkay aay
arpshay ookoutlay orfay aay ightfay. Ownay atthay allay ethay ealssay anday eirthay ivesway ereway
onay ethay andlay, youay ouldcay earhay eirthay amorclay ilesmay outay otay easay aboveay ethay
oudestlay alesgay. Atay ethay owestlay ountingcay erethay ereway overay aay illionmay ealssay
onay ethay each--oldbay ealssay, othermay ealssay, inytay abiesbay, anday olluschickiehay,
ightingfay, ufflingscay, eatingblay, awlingcray, anday ayingplay ogether--goingtay
ownday otay ethay easay anday omingcay upay omfray itay inay angsgay anday egimentsray, yinglay
overay everyay ootfay ofay oundgray asay arfay asay ethay eyeay ouldcay eachray, anday irmishingskay
aboutay inay igadesbray oughthray ethay ogfay. Itay isay earlynay alwaysay oggyfay atay
Ovastoshnahnay, exceptay enwhay ethay unsay omescay outay anday akesmay everythingay ooklay
allay earlypay anday ainbow-coloredray orfay aay ittlelay ilewhay.

Otickkay, Atkah’smay abybay, asway ornbay inay ethay iddlemay ofay atthay onfusioncay, anday ehay
asway allay eadhay anday ouldersshay, ithway alepay, ateryway ueblay eyesay, asay inytay ealssay
ustmay ebay, utbay erethay asway omethingsay aboutay ishay oatcay atthay ademay ishay othermay
ooklay atay imhay eryvay oselyclay.

ea“Say Atch,”cay eshay aidsay, atay astlay, our“ay aby’sbay oinggay otay ebay ite!”whay

Empty“ay am-shellsclay anday ydray eaweed!”say ortedsnay Easay Atchcay. ere“Thay evernay ashay
eenbay uchsay aay ingthay inay ethay orldway asay aay itewhay eal.”say

I“ay an’tcay elphay at,”thay aidsay Atkah;may ere’s“thay oinggay otay ebay ow.”nay Anday eshay
angsay ethay owlay, ooningcray ealsay ongsay atthay allay ethay othermay ealssay ingsay otay eirthay
abies:bay

Youay ustn’tmay imsway illtay you’reay ixsay eeksway olday,
Oray youray eadhay illway ebay unksay ybay youray eels;hay

Areay adbay orfay abybay ealssay.
