Asay adbay asay adbay ancay e;bay
Utbay ashsplay anday owgray ongstray,
Anday youay an’tcay ebay ongwray.
Ildchay ofay ethay Openay Easay!

Ofay oursecay ethay ittlelay ellowfay idday otnay understanday ethay ordsway atay irstfay. Ehay
addledpay anday ambledscray aboutay ybay ishay other’smay idesay, anday earnedlay otay ufflescay
outay ofay ethay ayway enwhay ishay atherfay asway ightingfay ithway anotheray ealsay, anday ethay
otway olledray anday oaredray upay anday ownday ethay ipperyslay ocksray. Atkahmay useday otay ogay
otay easay otay etgay ingsthay otay eatay, anday ethay abybay asway edfay onlyay onceay inay otway aysday,
utbay enthay ehay ateay allay ehay ouldcay anday ovethray uponay itay.

Ethay irstfay ingthay ehay idday asway otay awlcray inlanday, anday erethay ehay etmay enstay
ofay ousandsthay ofay abiesbay ofay ishay ownay ageay, anday eythay ayedplay ogethertay ikelay
uppiespay, entway otay eepslay onay ethay eanclay andsay, anday ayedplay againay. Ethay olday
eoplepay inay ethay urseriesnay ooktay onay oticenay ofay emthay, anday ethay olluschickiehay
eptkay otay eirthay ownay oundsgray, anday ethay abiesbay adhay aay eautifulbay aytimeplay.

Enwhay Atkahmay amecay ackbay omfray erhay eep-seaday ishingfay eshay ouldway ogay aightstray
otay eirthay aygroundplay anday allcay asay aay eepshay allscay orfay aay amblay, anday aitway untilay
eshay eardhay Otickkay eatblay. Enthay eshay ouldway aketay ethay aighteststray ofay aightstray
ineslay inay ishay irectionday, ikingstray outay ithway erhay orefay ippersflay anday ockingknay
ethay youngstersay eadhay overay eelshay ightray anday eftlay. Erethay ereway alwaysay aay ewfay
undredhay othersmay untinghay orfay eirthay ildrenchay oughthray ethay aygroundsplay, anday
ethay abiesbay ereway eptkay ivelylay. Utbay, asay Atkahmay oldtay Otickkay, o“Say onglay asay youay
on’tday ielay inay uddymay aterway anday etgay angemay, oray ubray ethay ardhay andsay intoay aay utcay
oray atchscray, anday osay onglay asay youay evernay ogay immingsway enwhay erethay isay aay eavyhay
easay, othingnay illway urthay youay ere.”hay

Ittlelay ealssay ancay onay oremay imsway anthay ittlelay ildrenchay, utbay eythay areay unhappyay
illtay eythay earnlay. Ethay irstfay imetay atthay Otickkay entway ownday otay ethay easay aay aveway
arriedcay imhay outay eyondbay ishay epthday, anday ishay igbay eadhay anksay anday ishay ittlelay
indhay ippersflay ewflay upay exactlyay asay ishay othermay adhay oldtay imhay inay ethay ongsay,
anday ifay ethay extnay aveway adhay otnay ownthray imhay ackbay againay ehay ouldway avehay
owneddray.

Afteray atthay, ehay earnedlay otay ielay inay aay eachbay oolpay anday etlay ethay ashway ofay ethay
avesway ustjay overcay imhay anday iftlay imhay upay ilewhay ehay addledpay, utbay ehay alwaysay
eptkay ishay eyeay openay orfay igbay avesway atthay ightmay urthay. Ehay asway otway eeksway
earninglay otay useay ishay ippers;flay anday allay atthay ilewhay ehay ounderedflay inay anday
outay ofay ethay aterway, anday oughedcay anday untedgray anday awledcray upay ethay eachbay anday
ooktay atnapscay onay ethay andsay, anday entway ackbay againay, untilay atay astlay ehay oundfay
atthay ehay ulytray elongedbay otay ethay aterway.

Enthay youay ancay imagineay ethay imestay atthay ehay adhay ithway ishay ompanionscay, uckingday
underay ethay ollers;ray oray omingcay inay onay optay ofay aay ombercay anday andinglay ithway aay
ashsway anday aay uttersplay asay ethay igbay aveway entway irlingwhay arfay upay ethay each;bay oray
andingstay upay onay ishay ailtay anday atchingscray ishay eadhay asay ethay olday eoplepay id;day
oray ayingplay I’m“ay ethay Ingkay ofay ethay Astle”cay onay ipperyslay, eedyway ocksray atthay
ustjay uckstay outay ofay ethay ashway. Ownay anday enthay ehay ouldway eesay aay inthay infay, ikelay
aay igbay ark’sshay infay, iftingdray alongay oseclay otay oreshay, anday ehay ewknay atthay atthay
asway ethay Illerkay Alewhay, ethay Ampusgray, owhay eatsay youngay ealssay enwhay ehay ancay etgay
em;thay anday Otickkay ouldway eadhay orfay ethay eachbay ikelay anay arroway, anday ethay infay
ouldway igjay offay owlyslay, asay ifay itay ereway ookinglay orfay othingnay atay allay.

Atelay inay Octoberay ethay ealssay eganbay otay eavelay Stay. Aul’spay orfay ethay eepday easay, ybay
amiliesfay anday ibestray, anday erethay asway onay oremay ightingfay overay ethay urseriesnay,
anday ethay olluschickiehay ayedplay anywhereay eythay ikedlay. ext“Nay year,”ay aidsay
Atkahmay otay Otickkay, you“ay illway ebay aay olluschickie;hay utbay isthay yearay youay ustmay
earnlay owhay otay atchcay ish.”fay

Eythay etsay outay ogethertay acrossay ethay Acificpay, anday Atkahmay owedshay Otickkay owhay
otay eepslay onay ishay ackbay ithway ishay ippersflay uckedtay ownday ybay ishay idesay anday ishay
ittlelay osenay ustjay outay ofay ethay aterway. Onay adlecray isay osay omfortablecay asay ethay
onglay, ockingray ellsway ofay ethay Acificpay. Enwhay Otickkay eltfay ishay inskay ingletay allay
overay, Atkahmay oldtay imhay ehay asway earninglay ethay eel“fay ofay ethay ater,”way anday atthay
inglytay, icklypray eelingsfay eantmay adbay eatherway omingcay, anday ehay ustmay imsway ardhay
anday etgay awayay.

In“ay aay ittlelay ime,”tay eshay aidsay, you’ll“ay owknay erewhay otay imsway otay, utbay ustjay
ownay e’llway ollowfay Easay Igpay, ethay Orpoisepay, orfay ehay isay eryvay ise.”way Aay oolschay
ofay orpoisespay ereway uckingday anday earingtay oughthray ethay aterway, anday ittlelay
Otickkay ollowedfay emthay asay astfay asay ehay ouldcay. ow“Hay oday youay owknay erewhay otay ogay
o?”tay ehay antedpay. Ethay eaderlay ofay ethay oolschay olledray ishay itewhay eyeay anday uckedday
underay. y“May ailtay inglestay, youngster,”ay ehay aidsay. at“Thay eansmay ere’sthay aay alegay
ehindbay emay. Omecay alongay! Enwhay you’reay outhsay ofay ethay Ickystay Aterway e[hay eantmay
ethay Equatoray] anday youray ailtay inglestay, atthay eansmay ere’sthay aay alegay inay ontfray
ofay youay anday youay ustmay eadhay orthnay. Omecay alongay! Ethay aterway eelsfay adbay ere.”hay

Isthay asway oneay ofay eryvay anymay ingsthay atthay Otickkay earnedlay, anday ehay asway alwaysay
earninglay. Atkahmay aughttay imhay otay ollowfay ethay odcay anday ethay alibuthay alongay ethay
under-seaay anksbay anday enchwray ethay ocklingray outay ofay ishay olehay amongay ethay eeds;way
owhay otay irtskay ethay eckswray yinglay aay undredhay athomsfay elowbay aterway anday artday
ikelay aay ifleray ulletbay inay atay oneay ortholepay anday outay atay anotheray asay ethay ishesfay
an;ray owhay otay anceday onay ethay optay ofay ethay avesway enwhay ethay ightninglay asway acingray
allay overay ethay yskay, anday aveway ishay ipperflay olitelypay otay ethay umpy-tailedstay
Albatrossay anday ethay An-of-warmay Awkhay asay eythay entway ownday ethay ind;way owhay otay
umpjay eethray oray ourfay eetfay earclay ofay ethay aterway ikelay aay olphinday, ippersflay
oseclay otay ethay idesay anday ailtay urved;cay otay eavelay ethay yingflay ishfay aloneay
ecausebay eythay areay allay ony;bay otay aketay ethay oulder-pieceshay outay ofay aay odcay atay
ullfay eedspay entay athomsfay eepday, anday evernay otay opstay anday ooklay atay aay oatbay oray aay
ipshay, utbay articularlypay aay ow-boatray. Atay ethay enday ofay ixsay onthsmay atwhay Otickkay
idday otnay owknay aboutay eep-seaday ishingfay asway otnay orthway ethay owingknay. Anday allay
atthay imetay ehay evernay etsay ipperflay onay ydray oundgray.

Oneay ayday, oweverhay, asay ehay asway yinglay alfhay asleepay inay ethay armway aterway
omewheresay offay ethay Islanday ofay Uanjay Ernandezfay, ehay eltfay aintfay anday azylay allay
overay, ustjay asay umanhay eoplepay oday enwhay ethay ingspray isay inay eirthay egslay, anday ehay
ememberedray ethay oodgay irmfay eachesbay ofay Ovastoshnahnay evensay ousandthay ilesmay
awayay, ethay amesgay ishay ompanionscay ayedplay, ethay ellsmay ofay ethay eaweedsay, ethay
ealsay oarray, anday ethay ightingfay. Atthay eryvay inutemay ehay urnedtay orthnay, immingsway
eadilystay, anday asay ehay entway onay ehay etmay oresscay ofay ishay atesmay, allay oundbay orfay
ethay amesay aceplay, anday eythay aid:say eeting“Gray, Otickkay! Isthay yearay eway areay
allay olluschickiehay, anday eway ancay anceday ethay Ire-dancefay inay ethay eakersbray offay
Ukannonlay anday ayplay onay ethay ewnay assgray. Utbay erewhay idday youay etgay atthay oat?”cay

Otick’skay urfay asway almostay urepay itewhay ownay, anday oughthay ehay eltfay eryvay oudpray ofay
itay, ehay onlyay aidsay, im“Sway uicklyqay! Ymay onesbay areay achingay orfay ethay and.”lay Anday
osay eythay allay amecay otay ethay eachesbay erewhay eythay adhay eenbay ornbay, anday eardhay ethay
olday ealssay, eirthay athersfay, ightingfay inay ethay ollingray istmay.

Atthay ightnay Otickkay ancedday ethay Ire-dancefay ithway ethay yearlingay ealssay. Ethay easay
isay ullfay ofay irefay onay ummersay ightsnay allay ethay ayway ownday omfray Ovastoshnahnay otay
Ukannonlay, anday eachay ealsay eaveslay aay akeway ikelay urningbay oilay ehindbay imhay anday aay
amingflay ashflay enwhay ehay umpsjay, anday ethay avesway eakbray inay eatgray osphorescentphay
eaksstray anday irlssway. Enthay eythay entway inlanday otay ethay olluschickiehay oundsgray
anday olledray upay anday ownday inay ethay ewnay ildway eatwhay anday oldtay oriesstay ofay atwhay
eythay adhay oneday ilewhay eythay adhay eenbay atay easay. Eythay alkedtay aboutay ethay Acificpay
asay oysbay ouldway alktay aboutay aay oodway atthay eythay adhay eenbay uttingnay inay, anday ifay
anyoneay adhay understooday emthay ehay ouldcay avehay onegay awayay anday ademay uchsay aay artchay
ofay atthay oceanay asay evernay asway. Ethay ee-thray anday our-year-oldfay olluschickiehay
ompedray ownday omfray Utchinson’shay Illhay ying:cray Out“ay ofay ethay ayway, youngstersay!
Ethay easay isay eepday anday youay on’tday owknay allay at’sthay inay itay yetay. Aitway illtay
you’veay oundedray ethay Ornhay. Ihay, youay yearlingay, erewhay idday youay etgay atthay itewhay
oat?”cay

I“ay idn’tday etgay it,”ay aidsay Otickkay. It“ay ew.”gray Anday ustjay asay ehay asway oinggay otay

amecay omfray ehindbay aay andsay uneday, anday Otickkay, owhay adhay evernay eensay aay anmay
eforebay, oughedcay anday oweredlay ishay eadhay. Ethay olluschickiehay ustjay undledbay offay
aay ewfay yardsay anday atsay aringstay upidlystay. Ethay enmay ereway onay esslay anthay Erickkay
Ooterinbay, ethay iefchay ofay ethay eal-hunterssay onay ethay islanday, anday Atalamonpay,

intoay eal-skinsay acketsjay aterlay onay.

o!”“Hay aidsay Atalamonpay. ook“Lay! Ere’sthay aay itewhay eal!”say

Uick!”qay

Atalamonpay attledray aay airpay ofay eal’ssay ouldershay onesbay inay ontfray ofay aay erdhay
ofay olluschickiehay anday eythay oppedstay eadday, uffingpay anday owingblay. Enthay ehay
eppedstay earnay anday ethay ealssay eganbay otay ovemay, anday Erickkay eadedhay emthay inlanday,
anday eythay evernay iedtray otay etgay ackbay otay eirthay ompanionscay. Undredshay anday
undredshay ofay ousandsthay ofay ealssay atchedway emthay eingbay ivendray, utbay eythay entway
onay ayingplay ustjay ethay amesay. Otickkay asway ethay onlyay oneay owhay askeday uestionsqay,
anday onenay ofay ishay ompanionscay ouldcay elltay imhay anythingay, exceptay atthay ethay
enmay alwaysay ovedray ealssay inay atthay ayway orfay ixsay eeksway oray otway onthsmay ofay everyay
yearay.

I“ay amay oinggay otay ollow,”fay ehay aidsay, anday ishay eyesay earlynay oppedpay outay ofay ishay
eadhay asay ehay uffledshay alongay inay ethay akeway ofay ethay erdhay.

e“Thay itewhay ealsay isay omingcay afteray us,”ay iedcray Atalamonpay. at’s“Thay ethay irstfay
imetay aay ealsay ashay everay omecay otay ethay illing-groundskay alone.”ay

“Hshay! On’tday ooklay ehindbay you,”ay aidsay Erickkay. It“ay isay Aharrof’szay ostghay! Iay
ustmay eakspay otay ethay iestpray aboutay is.”thay

Ethay istanceday otay ethay illing-groundskay asway onlyay alfhay aay ilemay, utbay itay ooktay anay
ourhay otay overcay, ecausebay ifay ethay ealssay entway ootay astfay Erickkay ewknay atthay eythay
ouldway etgay eatedhay anday enthay eirthay urfay ouldway omecay offay inay atchespay enwhay eythay
ereway innedskay. Osay eythay entway onay eryvay owlyslay, astpay Easay Ion’slay Ecknay, astpay
Ebsterway Ousehay, illtay eythay amecay otay ethay Altsay Ousehay ustjay eyondbay ethay ightsay
ofay ethay ealssay onay ethay eachbay. Otickkay ollowedfay, antingpay anday onderingway.
Ehay oughtthay atthay ehay asway atay ethay orld’sway enday, utbay ethay oarray ofay ethay ealsay
urseriesnay ehindbay imhay oundedsay asay oudlay asay ethay oarray ofay aay aintray inay aay unneltay.
Enthay Erickkay atsay ownday onay ethay ossmay anday ulledpay outay aay eavyhay ewterpay atchway
anday etlay ethay ovedray oolcay offay orfay irtythay inutesmay, anday Otickkay ouldcay earhay ethay
og-dewfay ippingdray offay ethay imbray ofay ishay apcay. Enthay entay oray elvetway enmay, eachay
ithway anay iron-bounday ubclay eethray oray ourfay eetfay onglay, amecay upay, anday Erickkay
ointedpay outay oneay oray otway ofay ethay ovedray atthay ereway ittenbay ybay eirthay ompanionscay
oray ootay othay, anday ethay enmay ickedkay osethay asideay ithway eirthay eavyhay ootsbay ademay
ofay ethay inskay ofay aay alrus’sway oatthray, anday enthay Erickkay aidsay, et“Lay o!”gay anday
enthay ethay enmay ubbedclay ethay ealssay onay ethay eadhay asay astfay asay eythay ouldcay.

Entay inutesmay aterlay ittlelay Otickkay idday otnay ecognizeray ishay iendsfray anyay oremay,
orfay eirthay insskay ereway ippedray offay omfray ethay osenay otay ethay indhay ippersflay,
ippedwhay offay anday ownthray ownday onay ethay oundgray inay aay ilepay. Atthay asway enoughay
orfay Otickkay. Ehay urnedtay anday allopedgay a(ay ealsay ancay allopgay eryvay iftlysway orfay
aay ortshay imetay) ackbay otay ethay ea;say ishay ittlelay ewnay ustachemay istlingbray ithway
orrorhay. Atay Easay Ion’slay Ecknay, erewhay ethay eatgray easay ionslay itsay onay ethay edgeay
ofay ethay urfsay, ehay ungflay imselfhay ipper-overheadflay intoay ethay oolcay aterway anday
ockedray erethay, aspinggay iserablymay. at’s“Whay ere?”hay aidsay aay easay ionlay ufflygray,
orfay asay aay uleray ethay easay ionslay eepkay emselvesthay otay emselvesthay.

ell“Way oneday orfay aay yearling!”ay aidsay ethay Easay Ionlay, owhay ouldcay appreciateay oodgay
immingsway. I“ay upposesay itay isay atherray awfulay omfray youray ayway ofay ookinglay atay itay,

otay owknay ofay itay, anday unlessay youay ancay indfay anay islanday erewhay onay enmay everay omecay
youay illway alwaysay ebay iven.”dray

Isn’t“ay erethay anyay uchsay island?”ay eganbay Otickkay.

I’ve“ay ollowedfay ethay oltoospay e[thay alibuthay] orfay entytway yearsay, anday Iay an’tcay
aysay I’veay oundfay itay yetay. Utbay ooklay ere--youhay eemsay otay avehay aay ondnessfay orfay
alkingtay otay youray etters--supposebay youay ogay otay Alrusway Isletay anday alktay otay
Easay Itchvay. Ehay aymay owknay omethingsay. On’tday ounceflay offay ikelay atthay. It’say aay
ix-milesay imsway, anday ifay Iay ereway youay Iay ouldshay aulhay outay anday aketay aay apnay irstfay,
ittlelay one.”ay

Otickkay oughtthay atthay atthay asway oodgay adviceay, osay ehay amsway oundray otay ishay ownay
eachbay, auledhay outay, anday eptslay orfay alfhay anay ourhay, itchingtway allay overay, asay
ealssay illway. Enthay ehay eadedhay aightstray orfay Alrusway Isletay, aay ittlelay owlay eetshay
ofay ockyray islanday almostay ueday ortheastnay omfray Ovastoshnahnay, allay edgeslay anday
ockray anday ulls’gay estsnay, erewhay ethay alrusway erdedhay ybay emselvesthay.

Ehay andedlay oseclay otay olday Easay Itch--thevay igbay, uglyay, oatedblay, impledpay,
at-neckedfay, ong-tuskedlay alrusway ofay ethay Orthnay Acificpay, owhay ashay onay annersmay
exceptay enwhay ehay isay asleep--asay ehay asway enthay, ithway ishay indhay ippersflay alfhay inay
anday alfhay outay ofay ethay urfsay.

ake“Way up!”ay arkedbay Otickkay, orfay ethay ullsgay ereway akingmay aay eatgray oisenay.

ah“Hay! Ohay! Hmphay! At’swhay at?”thay aidsay Easay Itchvay, anday ehay uckstray ethay extnay

Otickkay amsway ackbay otay Ovastoshnahnay, eavinglay ethay ullsgay otay eamscray. Erethay ehay
oundfay atthay onay oneay ympathizedsay ithway imhay inay ishay ittlelay attemptay otay iscoverday
aay uietqay aceplay orfay ethay ealssay. Eythay oldtay imhay atthay enmay adhay alwaysay ivendray
ethay olluschickie--ithay asway artpay ofay ethay ay’sday ork--andway atthay ifay ehay idday otnay
ikelay otay eesay uglyay ingsthay ehay ouldshay otnay avehay onegay otay ethay illingkay oundsgray.
Utbay onenay ofay ethay otheray ealssay adhay eensay ethay illingkay, anday atthay ademay ethay
ifferenceday etweenbay imhay anday ishay iendsfray. Esidesbay, Otickkay asway aay itewhay
ealsay.

at“Whay youay ustmay o,”day aidsay olday Easay Atchcay, afteray ehay adhay eardhay ishay on’ssay
adventuresay, is“ay otay owgray upay anday ebay aay igbay ealsay ikelay youray atherfay, anday avehay
aay urserynay onay ethay eachbay, anday enthay eythay illway eavelay youay aloneay. Inay anotheray
ivefay yearsay youay oughtay otay ebay ableay otay ightfay orfay yourself.”ay Evenay entlegay
Atkahmay, ishay othermay, aid:say You“ay illway evernay ebay ableay otay opstay ethay illingkay.
Ogay anday ayplay inay ethay easay, Otick.”kay Anday Otickkay entway offay anday ancedday ethay
Ire-dancefay ithway aay eryvay eavyhay ittlelay earthay.

Atthay autumnay ehay eftlay ethay eachbay asay oonsay asay ehay ouldcay, anday etsay offay aloneay
ecausebay ofay aay otionnay inay ishay ullet-headbay. Ehay asway oinggay otay indfay Easay Owcay,
ifay erethay asway uchsay aay ersonpay inay ethay easay, anday ehay asway oinggay otay indfay aay uietqay
islanday ithway oodgay irmfay eachesbay orfay ealssay otay ivelay onay, erewhay enmay ouldcay otnay
etgay atay emthay. Osay ehay exploreday anday exploreday ybay imselfhay omfray ethay Orthnay otay
ethay Outhsay Acificpay, immingsway asay uchmay asay eethray undredhay ilesmay inay aay ayday
anday aay ightnay. Ehay etmay ithway oremay adventuresay anthay ancay ebay oldtay, anday arrowlynay
escapeday eingbay aughtcay ybay ethay Askingbay Arkshay, anday ethay Ottedspay Arkshay, anday
ethay Ammerheadhay, anday ehay etmay allay ethay untrustworthyay uffiansray atthay oaflay upay
anday ownday ethay eassay, anday ethay eavyhay olitepay ishfay, anday ethay arletscay ottedspay
allopsscay atthay areay ooredmay inay oneay aceplay orfay undredshay ofay yearsay, anday owgray
eryvay oudpray ofay it;ay utbay ehay evernay etmay Easay Owcay, anday ehay evernay oundfay anay islanday
atthay ehay ouldcay ancyfay.

Ifay ethay eachbay asway oodgay anday ardhay, ithway aay opeslay ehindbay itay orfay ealssay otay ayplay
onay, erethay asway alwaysay ethay okesmay ofay aay alerwhay onay ethay orizonhay, oilingbay ownday
ubberblay, anday Otickkay ewknay atwhay atthay eantmay. Oray elseay ehay ouldcay eesay atthay
ealssay adhay onceay isitedvay ethay islanday anday eenbay illedkay offay, anday Otickkay ewknay
atthay erewhay enmay adhay omecay onceay eythay ouldway omecay againay.

Ehay ickedpay upay ithway anay olday umpy-tailedstay albatrossay, owhay oldtay imhay atthay
Erguelenkay Islanday asway ethay eryvay aceplay orfay eacepay anday uietqay, anday enwhay Otickkay
entway ownday erethay ehay asway allay utbay ashedsmay otay iecespay againstay omesay ickedway
ackblay iffsclay inay aay eavyhay eet-stormslay ithway ightninglay anday underthay. Yetay asay
ehay ulledpay outay againstay ethay alegay ehay ouldcay eesay atthay evenay erethay adhay onceay
eenbay aay ealsay urserynay. Anday itay asway osay inay allay ethay otheray islandsay atthay ehay
isitedvay.

Immershinlay avegay aay onglay istlay ofay emthay, orfay ehay aidsay atthay Otickkay entspay ivefay
easonssay exploringay, ithway aay ourfay onths’may estray eachay yearay atay Ovastoshnahnay,
enwhay ethay olluschickiehay useday otay akemay unfay ofay imhay anday ishay imaginaryay
islandsay. Ehay entway otay ethay Allapagosgay, aay orridhay ydray aceplay onay ethay Equatoray,
erewhay ehay asway earlynay akedbay otay eath;day ehay entway otay ethay Eorgiagay Islandsay,
ethay Orkneysay, Emeralday Islanday, Ittlelay Ightingalenay Islanday, Ough’sgay Islanday,
Ouvet’sbay Islanday, ethay Ossetscray, anday evenay otay aay ittlelay eckspay ofay anay islanday
outhsay ofay ethay Apecay ofay Oodgay Opehay. Utbay everywhereay ethay Eoplepay ofay ethay Easay
oldtay imhay ethay amesay ingsthay. Ealssay adhay omecay otay osethay islandsay onceay uponay aay
imetay, utbay enmay adhay illedkay emthay allay offay. Evenay enwhay ehay amsway ousandsthay ofay
ilesmay outay ofay ethay Acificpay anday otgay otay aay aceplay alledcay Apecay Orrientescay at(thay
asway enwhay ehay asway omingcay ackbay omfray Ough’sgay Island)ay, ehay oundfay aay ewfay undredhay
angymay ealssay onay aay ockray anday eythay oldtay imhay atthay enmay amecay erethay ootay.

Atthay earlynay okebray ishay earthay, anday ehay eadedhay oundray ethay Ornhay ackbay otay ishay
ownay eaches;bay anday onay ishay ayway orthnay ehay auledhay outay onay anay islanday ullfay ofay
eengray eestray, erewhay ehay oundfay anay olday, olday ealsay owhay asway yingday, anday Otickkay
aughtcay ishfay orfay imhay anday oldtay imhay allay ishay orrowssay. ow,”“Nay aidsay Otickkay,
I“ay amay oinggay ackbay otay Ovastoshnahnay, anday ifay Iay amay ivendray otay ethay illing-penskay
ithway ethay olluschickiehay Iay allshay otnay are.”cay

Ethay olday ealsay aidsay, y“Tray onceay oremay. Iay amay ethay astlay ofay ethay Ostlay Ookeryray ofay
Asafueramay, anday inay ethay aysday enwhay enmay illedkay usay ybay ethay undredhay ousandthay
erethay asway aay orystay onay ethay eachesbay atthay omesay ayday aay itewhay ealsay ouldway omecay
outay ofay ethay Orthnay anday eadlay ethay ealsay eoplepay otay aay uietqay aceplay. Iay amay olday,
anday Iay allshay evernay ivelay otay eesay atthay ayday, utbay othersay illway. Ytray onceay ore.”may

Anday Otickkay urledcay upay ishay ustachemay it(ay asway aay eautybay) anday aidsay, I“ay amay ethay
onlyay itewhay ealsay atthay ashay everay eenbay ornbay onay ethay eachesbay, anday Iay amay ethay
onlyay ealsay, ackblay oray itewhay, owhay everay oughtthay ofay ookinglay orfay ewnay islands.”ay

Isthay eeredchay imhay immensely;ay anday enwhay ehay amecay ackbay otay Ovastoshnahnay atthay
ummersay, Atkahmay, ishay othermay, eggedbay imhay otay arrymay anday ettlesay ownday, orfay
ehay asway onay ongerlay aay olluschickhay utbay aay ull-grownfay ea-catchsay, ithway aay urlycay
itewhay anemay onay ishay ouldersshay, asay eavyhay, asay igbay, anday asay iercefay asay ishay
atherfay. ive“Gay emay anotheray eason,”say ehay aidsay. emember“Ray, Othermay, itay isay
alwaysay ethay eventhsay aveway atthay oesgay arthestfay upay ethay each.”bay

Uriouslycay enoughay, erethay asway anotheray ealsay owhay oughtthay atthay eshay ouldway utpay
offay arryingmay illtay ethay extnay yearay, anday Otickkay ancedday ethay Ire-dancefay ithway
erhay allay ownday Ukannonlay Eachbay ethay ightnay eforebay ehay etsay offay onay ishay astlay
explorationay. Isthay imetay ehay entway estwardway, ecausebay ehay adhay allenfay onay ethay
ailtray ofay aay eatgray oalshay ofay alibuthay, anday ehay eedednay atay eastlay oneay undredhay
oundspay ofay ishfay aay ayday otay eepkay imhay inay oodgay onditioncay. Ehay asedchay emthay illtay
ehay asway iredtay, anday enthay ehay urledcay imselfhay upay anday entway otay eepslay onay ethay
ollowshay ofay ethay oundgray ellsway atthay etssay inay otay Oppercay Islanday. Ehay ewknay ethay
oastcay erfectlypay ellway, osay aboutay idnightmay, enwhay ehay eltfay imselfhay entlygay
umpedbay onay aay eed-bedway, ehay aidsay, “Hmay, ide’stay unningray ongstray onight,”tay anday
urningtay overay underay aterway openeday ishay eyesay owlyslay anday etchedstray. Enthay
ehay umpedjay ikelay aay atcay, orfay ehay awsay ugehay ingsthay osingnay aboutay inay ethay oalshay
aterway anday owsingbray onay ethay eavyhay ingesfray ofay ethay eedsway.

y“Bay ethay Eatgray Omberscay ofay Agellan!”may ehay aidsay, eneathbay ishay ustachemay. o“Whay
inay ethay Eepday Easay areay esethay eople?”pay

Eythay ereway ikelay onay alrusway, easay ionlay, ealsay, earbay, alewhay, arkshay, ishfay,

ovel-likeshay ailtay atthay ookedlay asay ifay itay adhay eenbay ittledwhay outay ofay etway

anday eythay alancedbay onay ethay endsay ofay eirthay ailstay inay eepday aterway enwhay eythay
eren’tway azinggray, owingbay olemnlysay otay eachay otheray anday avingway eirthay ontfray
ippersflay asay aay atfay anmay avesway ishay armay.

Enthay ehay ememberedray inay aay ashflay atwhay ethay Urgomasterbay ullgay adhay eamedscray
otay imhay enwhay ehay asway aay ittlelay yearlingay atay Alrusway Isletay, anday ehay umbledtay
ackwardbay inay ethay aterway, orfay ehay ewknay atthay ehay adhay oundfay Easay Owcay atay astlay.

Ethay easay owscay entway onay oopingschlay anday azinggray anday umpingchay inay ethay eedway,
anday Otickkay askeday emthay uestionsqay inay everyay anguagelay atthay ehay adhay ickedpay
upay inay ishay avels;tray anday ethay Easay Eoplepay alktay earlynay asay anymay anguageslay asay
umanhay eingsbay. Utbay ethay easay owscay idday otnay answeray ecausebay Easay Owcay annotcay
alktay. Ehay ashay onlyay ixsay onesbay inay ishay ecknay erewhay ehay oughtay otay avehay evensay,
anday eythay aysay underay ethay easay atthay atthay eventspray imhay omfray eakingspay evenay
otay ishay ompanionscay. Utbay, asay youay owknay, ehay ashay anay extraay ointjay inay ishay
oreflipperfay, anday ybay avingway itay upay anday ownday anday aboutay ehay akesmay atwhay
answersay otay aay ortsay ofay umsyclay elegraphictay odecay.

Ybay aylightday Otick’skay anemay asway andingstay onay enday anday ishay empertay asway onegay
erewhay ethay eadday abscray ogay. Enthay ethay Easay Owcay eganbay otay aveltray orthwardnay eryvay
owlyslay, oppingstay otay oldhay absurday owingbay ouncilscay omfray imetay otay imetay, anday
Otickkay ollowedfay emthay, ayingsay otay imselfhay, eople“Pay owhay areay uchsay idiotsay asay
esethay areay ouldway avehay eenbay illedkay onglay agoay ifay eythay adn’thay oundfay outay omesay
afesay islanday. Anday atwhay isay oodgay enoughay orfay ethay Easay Owcay isay oodgay enoughay orfay
ethay Easay Atchcay. Allay ethay amesay, Iay ishway ey’dthay urry.”hay

Itay asway earyway orkway orfay Otickkay. Ethay erdhay evernay entway oremay anthay ortyfay oray
iftyfay ilesmay aay ayday, anday oppedstay otay eedfay atay ightnay, anday eptkay oseclay otay ethay
oreshay allay ethay ime;tay ilewhay Otickkay amsway oundray emthay, anday overay emthay, anday
underay emthay, utbay ehay ouldcay otnay urryhay emthay upay one-halfay ilemay. Asay eythay entway
artherfay orthnay eythay eldhay aay owingbay ouncilcay everyay ewfay ourshay, anday Otickkay
earlynay itbay offay ishay ustachemay ithway impatienceay illtay ehay awsay atthay eythay ereway
ollowingfay upay aay armway urrentcay ofay aterway, anday enthay ehay espectedray emthay oremay.

Oneay ightnay eythay anksay oughthray ethay inyshay ater--sankway ikelay ones--andstay orfay
ethay irstfay imetay incesay ehay adhay ownknay emthay eganbay otay imsway uicklyqay. Otickkay
ollowedfay, anday ethay acepay astonisheday imhay, orfay ehay evernay eameddray atthay Easay Owcay
asway anythingay ofay aay immersway. Eythay eadedhay orfay aay iffclay ybay ethay ore--ashay iffclay
atthay anray ownday intoay eepday aterway, anday ungedplay intoay aay arkday olehay atay ethay
ootfay ofay itay, entytway athomsfay underay ethay easay. Itay asway aay onglay, onglay imsway, anday
Otickkay adlybay antedway eshfray airay eforebay ehay asway outay ofay ethay arkday unneltay eythay
edlay imhay oughthray.

y“May ig!”way ehay aidsay, enwhay ehay oseray, aspinggay anday uffingpay, intoay openay aterway atay
ethay artherfay enday. It“ay asway aay onglay iveday, utbay itay asway orthway it.”ay

Ethay easay owscay adhay eparatedsay anday ereway owsingbray azilylay alongay ethay edgesay ofay
ethay inestfay eachesbay atthay Otickkay adhay everay eensay. Erethay ereway onglay
etchesstray ofay ooth-wornsmay ockray unningray orfay ilesmay, exactlyay ittedfay otay akemay
eal-nurseriessay, anday erethay ereway ay-groundsplay ofay ardhay andsay opingslay inlanday
ehindbay emthay, anday erethay ereway ollersray orfay ealssay otay anceday inay, anday onglay
assgray otay ollray inay, anday andsay unesday otay imbclay upay anday ownday, anday, estbay ofay allay,
Otickkay ewknay ybay ethay eelfay ofay ethay aterway, ichwhay evernay eceivesday aay uetray easay
atchcay, atthay onay enmay adhay everay omecay erethay.

Ethay irstfay ingthay ehay idday asway otay assureay imselfhay atthay ethay ishingfay asway oodgay,
anday enthay ehay amsway alongay ethay eachesbay anday ountedcay upay ethay elightfulday owlay
andysay islandsay alfhay iddenhay inay ethay eautifulbay ollingray ogfay. Awayay otay ethay
orthwardnay, outay otay easay, anray aay inelay ofay arsbay anday oalsshay anday ocksray atthay
ouldway evernay etlay aay ipshay omecay ithinway ixsay ilesmay ofay ethay eachbay, anday etweenbay
ethay islandsay anday ethay ainlandmay asway aay etchstray ofay eepday aterway atthay anray upay otay
ethay erpendicularpay iffsclay, anday omewheresay elowbay ethay iffsclay asway ethay outhmay
ofay ethay unneltay.

It’s“ay Ovastoshnahnay overay againay, utbay entay imestay etter,”bay aidsay Otickkay. ea“Say
Owcay ustmay ebay iserway anthay Iay oughtthay. Enmay an’tcay omecay ownday ethay iffsclay, evenay
ifay erethay ereway anyay en;may anday ethay oalsshay otay eawardsay ouldway ockknay aay ipshay otay
interssplay. Ifay anyay aceplay inay ethay easay isay afesay, isthay isay it.”ay

Ehay eganbay otay inkthay ofay ethay ealsay ehay adhay eftlay ehindbay imhay, utbay oughthay ehay asway
inay aay urryhay otay ogay ackbay otay Ovastoshnahnay, ehay oroughlythay exploreday ethay ewnay
ountrycay, osay atthay ehay ouldway ebay ableay otay answeray allay uestionsqay.

Enthay ehay ivedday anday ademay uresay ofay ethay outhmay ofay ethay unneltay, anday acedray
oughthray otay ethay outhwardsay. Onay oneay utbay aay easay owcay oray aay ealsay ouldway avehay
eameddray ofay erethay eingbay uchsay aay aceplay, anday enwhay ehay ookedlay ackbay atay ethay
iffsclay evenay Otickkay ouldcay ardlyhay elievebay atthay ehay adhay eenbay underay emthay.

Ehay asway ixsay aysday oinggay omehay, oughthay ehay asway otnay immingsway owly;slay anday enwhay
ehay auledhay outay ustjay aboveay Easay Ion’slay Ecknay ethay irstfay ersonpay ehay etmay asway ethay
ealsay owhay adhay eenbay aitingway orfay imhay, anday eshay awsay ybay ethay ooklay inay ishay eyesay
atthay ehay adhay oundfay ishay islanday atay astlay.

Utbay ethay olluschickiehay anday Easay Atchcay, ishay atherfay, anday allay ethay otheray ealssay
aughedlay atay imhay enwhay ehay oldtay emthay atwhay ehay adhay iscoveredday, anday aay youngay
ealsay aboutay ishay ownay ageay aidsay, is“Thay isay allay eryvay ellway, Otickkay, utbay youay
an’tcay omecay omfray onay oneay owsknay erewhay anday orderay usay offay ikelay isthay. Ememberray
e’veway eenbay ightingfay orfay ouray urseriesnay, anday at’sthay aay ingthay youay evernay idday.
Youay eferredpray owlingpray aboutay inay ethay ea.”say

Ethay otheray ealssay aughedlay atay isthay, anday ethay youngay ealsay eganbay istingtway ishay
eadhay omfray idesay otay idesay. Ehay adhay ustjay arriedmay atthay yearay, anday asway akingmay aay
eatgray ussfay aboutay itay.

I’ve“ay onay urserynay otay ightfay or,”fay aidsay Otickkay. I“ay onlyay antway otay owshay youay
allay aay aceplay erewhay youay illway ebay afesay. At’swhay ethay useay ofay ighting?”fay

Oh“ay, ifay you’reay yingtray otay ackbay outay, ofay oursecay I’veay onay oremay otay ay,”say aidsay
ethay youngay ealsay ithway anay uglyay ucklechay.

ill“Way youay omecay ithway emay ifay Iay in?”way aidsay Otickkay. Anday aay eengray ightlay amecay
intoay ishay eyeay, orfay ehay asway eryvay angryay atay avinghay otay ightfay atay allay.

ery“Vay ood,”gay aidsay ethay youngay ealsay arelesslycay. If“ay youay inway, I’llay ome.”cay

Ehay adhay onay imetay otay angechay ishay indmay, orfay Otick’skay eadhay asway outay anday ishay
eethtay unksay inay ethay ubberblay ofay ethay youngay eal’ssay ecknay. Enthay ehay ewthray
imselfhay ackbay onay ishay auncheshay anday auledhay ishay enemyay ownday ethay eachbay, ookshay
imhay, anday ockedknay imhay overay. Enthay Otickkay oaredray otay ethay eals:say I’ve“ay oneday
ymay estbay orfay youay esethay ivefay easonssay astpay. I’veay oundfay youay ethay islanday erewhay
you’llay ebay afesay, utbay unlessay youray eadshay areay aggeddray offay youray illysay ecksnay
youay on’tway elievebay. I’may oinggay otay eachtay youay ownay. Ooklay outay orfay yourselves!”ay

Immershinlay oldtay emay atthay evernay inay ishay ife--andlay Immershinlay eessay entay
ousandthay igbay ealssay ightingfay everyay year--neveray inay allay ishay ittlelay ifelay
idday ehay eesay anythingay ikelay Otick’skay argechay intoay ethay urseriesnay. Ehay ungflay
imselfhay atay ethay iggestbay easay atchcay ehay ouldcay indfay, aughtcay imhay ybay ethay
oatthray, okedchay imhay anday umpedbay imhay anday angedbay imhay illtay ehay untedgray orfay
ercymay, anday enthay ewthray imhay asideay anday attackeday ethay extnay. Youay eesay, Otickkay
adhay evernay astedfay orfay ourfay onthsmay asay ethay igbay ealssay idday everyay yearay, anday
ishay eep-seaday immingsway ipstray eptkay imhay inay erfectpay onditioncay, anday, estbay
ofay allay, ehay adhay evernay oughtfay eforebay. Ishay urlycay itewhay anemay oodstay upay ithway
ageray, anday ishay eyesay amedflay, anday ishay igbay ogday eethtay istenedglay, anday ehay asway
endidsplay otay ooklay atay. Olday Easay Atchcay, ishay atherfay, awsay imhay earingtay astpay,
aulinghay ethay izzledgray olday ealssay aboutay asay oughthay eythay adhay eenbay alibuthay,
anday upsettingay ethay youngay achelorsbay inay allay irections;day anday Easay Atchcay avegay
aay oarray anday outed:shay e“Hay aymay ebay aay oolfay, utbay ehay isay ethay estbay ighterfay onay ethay
eachesbay! On’tday ackletay youray atherfay, ymay onsay! E’shay ithway you!”ay

Otickkay oaredray inay answeray, anday olday Easay Atchcay addledway inay ithway ishay ustachemay
onay enday, owingblay ikelay aay ocomotivelay, ilewhay Atkahmay anday ethay ealsay atthay asway
oinggay otay arrymay Otickkay oweredcay ownday anday admireday eirthay en-folkmay. Itay asway
aay orgeousgay ightfay, orfay ethay otway oughtfay asay onglay asay erethay asway aay ealsay atthay
aredday iftlay upay ishay eadhay, anday enwhay erethay ereway onenay eythay aradedpay andlygray upay
anday ownday ethay eachbay idesay ybay idesay, ellowingbay.

Atay ightnay, ustjay asay ethay Orthernnay Ightslay ereway inkingway anday ashingflay oughthray
ethay ogfay, Otickkay imbedclay aay arebay ockray anday ookedlay ownday onay ethay atteredscay
urseriesnay anday ethay orntay anday eedingblay ealssay. ow,”“Nay ehay aidsay, I’ve“ay aughttay
youay youray esson.”lay

y“May ig!”way aidsay olday Easay Atchcay, oostingbay imselfhay upay ifflystay, orfay ehay asway
earfullyfay auledmay. e“Thay Illerkay Alewhay imselfhay ouldcay otnay avehay utcay emthay upay

youray island--ifay erethay isay uchsay aay ace.”play

ear“Hay youay, atfay igspay ofay ethay easay. Owhay omescay ithway emay otay ethay Easay Ow’scay
unneltay? Answeray, oray Iay allshay eachtay youay again,”ay oaredray Otickkay.

Erethay asway aay urmurmay ikelay ethay ippleray ofay ethay idetay allay upay anday ownday ethay
eachesbay. e“Way illway ome,”cay aidsay ousandsthay ofay iredtay oicesvay. e“Way illway ollowfay
Otickkay, ethay Itewhay Eal.”say

Enthay Otickkay oppeddray ishay eadhay etweenbay ishay ouldersshay anday utshay ishay eyesay
oudlypray. Ehay asway otnay aay itewhay ealsay anyay oremay, utbay edray omfray eadhay otay ailtay.
Allay ethay amesay ehay ouldway avehay ornedscay otay ooklay atay oray ouchtay oneay ofay ishay
oundsway.

Aay eekway aterlay ehay anday ishay armyay early(nay entay ousandthay olluschickiehay anday olday
ealssay) entway awayay orthnay otay ethay Easay Ow’scay unneltay, Otickkay eadinglay emthay,
anday ethay ealssay atthay ayedstay atay Ovastoshnahnay alledcay emthay idiotsay. Utbay extnay
ingspray, enwhay eythay allay etmay offay ethay ishingfay anksbay ofay ethay Acificpay, Otick’skay
ealssay oldtay uchsay alestay ofay ethay ewnay eachesbay eyondbay Easay Ow’scay unneltay atthay
oremay anday oremay ealssay eftlay Ovastoshnahnay. Ofay oursecay itay asway otnay allay oneday atay
onceay, orfay ethay ealssay areay otnay eryvay everclay, anday eythay eednay aay onglay imetay otay
urntay ingsthay overay inay eirthay indsmay, utbay yearay afteray yearay oremay ealssay entway
awayay omfray Ovastoshnahnay, anday Ukannonlay, anday ethay otheray urseriesnay, otay ethay
uietqay, elteredshay eachesbay erewhay Otickkay itssay allay ethay ummersay oughthray,
ettinggay iggerbay anday atterfay anday ongerstray eachay yearay, ilewhay ethay
olluschickiehay ayplay arounday imhay, inay atthay easay erewhay onay anmay omescay.




Ukannonlay


Isthay isay ethay eatgray eep-seaday ongsay atthay allay ethay Stay. Aulpay ealssay ingsay enwhay
eythay areay eadinghay ackbay otay eirthay eachesbay inay ethay ummersay. Itay isay aay ortsay ofay
eryvay adsay ealsay Ationalnay Anthemay.

Iay etmay ymay atesmay inay ethay orningmay and(ay, ohay, utbay Iay amay old!ay)
Erewhay oaringray onay ethay edgeslay ethay ummersay ound-swellgray olled;ray
Iay eardhay emthay iftlay ethay oruschay atthay owneddray ethay eakers’bray ong—say
Ethay Eachesbay ofay Ukannon—twolay illionmay oicesvay ongstray.

e_Thay ongsay ofay easantplay ationsstay esidebay ethay altsay agoonslay,
Ethay ongsay ofay owingblay uadronssqay atthay uffledshay ownday ethay unesday,
Ethay ongsay ofay idnightmay ancesday atthay urnedchay ethay easay otay ame—flay
Ethay Eachesbay ofay Ukannon—beforelay ethay ealerssay ame!_cay

Iay etmay ymay atesmay inay ethay orningmay I’ll(ay evernay eetmay emthay ore!);may
Eythay amecay anday entway inay egionslay atthay arkenedday allay ethay oreshay.
Anday o’eray ethay oam-fleckedfay offingay asay arfay asay oicevay ouldcay eachray
Eway ailedhay ethay anding-partieslay anday eway angsay emthay upay ethay eachbay.

e_Thay Eachesbay ofay Ukannon—thelay interway eatwhay osay all—tay
Ethay ippingdray, inkledcray ichenslay, anday ethay ea-fogsay enchingdray allay!
Ethay atformsplay ofay ouray aygroundplay, allay iningshay oothsmay anday ornway!
Ethay Eachesbay ofay Ukannon—thelay omehay erewhay eway ereway orn!_bay

Iay etmay ymay atesmay inay ethay orningmay, aay okenbray, atteredscay andbay.
Enmay ootshay usay inay ethay aterway anday ubclay usay onay ethay and;lay
Enmay ivedray usay otay ethay Altsay Ousehay ikelay illysay eepshay anday ametay,
Anday illstay eway ingsay Ukannon—beforelay ethay ealerssay amecay.

eel_Whay ownday, eelwhay ownday otay outhward;say ohay, Ooverooskagay, ogay!
Anday elltay ethay Eep-Seaday Iceroysvay ethay orystay ofay ouray oe;way
Ereay, emptyay asay ethay ark’sshay eggay ethay empesttay ingsflay ashoreay,
Ethay Eachesbay ofay Ukannonlay allshay owknay eirthay onssay onay ore!_may

oe(_Way etidebay eethay, Ag!_nay)

Isthay isay ethay orystay ofay ethay eatgray arway atthay Ikki-tikki-taviray oughtfay
ingle-handedsay, oughthray ethay ath-roomsbay ofay ethay igbay ungalowbay inay Egowleesay
antonmentcay. Arzeeday, ethay Ailorbirdtay, elpedhay imhay, anday Uchundrachay, ethay
uskratmay, owhay evernay omescay outay intoay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay oorflay, utbay alwaysay
eepscray oundray ybay ethay allway, avegay imhay adviceay, utbay Ikki-tikkiray idday ethay ealray
ightingfay.

Ehay asway aay ongoosemay, atherray ikelay aay ittlelay atcay inay ishay urfay anday ishay ailtay, utbay
uiteqay ikelay aay easelway inay ishay eadhay anday ishay abitshay. Ishay eyesay anday ethay enday
ofay ishay estlessray osenay ereway inkpay. Ehay ouldcay atchscray imselfhay anywhereay ehay
easedplay ithway anyay eglay, ontfray oray ackbay, atthay ehay osechay otay useay. Ehay ouldcay
uffflay upay ishay ailtay illtay itay ookedlay ikelay aay ottlebay ushbray, anday ishay arway ycray asay
ehay uttledscay oughthray ethay onglay assgray as:way ikk-tikk-tikki-tikki-tchk!”“Ray

Oneay ayday, aay ighhay ummersay oodflay ashedway imhay outay ofay ethay urrowbay erewhay ehay ivedlay
ithway ishay atherfay anday othermay, anday arriedcay imhay, ickingkay anday uckingclay, ownday
aay oadsideray itchday. Ehay oundfay aay ittlelay ispway ofay assgray oatingflay erethay, anday
ungclay otay itay illtay ehay ostlay ishay ensessay. Enwhay ehay evivedray, ehay asway yinglay inay
ethay othay unsay onay ethay iddlemay ofay aay ardengay athpay, eryvay aggleddray indeeday, anday aay
allsmay oybay asway ayingsay, ere’s“Hay aay eadday ongoosemay. Et’slay avehay aay uneral.”fay

o,”“Nay aidsay ishay othermay, et’s“lay aketay imhay inay anday ydray imhay. Erhapspay ehay isn’tay
eallyray ead.”day

Eythay ooktay imhay intoay ethay ousehay, anday aay igbay anmay ickedpay imhay upay etweenbay ishay
ingerfay anday umbthay anday aidsay ehay asway otnay eadday utbay alfhay okedchay. Osay eythay
appedwray imhay inay ottoncay oolway, anday armedway imhay overay aay ittlelay irefay, anday ehay
openeday ishay eyesay anday eezedsnay.

ow,”“Nay aidsay ethay igbay anmay e(hay asway anay Englishmanay owhay adhay ustjay ovedmay intoay
ethay ungalow)bay, on’t“day ightenfray imhay, anday e’llway eesay atwhay e’llhay o.”day

Itay isay ethay ardesthay ingthay inay ethay orldway otay ightenfray aay ongoosemay, ecausebay
ehay isay eatenay upay omfray osenay otay ailtay ithway uriositycay. Ethay ottomay ofay allay
ethay ongoosemay amilyfay isay un“Ray anday indfay out,”ay anday Ikki-tikkiray asway aay uetray
ongoosemay. Ehay ookedlay atay ethay ottoncay oolway, ecidedday atthay itay asway otnay oodgay otay
eatay, anray allay oundray ethay abletay, atsay upay anday utpay ishay urfay inay orderay, atchedscray
imselfhay, anday umpedjay onay ethay allsmay oy’sbay ouldershay.

on’t“Day ebay ightenedfray, Eddy,”tay aidsay ishay atherfay. at’s“Thay ishay ayway ofay akingmay
iends.”fray

Ouch“ay! E’shay icklingtay underay ymay in,”chay aidsay Eddytay.

Ikki-tikkiray ookedlay ownday etweenbay ethay oy’sbay ollarcay anday ecknay, uffedsnay atay
ishay earay, anday imbedclay ownday otay ethay oorflay, erewhay ehay atsay ubbingray ishay osenay.

ood“Gay acious,”gray aidsay Eddy’stay othermay, and“ay at’sthay aay ildway eaturecray! Iay
upposesay e’shay osay ametay ecausebay e’veway eenbay indkay otay im.”hay

All“ay ongoosesmay areay ikelay at,”thay aidsay erhay usbandhay. If“ay Eddytay oesn’tday ickpay
imhay upay ybay ethay ailtay, oray ytray otay utpay imhay inay aay agecay, e’llhay unray inay anday outay ofay
ethay ousehay allay ayday onglay. Et’slay ivegay imhay omethingsay otay eat.”ay

Eythay avegay imhay aay ittlelay iecepay ofay awray eatmay. Ikki-tikkiray ikedlay itay
immenselyay, anday enwhay itay asway inishedfay ehay entway outay intoay ethay erandavay anday atsay
inay ethay unshinesay anday uffedflay upay ishay urfay otay akemay itay ydray otay ethay ootsray. Enthay
ehay eltfay etterbay.

ere“Thay areay oremay ingsthay otay indfay outay aboutay inay isthay ouse,”hay ehay aidsay otay
imselfhay, an“thay allay ymay amilyfay ouldcay indfay outay inay allay eirthay iveslay. Iay allshay
ertainlycay aystay anday indfay out.”ay

Ehay entspay allay atthay ayday oamingray overay ethay ousehay. Ehay earlynay owneddray imselfhay
inay ethay ath-tubsbay, utpay ishay osenay intoay ethay inkay onay aay itingwray abletay, anday
urnedbay itay onay ethay enday ofay ethay igbay an’smay igarcay, orfay ehay imbedclay upay inay ethay
igbay an’smay aplay otay eesay owhay itingwray asway oneday. Atay ightfallnay ehay anray intoay
Eddy’stay urserynay otay atchway owhay erosenekay ampslay ereway ightedlay, anday enwhay Eddytay
entway otay edbay Ikki-tikkiray imbedclay upay ootay. Utbay ehay asway aay estlessray ompanioncay,
ecausebay ehay adhay otay etgay upay anday attenday otay everyay oisenay allay oughthray ethay
ightnay, anday indfay outay atwhay ademay itay. Eddy’stay othermay anday atherfay amecay inay,
ethay astlay ingthay, otay ooklay atay eirthay oybay, anday Ikki-tikkiray asway awakeay onay
ethay illowpay. I“ay on’tday ikelay at,”thay aidsay Eddy’stay othermay. e“Hay aymay itebay ethay
ild.”chay e’ll“Hay oday onay uchsay ing,”thay aidsay ethay atherfay. eddy’s“Tay afersay ithway
atthay ittlelay eastbay anthay ifay ehay adhay aay oodhoundblay otay atchway imhay. Ifay aay akesnay
amecay intoay ethay urserynay ow--”nay

Utbay Eddy’stay othermay ouldn’tway inkthay ofay anythingay osay awfulay.

Earlyay inay ethay orningmay Ikki-tikkiray amecay otay earlyay eakfastbray inay ethay erandavay
idingray onay Eddy’stay ouldershay, anday eythay avegay imhay ananabay anday omesay oiledbay
eggay. Ehay atsay onay allay eirthay apslay oneay afteray ethay otheray, ecausebay everyay
ell-brought-upway ongoosemay alwaysay opeshay otay ebay aay ousehay ongoosemay omesay ayday
anday avehay oomsray otay unray aboutay in;ay anday Ikki-tikki’sray othermay e(shay useday otay
ivelay inay ethay eneral’sgay ousehay atay Egowleesay) adhay arefullycay oldtay Ikkiray atwhay
otay oday ifay everay ehay amecay acrossay itewhay enmay.

Enthay Ikki-tikkiray entway outay intoay ethay ardengay otay eesay atwhay asway otay ebay eensay.
Itay asway aay argelay ardengay, onlyay alfhay ultivatedcay, ithway ushesbay, asay igbay asay
ummer-housessay, ofay Arshalmay Ielnay osesray, imelay anday orangeay eestray, umpsclay ofay
amboosbay, anday icketsthay ofay ighhay assgray. Ikki-tikkiray ickedlay ishay ipslay. is“Thay
isay aay endidsplay unting-ground,”hay ehay aidsay, anday ishay ailtay ewgray ottle-brushybay
atay ethay oughtthay ofay itay, anday ehay uttledscay upay anday ownday ethay ardengay, uffingsnay
erehay anday erethay illtay ehay eardhay eryvay orrowfulsay oicesvay inay aay orn-bushthay.

Itay asway Arzeeday, ethay Ailorbirdtay, anday ishay ifeway. Eythay adhay ademay aay eautifulbay
estnay ybay ullingpay otway igbay eaveslay ogethertay anday itchingstay emthay upay ethay edgesay
ithway ibersfay, anday adhay illedfay ethay ollowhay ithway ottoncay anday ownyday uffflay. Ethay
estnay ayedsway otay anday ofray, asay eythay atsay onay ethay imray anday iedcray.

at“Whay isay ethay atter?”may askeday Ikki-tikkiray.

e“Way areay eryvay iserable,”may aidsay Arzeeday. One“ay ofay ouray abiesbay ellfay outay ofay ethay
estnay yesterdayay anday Agnay ateay im.”hay

“H’m!”ay aidsay Ikki-tikkiray, at“thay isay eryvay ad--butsay Iay amay aay angerstray erehay.
Owhay isay Ag?”nay

Arzeeday anday ishay ifeway onlyay oweredcay ownday inay ethay estnay ithoutway answeringay, orfay
omfray ethay ickthay assgray atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay ushbay erethay amecay aay owlay iss--ahay
orridhay oldcay oundsay atthay ademay Ikki-tikkiray umpjay ackbay otway earclay eetfay. Enthay
inchay ybay inchay outay ofay ethay assgray oseray upay ethay eadhay anday eadspray oodhay ofay Agnay,
ethay igbay ackblay obracay, anday ehay asway ivefay eetfay onglay omfray onguetay otay ailtay.
Enwhay ehay adhay iftedlay one-thirday ofay imselfhay earclay ofay ethay oundgray, ehay ayedstay
alancingbay otay anday ofray exactlyay asay aay andelionday ufttay alancesbay inay ethay indway,
anday ehay ookedlay atay Ikki-tikkiray ithway ethay ickedway ake’ssnay eyesay atthay evernay
angechay eirthay expressionay, ateverwhay ethay akesnay aymay ebay inkingthay ofay.

o“Whay isay Ag?”nay aidsay ehay. I“ay amay Agnay. Ethay eatgray Odgay Ahmbray utpay ishay arkmay uponay
allay ouray eoplepay, enwhay ethay irstfay obracay eadspray ishay oodhay otay eepkay ethay unsay offay
Ahmbray asay ehay eptslay. Ooklay, anday ebay afraid!”ay

Ehay eadspray outay ishay oodhay oremay anthay everay, anday Ikki-tikkiray awsay ethay
ectacle-markspay onay ethay ackbay ofay itay atthay ookslay exactlyay ikelay ethay eyeay artpay
ofay aay ook-and-eyehay asteningfay. Ehay asway afraiday orfay ethay inutemay, utbay itay isay
impossibleay orfay aay ongoosemay otay aystay ightenedfray orfay anyay engthlay ofay imetay, anday
oughthay Ikki-tikkiray adhay evernay etmay aay ivelay obracay eforebay, ishay othermay adhay edfay
imhay onay eadday onesay, anday ehay ewknay atthay allay aay owngray ongoose’smay usinessbay inay
ifelay asway otay ightfay anday eatay akessnay. Agnay ewknay atthay ootay anday, atay ethay ottombay
ofay ishay oldcay earthay, ehay asway afraiday.

ell,”“Way aidsay Ikki-tikkiray, anday ishay ailtay eganbay otay uffflay upay againay, arks“may
oray onay arksmay, oday youay inkthay itay isay ightray orfay youay otay eatay edglingsflay outay ofay aay
est?”nay

Agnay asway inkingthay otay imselfhay, anday atchingway ethay eastlay ittlelay ovementmay inay
ethay assgray ehindbay Ikki-tikkiray. Ehay ewknay atthay ongoosesmay inay ethay ardengay
eantmay eathday oonersay oray aterlay orfay imhay anday ishay amilyfay, utbay ehay antedway otay etgay
Ikki-tikkiray offay ishay uardgay. Osay ehay oppeddray ishay eadhay aay ittlelay, anday utpay itay
onay oneay idesay.

et“Lay usay alk,”tay ehay aidsay. You“ay eatay eggsay. Ywhay ouldshay otnay Iay eatay irds?”bay

ehind“Bay youay! Ooklay ehindbay you!”ay angsay Arzeeday.

Ikki-tikkiray ewknay etterbay anthay otay asteway imetay inay aringstay. Ehay umpedjay upay inay
ethay airay asay ighhay asay ehay ouldcay ogay, anday ustjay underay imhay izzedwhay ybay ethay eadhay
ofay Againanay, Ag’snay ickedway ifeway. Eshay adhay eptcray upay ehindbay imhay asay ehay asway
alkingtay, otay akemay anay enday ofay imhay. Ehay eardhay erhay avagesay isshay asay ethay okestray
issedmay. Ehay amecay ownday almostay acrossay erhay ackbay, anday ifay ehay adhay eenbay anay olday
ongoosemay ehay ouldway avehay ownknay atthay enthay asway ethay imetay otay eakbray erhay ackbay
ithway oneay ite;bay utbay ehay asway afraiday ofay ethay erribletay ashinglay eturnray okestray
ofay ethay obracay. Ehay itbay, indeeday, utbay idday otnay itebay onglay enoughay, anday ehay
umpedjay earclay ofay ethay iskingwhay ailtay, eavinglay Againanay orntay anday angryay.

icked“Way, ickedway Arzee!”day aidsay Agnay, ashinglay upay asay ighhay asay ehay ouldcay eachray
owardtay ethay estnay inay ethay orn-bushthay. Utbay Arzeeday adhay uiltbay itay outay ofay eachray
ofay akessnay, anday itay onlyay ayedsway otay anday ofray.

Ikki-tikkiray eltfay ishay eyesay owinggray edray anday othay en(whay aay ongoose’smay eyesay
owgray edray, ehay isay angry)ay, anday ehay atsay ackbay onay ishay ailtay anday indhay egslay ikelay aay
ittlelay angarookay, anday ookedlay allay oundray imhay, anday atteredchay ithway ageray. Utbay
Agnay anday Againanay adhay isappearedday intoay ethay assgray. Enwhay aay akesnay issesmay itsay
okestray, itay evernay ayssay anythingay oray ivesgay anyay ignsay ofay atwhay itay eansmay otay oday
extnay. Ikki-tikkiray idday otnay arecay otay ollowfay emthay, orfay ehay idday otnay eelfay uresay
atthay ehay ouldcay anagemay otway akessnay atay onceay. Osay ehay ottedtray offay otay ethay avelgray
athpay earnay ethay ousehay, anday atsay ownday otay inkthay. Itay asway aay erioussay attermay orfay
imhay.

Ifay youay eadray ethay olday ooksbay ofay aturalnay istoryhay, youay illway indfay eythay aysay
atthay enwhay ethay ongoosemay ightsfay ethay akesnay anday appenshay otay etgay ittenbay,
ehay unsray offay anday eatsay omesay erbhay atthay urescay imhay. Atthay isay otnay uetray.
Ethay ictoryvay isay onlyay aay attermay ofay uicknessqay ofay eyeay anday uicknessqay ofay
oot--snake’sfay owblay againstay ongoose’smay ump--andjay asay onay eyeay ancay ollowfay ethay
otionmay ofay aay ake’ssnay eadhay enwhay itay ikesstray, isthay akesmay ingsthay uchmay oremay
onderfulway anthay anyay agicmay erbhay. Ikki-tikkiray ewknay ehay asway aay youngay ongoosemay,
anday itay ademay imhay allay ethay oremay easedplay otay inkthay atthay ehay adhay anagedmay otay
escapeay aay owblay omfray ehindbay. Itay avegay imhay onfidencecay inay imselfhay, anday enwhay
Eddytay amecay unningray ownday ethay athpay, Ikki-tikkiray asway eadyray otay ebay ettedpay.

Utbay ustjay asay Eddytay asway oopingstay, omethingsay iggledwray aay ittlelay inay ethay ustday,
anday aay inytay oicevay aid:say e“Bay arefulcay. Iay amay Eath!”day Itay asway Araitkay, ethay
ustyday ownbray akelingsnay atthay ieslay orfay oicechay onay ethay ustyday earth;ay anday ishay
itebay isay asay angerousday asay ethay obra’scay. Utbay ehay isay osay allsmay atthay obodynay
inksthay ofay imhay, anday osay ehay oesday ethay oremay armhay otay eoplepay.

Ikki-tikki’sray eyesay ewgray edray againay, anday ehay ancedday upay otay Araitkay ithway ethay
eculiarpay ockingray, ayingsway otionmay atthay ehay adhay inheriteday omfray ishay amilyfay.
Itay ookslay eryvay unnyfay, utbay itay isay osay erfectlypay alancedbay aay aitgay atthay youay ancay
yflay offay omfray itay atay anyay angleay youay easeplay, anday inay ealingday ithway akessnay isthay
isay anay advantageay. Ifay Ikki-tikkiray adhay onlyay ownknay, ehay asway oingday aay uchmay oremay
angerousday ingthay anthay ightingfay Agnay, orfay Araitkay isay osay allsmay, anday ancay urntay
osay uicklyqay, atthay unlessay Ikkiray itbay imhay oseclay otay ethay ackbay ofay ethay eadhay,
ehay ouldway etgay ethay eturnray okestray inay ishay eyeay oray ishay iplay. Utbay Ikkiray idday otnay
owknay. Ishay eyesay ereway allay edray, anday ehay ockedray ackbay anday orthfay, ookinglay orfay
aay oodgay aceplay otay oldhay. Araitkay uckstray outay. Ikkiray umpedjay idewayssay anday
iedtray otay unray inay, utbay ethay ickedway ittlelay ustyday aygray eadhay ashedlay ithinway aay
actionfray ofay ishay ouldershay, anday ehay adhay otay umpjay overay ethay odybay, anday ethay eadhay
ollowedfay ishay eelshay oseclay.

Eddytay outedshay otay ethay ouse:hay Oh“ay, ooklay erehay! Ouray ongoosemay isay illingkay aay
ake.”snay Anday Ikki-tikkiray eardhay aay eamscray omfray Eddy’stay othermay. Ishay atherfay
anray outay ithway aay ickstay, utbay ybay ethay imetay ehay amecay upay, Araitkay adhay ungedlay outay
onceay ootay arfay, anday Ikki-tikkiray adhay ungspray, umpedjay onay ethay ake’ssnay ackbay,
oppeddray ishay eadhay arfay etweenbay ishay orelegsfay, ittenbay asay ighhay upay ethay ackbay
asay ehay ouldcay etgay oldhay, anday olledray awayay. Atthay itebay aralyzedpay Araitkay, anday
Ikki-tikkiray asway ustjay oinggay otay eatay imhay upay omfray ethay ailtay, afteray ethay ustomcay
ofay ishay amilyfay atay innerday, enwhay ehay ememberedray atthay aay ullfay ealmay akesmay aay
owslay ongoosemay, anday ifay ehay antedway allay ishay engthstray anday uicknessqay eadyray, ehay
ustmay eepkay imselfhay inthay.

Ehay entway awayay orfay aay ustday athbay underay ethay astor-oilcay ushesbay, ilewhay
Eddy’stay atherfay eatbay ethay eadday Araitkay. at“Whay isay ethay useay ofay at?”thay oughtthay
Ikki-tikkiray. I“ay avehay ettledsay itay all;”ay anday enthay Eddy’stay othermay ickedpay
imhay upay omfray ethay ustday anday uggedhay imhay, yingcray atthay ehay adhay avedsay Eddytay
omfray eathday, anday Eddy’stay atherfay aidsay atthay ehay asway aay ovidencepray, anday Eddytay
ookedlay onay ithway igbay aredscay eyesay. Ikki-tikkiray asway atherray amuseday atay allay ethay
ussfay, ichwhay, ofay oursecay, ehay idday otnay understanday. Eddy’stay othermay ightmay ustjay
asay ellway avehay ettedpay Eddytay orfay ayingplay inay ethay ustday. Ikkiray asway oroughlythay
enjoyingay imselfhay.

Atthay ightnay atay innerday, alkingway otay anday ofray amongay ethay ine-glassesway onay ethay
abletay, ehay ightmay avehay uffedstay imselfhay eethray imestay overay ithway icenay ingsthay.
Utbay ehay ememberedray Agnay anday Againanay, anday oughthay itay asway eryvay easantplay otay ebay
attedpay anday ettedpay ybay Eddy’stay othermay, anday otay itsay onay Eddy’stay ouldershay, ishay
eyesay ouldway etgay edray omfray imetay otay imetay, anday ehay ouldway ogay offay intoay ishay onglay
arway ycray ofay ikk-tikk-tikki-tikki-tchk!”“Ray

Eddytay arriedcay imhay offay otay edbay, anday insisteday onay Ikki-tikkiray eepingslay underay
ishay inchay. Ikki-tikkiray asway ootay ellway edbray otay itebay oray atchscray, utbay asay oonsay
asay Eddytay asway asleepay ehay entway offay orfay ishay ightlynay alkway oundray ethay ousehay,
anday inay ethay arkday ehay anray upay againstay Uchundrachay, ethay uskratmay, eepingcray
arounday ybay ethay allway. Uchundrachay isay aay oken-heartedbray ittlelay eastbay. Ehay
imperswhay anday eepschay allay ethay ightnay, yingtray otay akemay upay ishay indmay otay unray
intoay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay oomray. Utbay ehay evernay etsgay erethay.

on’t“Day illkay e,”may aidsay Uchundrachay, almostay eepingway. ikki-tikki“Ray, on’tday

old“Tay youay at?”whay
