ethay arden.”gay

I“ay idn’t--soday youay ustmay elltay emay. Uickqay, Uchundrachay, oray I’llay itebay you!”ay

Uchundrachay atsay ownday anday iedcray illtay ethay earstay olledray offay ishay iskerswhay.
I“ay amay aay eryvay oorpay an,”may ehay obbedsay. I“ay evernay adhay iritspay enoughay otay unray outay
intoay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay oomray. H’shay! Iay ustn’tmay elltay youay anythingay. An’tcay
youay earhay, Ikki-tikki?”ray

Ikki-tikkiray istenedlay. Ethay ousehay asway asay illstay asay illstay, utbay ehay oughtthay ehay
ouldcay ustjay atchcay ethay aintestfay atch-scratchscray inay ethay orld--away oisenay asay
aintfay asay atthay ofay aay aspway alkingway onay aay indow-pane--theway ydray atchscray ofay aay
ake’ssnay alesscay onay ick-workbray.

at’s“Thay Agnay oray Againa,”nay ehay aidsay otay imselfhay, and“ay ehay isay awlingcray intoay
ethay ath-roombay uiceslay. You’reay ightray, Uchundra;chay Iay ouldshay avehay alkedtay otay
Ua.”chay

Ehay olestay offay otay Eddy’stay ath-roombay, utbay erethay asway othingnay erethay, anday enthay
otay Eddy’stay other’smay athroombay. Atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay oothsmay asterplay allway
erethay asway aay ickbray ulledpay outay otay akemay aay uiceslay orfay ethay athbay aterway, anday asay
Ikki-tikkiray olestay inay ybay ethay asonrymay urbcay erewhay ethay athbay isay utpay, ehay eardhay
Agnay anday Againanay isperingwhay ogethertay outsideay inay ethay oonlightmay.

en“Whay ethay ousehay isay emptieday ofay eople,”pay aidsay Againanay otay erhay usbandhay, e“hay
illway avehay otay ogay awayay, anday enthay ethay ardengay illway ebay ouray ownay againay. Ogay inay
uietlyqay, anday ememberray atthay ethay igbay anmay owhay illedkay Araitkay isay ethay irstfay
oneay otay itebay. Enthay omecay outay anday elltay emay, anday eway illway unthay orfay Ikki-tikkiray
ogether.”tay

ut“Bay areay youay uresay atthay erethay isay anythingay otay ebay ainedgay ybay illingkay ethay
eople?”pay aidsay Agnay.

Everything“ay. Enwhay erethay ereway onay eoplepay inay ethay ungalowbay, idday eway avehay anyay
ongoosemay inay ethay ardengay? Osay onglay asay ethay ungalowbay isay emptyay, eway areay ingkay
anday ueenqay ofay ethay arden;gay anday ememberray atthay asay oonsay asay ouray eggsay inay ethay
elonmay edbay atchhay as(ay eythay aymay omorrow)tay, ouray ildrenchay illway eednay oomray anday
uiet.”qay

I“ay adhay otnay oughtthay ofay at,”thay aidsay Agnay. I“ay illway ogay, utbay erethay isay onay eednay
atthay eway ouldshay unthay orfay Ikki-tikkiray afterwarday. Iay illway illkay ethay igbay anmay
anday ishay ifeway, anday ethay ildchay ifay Iay ancay, anday omecay awayay uietlyqay. Enthay ethay
ungalowbay illway ebay emptyay, anday Ikki-tikkiray illway o.”gay

Ikki-tikkiray ingledtay allay overay ithway ageray anday atredhay atay isthay, anday enthay
Ag’snay eadhay amecay oughthray ethay uiceslay, anday ishay ivefay eetfay ofay oldcay odybay
ollowedfay itay. Angryay asay ehay asway, Ikki-tikkiray asway eryvay ightenedfray asay ehay awsay
ethay izesay ofay ethay igbay obracay. Agnay oiledcay imselfhay upay, aisedray ishay eadhay,
anday ookedlay intoay ethay athroombay inay ethay arkday, anday Ikkiray ouldcay eesay ishay eyesay
itterglay.

ow“Nay, ifay Iay illkay imhay erehay, Againanay illway ow;knay anday ifay Iay ightfay imhay onay
ethay openay oorflay, ethay oddsay areay inay ishay avorfay. Atwhay amay Iay otay o?”day aidsay
Ikki-tikki-taviray.

Agnay avedway otay anday ofray, anday enthay Ikki-tikkiray eardhay imhay inkingdray omfray ethay
iggestbay ater-jarway atthay asway useday otay illfay ethay athbay. at“Thay isay ood,”gay aidsay
ethay akesnay. ow“Nay, enwhay Araitkay asway illedkay, ethay igbay anmay adhay aay ickstay. Ehay aymay
avehay atthay ickstay illstay, utbay enwhay ehay omescay inay otay athebay inay ethay orningmay ehay
illway otnay avehay aay ickstay. Iay allshay aitway erehay illtay ehay omescay. Againa--donay youay
earhay e?--Imay allshay aitway erehay inay ethay oolcay illtay aytime.”day

Erethay asway onay answeray omfray outsideay, osay Ikki-tikkiray ewknay Againanay adhay onegay
awayay. Agnay oiledcay imselfhay ownday, oilcay ybay oilcay, oundray ethay ulgebay atay ethay
ottombay ofay ethay aterway arjay, anday Ikki-tikkiray ayedstay illstay asay eathday. Afteray anay
ourhay ehay eganbay otay ovemay, usclemay ybay usclemay, owardtay ethay arjay. Agnay asway asleepay,
anday Ikki-tikkiray ookedlay atay ishay igbay ackbay, onderingway ichwhay ouldway ebay ethay
estbay aceplay orfay aay oodgay oldhay. If“ay Iay on’tday eakbray ishay ackbay atay ethay irstfay
ump,”jay aidsay Ikkiray, e“hay ancay illstay ightfay. Anday ifay ehay ights--Ofay Ikki!”ray Ehay
ookedlay atay ethay icknessthay ofay ethay ecknay elowbay ethay oodhay, utbay atthay asway ootay
uchmay orfay im;hay anday aay itebay earnay ethay ailtay ouldway onlyay akemay Agnay avagesay.

It“ay ustmay ebay ethay ead”’hay ehay aidsay atay ast;lay e“thay eadhay aboveay ethay oodhay. Anday,
enwhay Iay amay onceay erethay, Iay ustmay otnay etlay o.”gay

Enthay ehay umpedjay. Ethay eadhay asway yinglay aay ittlelay earclay ofay ethay aterway arjay,
underay ethay urvecay ofay it;ay anday, asay ishay eethtay etmay, Ikkiray acedbray ishay ackbay
againstay ethay ulgebay ofay ethay edray earthenwareay otay oldhay ownday ethay eadhay. Isthay
avegay imhay ustjay oneay econd’ssay urchasepay, anday ehay ademay ethay ostmay ofay itay. Enthay ehay
asway atteredbay otay anday ofray asay aay atray isay akenshay ybay aay og--today anday ofray onay ethay
oorflay, upay anday ownday, anday arounday inay eatgray irclescay, utbay ishay eyesay ereway edray
anday ehay eldhay onay asay ethay odybay art-whippedcay overay ethay oorflay, upsettingay ethay
intay ipperday anday ethay oapsay ishday anday ethay eshflay ushbray, anday angedbay againstay ethay
intay idesay ofay ethay athbay. Asay ehay eldhay ehay osedclay ishay awsjay ightertay anday ightertay,
orfay ehay ademay uresay ehay ouldway ebay angedbay otay eathday, anday, orfay ethay onorhay ofay ishay
amilyfay, ehay eferredpray otay ebay oundfay ithway ishay eethtay ockedlay. Ehay asway izzyday,
achingay, anday eltfay akenshay otay iecespay enwhay omethingsay entway offay ikelay aay
underclapthay ustjay ehindbay imhay. Aay othay indway ockedknay imhay enselesssay anday edray
irefay ingedsay ishay urfay. Ethay igbay anmay adhay eenbay akenedway ybay ethay oisenay, anday adhay
iredfay othbay arrelsbay ofay aay otgunshay intoay Agnay ustjay ehindbay ethay oodhay.

Ikki-tikkiray eldhay onay ithway ishay eyesay utshay, orfay ownay ehay asway uiteqay uresay ehay asway
eadday. Utbay ethay eadhay idday otnay ovemay, anday ethay igbay anmay ickedpay imhay upay anday aidsay,
It’s“ay ethay ongoosemay againay, Aliceay. Ethay ittlelay apchay ashay avedsay ouray iveslay
ow.”nay

Enthay Eddy’stay othermay amecay inay ithway aay eryvay itewhay acefay, anday awsay atwhay asway
eftlay ofay Agnay, anday Ikki-tikkiray aggeddray imselfhay otay Eddy’stay edroombay anday
entspay alfhay ethay estray ofay ethay ightnay akingshay imselfhay enderlytay otay indfay outay
etherwhay ehay eallyray asway okenbray intoay ortyfay iecespay, asay ehay anciedfay.

Enwhay orningmay amecay ehay asway eryvay iffstay, utbay ellway easedplay ithway ishay oingsday.
ow“Nay Iay avehay Againanay otay ettlesay ithway, anday eshay illway ebay orseway anthay ivefay
Agsnay, anday ere’sthay onay owingknay enwhay ethay eggsay eshay okespay ofay illway atchhay.
Oodnessgay! Iay ustmay ogay anday eesay Arzee,”day ehay aidsay.

Ithoutway aitingway orfay eakfastbray, Ikki-tikkiray anray otay ethay ornbushthay erewhay
Arzeeday asway ingingsay aay ongsay ofay iumphtray atay ethay optay ofay ishay oicevay. Ethay ewsnay
ofay Ag’snay eathday asway allay overay ethay ardengay, orfay ethay eepersway adhay ownthray ethay
odybay onay ethay ubbish-heapray.

Oh“ay, youay upidstay ufttay ofay eathers!”fay aidsay Ikki-tikkiray angrilyay. Is“ay isthay
ethay imetay otay ing?”say

ag“Nay isay ead--isday ead--isday ead!”day angsay Arzeeday. e“Thay aliantvay Ikki-tikkiray
aughtcay imhay ybay ethay eadhay anday eldhay astfay. Ethay igbay anmay oughtbray ethay
ang-stickbay, anday Agnay ellfay inay otway iecespay! Ehay illway evernay eatay ymay abiesbay
again.”ay

All“ay at’sthay uetray enoughay. Utbay ere’swhay Againa?”nay aidsay Ikki-tikkiray, ookinglay
arefullycay oundray imhay.

againa“Nay amecay otay ethay athroombay uiceslay anday alledcay orfay Ag,”nay Arzeeday entway
onay, and“ay Agnay amecay outay onay ethay enday ofay aay ick--thestay eepersway ickedpay imhay upay
onay ethay enday ofay aay ickstay anday ewthray imhay uponay ethay ubbishray eaphay. Etlay usay ingsay
aboutay ethay eatgray, ethay ed-eyedray Ikki-tikki!”ray Anday Arzeeday illedfay ishay oatthray
anday angsay.

If“ay Iay ouldcay etgay upay otay youray estnay, I’day ollray youray abiesbay out!”ay aidsay
Ikki-tikkiray. You“ay on’tday owknay enwhay otay oday ethay ightray ingthay atay ethay ightray
imetay. You’reay afesay enoughay inay youray estnay erethay, utbay it’say arway orfay emay ownday
erehay. Opstay ingingsay aay inutemay, Arzee.”day

or“Fay ethay eatgray, ethay eautifulbay Ikki-tikki’sray akesay Iay illway op,”stay aidsay
Arzeeday. at“Whay isay itay, Oay Illerkay ofay ethay erribletay Ag?”nay

ere“Whay isay Againanay, orfay ethay irdthay ime?”tay

On“ay ethay ubbishray eaphay ybay ethay ablesstay, ourningmay orfay Agnay. Eatgray isay
Ikki-tikkiray ithway ethay itewhay eeth.”tay

other“Bay ymay itewhay eethtay! Avehay youay everay eardhay erewhay eshay eepskay erhay eggs?”ay

In“ay ethay elonmay edbay, onay ethay enday earestnay ethay allway, erewhay ethay unsay ikesstray
earlynay allay ayday. Eshay idhay emthay erethay eeksway ago.”ay

And“ay youay evernay oughtthay itay orthway ilewhay otay elltay emay? Ethay enday earestnay ethay
allway, youay aid?”say

ikki-tikki“Ray, youay areay otnay oinggay otay eatay erhay eggs?”ay

ot“Nay eatay exactly;ay onay. Arzeeday, ifay youay avehay aay aingray ofay ensesay youay illway yflay
offay otay ethay ablesstay anday etendpray atthay youray ingway isay okenbray, anday etlay Againanay
asechay youay awayay otay isthay ushbay. Iay ustmay etgay otay ethay elon-bedmay, anday ifay Iay entway
erethay ownay e’dshay eesay e.”may

Arzeeday asway aay eather-brainedfay ittlelay ellowfay owhay ouldcay evernay oldhay oremay
anthay oneay ideaay atay aay imetay inay ishay eadhay. Anday ustjay ecausebay ehay ewknay atthay
Againa’snay ildrenchay ereway ornbay inay eggsay ikelay ishay ownay, ehay idn’tday inkthay atay
irstfay atthay itay asway airfay otay illkay emthay. Utbay ishay ifeway asway aay ensiblesay irdbay,
anday eshay ewknay atthay obra’scay eggsay eantmay youngay obrascay aterlay onay. Osay eshay ewflay
offay omfray ethay estnay, anday eftlay Arzeeday otay eepkay ethay abiesbay armway, anday ontinuecay
ishay ongsay aboutay ethay eathday ofay Agnay. Arzeeday asway eryvay ikelay aay anmay inay omesay
aysway.

Eshay utteredflay inay ontfray ofay Againanay ybay ethay ubbishray eaphay anday iedcray outay,
Oh“ay, ymay ingway isay okenbray! Ethay oybay inay ethay ousehay ewthray aay onestay atay emay anday
okebray it.”ay Enthay eshay utteredflay oremay esperatelyday anthay everay.

Againanay iftedlay upay erhay eadhay anday issedhay, You“ay arnedway Ikki-tikkiray enwhay Iay
ouldway avehay illedkay imhay. Indeeday anday ulytray, you’veay osenchay aay adbay aceplay otay
ebay amelay in.”ay Anday eshay ovedmay owardtay Arzee’sday ifeway, ippingslay alongay overay ethay
ustday.

e“Thay oybay okebray itay ithway aay one!”stay iekedshray Arzee’sday ifeway.

ell“Way! Itay aymay ebay omesay onsolationcay otay youay enwhay you’reay eadday otay owknay atthay Iay
allshay ettlesay accountsay ithway ethay oybay. Ymay usbandhay ieslay onay ethay ubbishray eaphay
isthay orningmay, utbay eforebay ightnay ethay oybay inay ethay ousehay illway ielay eryvay illstay.
Atwhay isay ethay useay ofay unningray awayay? Iay amay uresay otay atchcay youay. Ittlelay oolfay,
ooklay atay e!”may

Arzee’sday ifeway ewknay etterbay anthay otay oday atthay, orfay aay irdbay owhay ookslay atay aay
ake’ssnay eyesay etsgay osay ightenedfray atthay eshay annotcay ovemay. Arzee’sday ifeway
utteredflay onay, ipingpay orrowfullysay, anday evernay eavinglay ethay oundgray, anday
Againanay uickenedqay erhay acepay.

Ikki-tikkiray eardhay emthay oinggay upay ethay athpay omfray ethay ablesstay, anday ehay acedray
orfay ethay enday ofay ethay elonmay atchpay earnay ethay allway. Erethay, inay ethay armway itterlay
aboveay ethay elonsmay, eryvay unninglycay iddenhay, ehay oundfay enty-fivetway eggsay,
aboutay ethay izesay ofay aay antam’sbay eggsay, utbay ithway itishwhay inskay insteaday ofay
ellshay.

I“ay asway otnay aay ayday ootay oon,”say ehay aidsay, orfay ehay ouldcay eesay ethay abybay obrascay
urledcay upay insideay ethay inskay, anday ehay ewknay atthay ethay inutemay eythay ereway atchedhay
eythay ouldcay eachay illkay aay anmay oray aay ongoosemay. Ehay itbay offay ethay opstay ofay ethay
eggsay asay astfay asay ehay ouldcay, akingtay arecay otay ushcray ethay youngay obrascay, anday
urnedtay overay ethay itterlay omfray imetay otay imetay otay eesay etherwhay ehay adhay issedmay
anyay. Atay astlay erethay ereway onlyay eethray eggsay eftlay, anday Ikki-tikkiray eganbay otay
ucklechay otay imselfhay, enwhay ehay eardhay Arzee’sday ifeway eaming:scray

ikki-tikki“Ray, Iay edlay Againanay owardtay ethay ousehay, anday eshay ashay onegay intoay ethay
erandavay, and--ohay, omecay uickly--sheqay eansmay illing!”kay

Ikki-tikkiray ashedsmay otway eggsay, anday umbledtay ackwardbay ownday ethay elon-bedmay
ithway ethay irdthay eggay inay ishay outhmay, anday uttledscay otay ethay erandavay asay ardhay asay
ehay ouldcay utpay ootfay otay ethay oundgray. Eddytay anday ishay othermay anday atherfay ereway
erethay atay earlyay eakfastbray, utbay Ikki-tikkiray awsay atthay eythay ereway otnay eatingay
anythingay. Eythay atsay one-stillstay, anday eirthay acesfay ereway itewhay. Againanay asway
oiledcay upay onay ethay attingmay ybay Eddy’stay airchay, ithinway easyay ikingstray istanceday
ofay Eddy’stay arebay eglay, anday eshay asway ayingsway otay anday ofray, ingingsay aay ongsay ofay
iumphtray.

on“Say ofay ethay igbay anmay atthay illedkay Ag,”nay eshay issedhay, ay“stay illstay. Iay amay otnay
eadyray yetay. Aitway aay ittlelay. Eepkay eryvay illstay, allay youay eethray! Ifay youay ovemay Iay
ikestray, anday ifay youay oday otnay ovemay Iay ikestray. Ohay, oolishfay eoplepay, owhay illedkay
ymay Ag!”nay

Eddy’stay eyesay ereway ixedfay onay ishay atherfay, anday allay ishay atherfay ouldcay oday asway
otay isperwhay, it“Say illstay, Eddytay. Youay ustn’tmay ovemay. Eddytay, eepkay ill.”stay

Enthay Ikki-tikkiray amecay upay anday iedcray, urn“Tay oundray, Againanay. Urntay anday
ight!”fay

All“ay inay oodgay ime,”tay aidsay eshay, ithoutway ovingmay erhay eyesay. I“ay illway ettlesay ymay
accountay ithway youay esentlypray. Ooklay atay youray iendsfray, Ikki-tikkiray. Eythay areay
illstay anday itewhay. Eythay areay afraiday. Eythay areday otnay ovemay, anday ifay youay omecay aay
epstay earernay Iay ike.”stray

ook“Lay atay youray eggs,”ay aidsay Ikki-tikkiray, in“ay ethay elonmay edbay earnay ethay allway.
Ogay anday ooklay, Againa!”nay

Ethay igbay akesnay urnedtay alfhay arounday, anday awsay ethay eggay onay ethay erandavay. Ah-h“ay!
Ivegay itay otay e,”may eshay aidsay.

Ikki-tikkiray utpay ishay awspay oneay onay eachay idesay ofay ethay eggay, anday ishay eyesay ereway
ood-redblay. at“Whay icepray orfay aay ake’ssnay eggay? Orfay aay youngay obracay? Orfay aay
youngay ingkay obracay? Orfay ethay ast--thelay eryvay astlay ofay ethay oodbray? Ethay antsay areay
eatingay allay ethay othersay ownday ybay ethay elonmay ed.”bay

Againanay unspay earclay oundray, orgettingfay everythingay orfay ethay akesay ofay ethay oneay
eggay. Ikki-tikkiray awsay Eddy’stay atherfay ootshay outay aay igbay andhay, atchcay Eddytay
ybay ethay ouldershay, anday agdray imhay acrossay ethay ittlelay abletay ithway ethay ea-cupstay,
afesay anday outay ofay eachray ofay Againanay.

icked“Tray! Ickedtray! Ickedtray! Ikk-tck-tck!”ray uckledchay Ikki-tikkiray. e“Thay
oybay isay afesay, anday itay asway I--I--Iay atthay aughtcay Agnay ybay ethay oodhay astlay ightnay
inay ethay athroom.”bay Enthay ehay eganbay otay umpjay upay anday ownday, allay ourfay eetfay
ogethertay, ishay eadhay oseclay otay ethay oorflay. e“Hay ewthray emay otay anday ofray, utbay ehay
ouldcay otnay akeshay emay offay. Ehay asway eadday eforebay ethay igbay anmay ewblay imhay inay otway.
Iay idday itay! Ikki-tikki-tck-tckray! Omecay enthay, Againanay. Omecay anday ightfay ithway
emay. Youay allshay otnay ebay aay idowway ong.”lay

Againanay awsay atthay eshay adhay ostlay erhay ancechay ofay illingkay Eddytay, anday ethay eggay
aylay etweenbay Ikki-tikki’sray awspay. ive“Gay emay ethay eggay, Ikki-tikkiray. Ivegay emay
ethay astlay ofay ymay eggsay, anday Iay illway ogay awayay anday evernay omecay ack,”bay eshay aidsay,
oweringlay erhay oodhay.

Yes“ay, youay illway ogay awayay, anday youay illway evernay omecay ackbay. Orfay youay illway ogay
otay ethay ubbishray eaphay ithway Agnay. Ightfay, idowway! Ethay igbay anmay ashay onegay orfay ishay
ungay! Ight!”fay

Ikki-tikkiray asway oundingbay allay oundray Againanay, eepingkay ustjay outay ofay eachray
ofay erhay okestray, ishay ittlelay eyesay ikelay othay oalscay. Againanay atheredgay erselfhay
ogethertay anday ungflay outay atay imhay. Ikki-tikkiray umpedjay upay anday ackwardbay. Againay
anday againay anday againay eshay uckstray, anday eachay imetay erhay eadhay amecay ithway aay ackwhay
onay ethay attingmay ofay ethay erandavay anday eshay atheredgay erselfhay ogethertay ikelay aay
atchway ingspray. Enthay Ikki-tikkiray ancedday inay aay irclecay otay etgay ehindbay erhay, anday
Againanay unspay oundray otay eepkay erhay eadhay otay ishay eadhay, osay atthay ethay ustleray ofay
erhay ailtay onay ethay attingmay oundedsay ikelay ydray eaveslay ownblay alongay ybay ethay indway.

Ehay adhay orgottenfay ethay eggay. Itay illstay aylay onay ethay erandavay, anday Againanay amecay
earernay anday earernay otay itay, illtay atay astlay, ilewhay Ikki-tikkiray asway awingdray
eathbray, eshay aughtcay itay inay erhay outhmay, urnedtay otay ethay erandavay epsstay, anday
ewflay ikelay anay arroway ownday ethay athpay, ithway Ikki-tikkiray ehindbay erhay. Enwhay
ethay obracay unsray orfay erhay ifelay, eshay oesgay ikelay aay ip-lashwhay ickedflay acrossay aay
orse’shay ecknay.

Ikki-tikkiray ewknay atthay ehay ustmay atchcay erhay, oray allay ethay oubletray ouldway eginbay
againay. Eshay eadedhay aightstray orfay ethay onglay assgray ybay ethay orn-bushthay, anday asay
ehay asway unningray Ikki-tikkiray eardhay Arzeeday illstay ingingsay ishay oolishfay ittlelay
ongsay ofay iumphtray. Utbay Arzee’sday ifeway asway iserway. Eshay ewflay offay erhay estnay
asay Againanay amecay alongay, anday appedflay erhay ingsway aboutay Againa’snay eadhay. Ifay
Arzeeday adhay elpedhay eythay ightmay avehay urnedtay erhay, utbay Againanay onlyay oweredlay
erhay oodhay anday entway onay. Illstay, ethay instant’say elayday oughtbray Ikki-tikkiray upay
otay erhay, anday asay eshay ungedplay intoay ethay at-holeray erewhay eshay anday Agnay useday otay
ivelay, ishay ittlelay itewhay eethtay ereway enchedclay onay erhay ailtay, anday ehay entway ownday
ithway er--andhay eryvay ewfay ongoosesmay, oweverhay iseway anday olday eythay aymay ebay,
arecay otay ollowfay aay obracay intoay itsay olehay. Itay asway arkday inay ethay ole;hay anday
Ikki-tikkiray evernay ewknay enwhay itay ightmay openay outay anday ivegay Againanay oomray otay
urntay anday ikestray atay imhay. Ehay eldhay onay avagelysay, anday uckstay outay ishay eetfay otay
actay asay akesbray onay ethay arkday opeslay ofay ethay othay, oistmay earthay.

Enthay ethay assgray ybay ethay outhmay ofay ethay olehay oppedstay avingway, anday Arzeeday aidsay,
It“ay isay allay overay ithway Ikki-tikkiray! Eway ustmay ingsay ishay eathday ongsay. Aliantvay
Ikki-tikkiray isay eadday! Orfay Againanay illway urelysay illkay imhay underground.”ay

Osay ehay angsay aay eryvay ournfulmay ongsay atthay ehay ademay upay onay ethay urspay ofay ethay
inutemay, anday ustjay asay ehay otgay otay ethay ostmay ouchingtay artpay, ethay assgray uiveredqay
againay, anday Ikki-tikkiray, overedcay ithway irtday, aggeddray imselfhay outay ofay ethay
olehay eglay ybay eglay, ickinglay ishay iskerswhay. Arzeeday oppedstay ithway aay ittlelay
outshay. Ikki-tikkiray ookshay omesay ofay ethay ustday outay ofay ishay urfay anday eezedsnay.
It“ay isay allay over,”ay ehay aidsay. e“Thay idowway illway evernay omecay outay again.”ay Anday
ethay edray antsay atthay ivelay etweenbay ethay assgray emsstay eardhay imhay, anday eganbay otay
ooptray ownday oneay afteray anotheray otay eesay ifay ehay adhay okenspay ethay uthtray.

Ikki-tikkiray urledcay imselfhay upay inay ethay assgray anday eptslay erewhay ehay as--sleptway
anday eptslay illtay itay asway atelay inay ethay afternoonay, orfay ehay adhay oneday aay ardhay
ay’sday orkway.

ow,”“Nay ehay aidsay, enwhay ehay awokeay, I“ay illway ogay ackbay otay ethay ousehay. Elltay ethay
Oppersmithcay, Arzeeday, anday ehay illway elltay ethay ardengay atthay Againanay isay ead.”day

Ethay Oppersmithcay isay aay irdbay owhay akesmay aay oisenay exactlyay ikelay ethay eatingbay ofay
aay ittlelay ammerhay onay aay oppercay ot;pay anday ethay easonray ehay isay alwaysay akingmay itay
isay ecausebay ehay isay ethay owntay iercray otay everyay Indianay ardengay, anday ellstay allay
ethay ewsnay otay everybodyay owhay arescay otay istenlay. Asay Ikki-tikkiray entway upay ethay
athpay, ehay eardhay ishay attention”“ay otesnay ikelay aay inytay innerday onggay, anday
enthay ethay eadystay ing-dong-tock“Day! Agnay isay ead--dongday! Againanay isay eadday!
Ing-dong-tock!”day Atthay etsay allay ethay irdsbay inay ethay ardengay ingingsay, anday ethay
ogsfray oakingcray, orfay Agnay anday Againanay useday otay eatay ogsfray asay ellway asay ittlelay
irdsbay.

Enwhay Ikkiray otgay otay ethay ousehay, Eddytay anday Eddy’stay othermay e(shay ookedlay eryvay
itewhay illstay, orfay eshay adhay eenbay aintingfay) anday Eddy’stay atherfay amecay outay anday
almostay iedcray overay im;hay anday atthay ightnay ehay ateay allay atthay asway ivengay imhay illtay
ehay ouldcay eatay onay oremay, anday entway otay edbay onay Eddy’stay ouldershay, erewhay Eddy’stay
othermay awsay imhay enwhay eshay amecay otay ooklay atelay atay ightnay.

e“Hay avedsay ouray iveslay anday Eddy’stay ife,”lay eshay aidsay otay erhay usbandhay. ust“Jay
inkthay, ehay avedsay allay ouray ives.”lay

Ikki-tikkiray okeway upay ithway aay umpjay, orfay ethay ongoosesmay areay ightlay eepersslay.

Oh“ay, it’say you,”ay aidsay ehay. at“Whay areay youay otheringbay orfay? Allay ethay obrascay areay
eadday. Anday ifay eythay eren’tway, I’may ere.”hay

Ikki-tikkiray adhay aay ightray otay ebay oudpray ofay imselfhay. Utbay ehay idday otnay owgray ootay
oudpray, anday ehay eptkay atthay ardengay asay aay ongoosemay ouldshay eepkay itay, ithway oothtay
anday umpjay anday ingspray anday itebay, illtay evernay aay obracay aredday owshay itsay eadhay
insideay ethay allsway.




Arzee’sday Antchay

ung(Say inay onorhay ofay Ikki-tikki-taviray)

Ingersay anday ailortay amay I--ay
Oubledday ethay oysjay atthay Iay ow--knay
Oudpray ofay ymay iltlay otay ethay yskay,
Oudpray ofay ethay ousehay atthay Iay ew--say
Overay anday underay, osay eaveway Iay ymay usic--somay eaveway Iay ethay ousehay atthay Iay
ewsay.

Ingsay otay youray edglingsflay againay,
Othermay, ohay iftlay upay youray eadhay!
Evilay atthay aguedplay usay isay ainslay,
Eathday inay ethay ardengay ieslay eadday.
Errortay atthay idhay inay ethay osesray isay impotent--flungay onay ethay ung-hillday
anday eadday!

Owhay ashay eliveredday usay, owhay?
Elltay emay ishay estnay anday ishay amenay.
Ikkiray, ethay aliantvay, ethay uetray,
Ikkitay, ithway eyeballsay ofay ameflay,
Ikk-tikki-tikkiray, ethay ivory-fangeday, ethay unterhay ithway eyeballsay ofay
ameflay!

Ivegay imhay ethay Anksthay ofay ethay Irdsbay,
Owingbay ithway ailtay eathersfay eadspray!
Aisepray imhay ithway ightingalenay ords--way
Aynay, Iay illway aisepray imhay insteaday.
Earhay! Iay illway ingsay youay ethay aisepray ofay ethay ottle-tailedbay Ikkiray, ithway
eyeballsay ofay edray!

ere(_Hay Ikki-tikkiray interrupteday, anday ethay estray ofay ethay ongsay isay ost._lay)




Oomaitay ofay ethay Elephantsay

Iay illway ememberray atwhay Iay asway, Iay amay icksay ofay operay anday ain--chay
Iay illway ememberray ymay olday engthstray anday allay ymay orestfay affairsay.
Iay illway otnay ellsay ymay ackbay otay anmay orfay aay undlebay ofay ugar-cane:say
Iay illway ogay outay otay ymay ownay indkay, anday ethay ood-folkway inay eirthay airslay.

Iay illway ogay outay untilay ethay ayday, untilay ethay orningmay eak--bray
Outay otay ethay ind’sway untainteday isskay, ethay ater’sway eanclay aress;cay
Iay illway orgetfay ymay ankle-ringay anday apsnay ymay icketpay akestay.
Iay illway evisitray ymay ostlay oveslay, anday aymatesplay asterlessmay!

Alakay Agnay, ichwhay eansmay Ackblay Akesnay, adhay ervedsay ethay Indianay Overnmentgay inay
everyay ayway atthay anay elephantay ouldcay ervesay itay orfay orty-sevenfay yearsay, anday asay
ehay asway ullyfay entytway yearsay olday enwhay ehay asway aughtcay, atthay akesmay imhay earlynay
eventy--asay iperay ageay orfay anay elephantay. Ehay ememberedray ushingpay, ithway aay igbay
eatherlay adpay onay ishay oreheadfay, atay aay ungay uckstay inay eepday udmay, anday atthay asway
eforebay ethay Afghanay Arway ofay 1842, anday ehay adhay otnay enthay omecay otay ishay ullfay
engthstray.

Ishay othermay Adharay Yari,--Radhapay ethay arling,--whoday adhay eenbay aughtcay inay ethay
amesay ivedray ithway Alakay Agnay, oldtay imhay, eforebay ishay ittlelay ilkmay uskstay adhay
oppeddray outay, atthay elephantsay owhay ereway afraiday alwaysay otgay urthay. Alakay Agnay
ewknay atthay atthay adviceay asway oodgay, orfay ethay irstfay imetay atthay ehay awsay aay ellshay
urstbay ehay ackedbay, eamingscray, intoay aay andstay ofay iledpay iflesray, anday ethay
ayonetsbay ickedpray imhay inay allay ishay oftestsay acesplay. Osay, eforebay ehay asway
enty-fivetway, ehay avegay upay eingbay afraiday, anday osay ehay asway ethay est-lovedbay
anday ethay est-looked-afterbay elephantay inay ethay ervicesay ofay ethay Overnmentgay ofay
Indiaay. Ehay adhay arriedcay entstay, elvetway undredhay ounds’pay eightway ofay entstay, onay
ethay archmay inay Upperay Indiaay. Ehay adhay eenbay oistedhay intoay aay ipshay atay ethay enday ofay
aay eamstay anecray anday akentay orfay aysday acrossay ethay aterway, anday ademay otay arrycay aay
ortarmay onay ishay ackbay inay aay angestray anday ockyray ountrycay eryvay arfay omfray Indiaay,
anday adhay eensay ethay Emperoray Eodorethay yinglay eadday inay Agdalamay, anday adhay
omecay ackbay againay inay ethay eamerstay entitleday, osay ethay oldierssay aidsay, otay ethay
Abyssinianay Arway edalmay. Ehay adhay eensay ishay ellowfay elephantsay ieday ofay oldcay anday
epilepsyay anday arvationstay anday unstrokesay upay atay aay aceplay alledcay Aliay Usjidmay,
entay yearsay ater;lay anday afterwarday ehay adhay eenbay entsay ownday ousandsthay ofay ilesmay
outhsay otay aulhay anday ilepay igbay alksbay ofay eaktay inay ethay imberyardstay atay Oulmeinmay.
Erethay ehay adhay alfhay illedkay anay insubordinateay youngay elephantay owhay asway
irkingshay ishay airfay areshay ofay orkway.

Afteray atthay ehay asway akentay offay imber-haulingtay, anday employeday, ithway aay ewfay
orescay otheray elephantsay owhay ereway ainedtray otay ethay usinessbay, inay elpinghay otay
atchcay ildway elephantsay amongay ethay Arogay illshay. Elephantsay areay eryvay ictlystray
eservedpray ybay ethay Indianay Overnmentgay. Erethay isay oneay olewhay epartmentday ichwhay
oesday othingnay elseay utbay unthay emthay, anday atchcay emthay, anday eakbray emthay inay, anday
endsay emthay upay anday ownday ethay ountrycay asay eythay areay eedednay orfay orkway.

Alakay Agnay oodstay entay airfay eetfay atay ethay ouldersshay, anday ishay uskstay adhay eenbay
utcay offay ortshay atay ivefay eetfay, anday oundbay oundray ethay endsay, otay eventpray emthay
ittingsplay, ithway andsbay ofay opper;cay utbay ehay ouldcay oday oremay ithway osethay umpsstay
anthay anyay untraineday elephantay ouldcay oday ithway ethay ealray arpenedshay onesay. Enwhay,
afteray eeksway anday eeksway ofay autiouscay ivingdray ofay atteredscay elephantsay acrossay
ethay illshay, ethay ortyfay oray iftyfay ildway onstersmay ereway ivendray intoay ethay astlay
ockadestay, anday ethay igbay opdray ategay, ademay ofay eetray unkstray ashedlay ogethertay,
arredjay ownday ehindbay emthay, Alakay Agnay, atay ethay ordway ofay ommandcay, ouldway ogay

at“Whay illway eythay o?”day Ittlelay Oomaitay alledcay outay.

Ohe“ay, ittlelay oneay. Artay outhay erethay? Ellway, Iay illway elltay eethay, orfay outhay asthay
aay oolcay eadhay. Eythay illway anceday, anday itay ehoovesbay ythay atherfay, owhay ashay
eptsway allay ethay illshay ofay allay ethay elephantsay, otay ouble-chainday ishay icketspay
o-night.”tay

at“Whay alktay isay is?”thay aidsay Igbay Oomaitay. or“Fay ortyfay yearsay, atherfay anday onsay,
eway avehay endedtay elephantsay, anday eway avehay evernay eardhay uchsay oonshinemay aboutay
ances.”day

Yes;“ay utbay aay ainsmanplay owhay iveslay inay aay uthay owsknay onlyay ethay ourfay allsway
ofay ishay uthay. Ellway, eavelay ythay elephantsay unshackleday onighttay anday eesay atwhay
omescay. Asay orfay eirthay ancingday, Iay avehay eensay ethay aceplay ere--Bapree-bapwhay!
Owhay anymay indingsway ashay ethay Ihangday Iverray? Erehay isay anotheray ordfay, anday eway
ustmay imsway ethay alvescay. Opstay illstay, youay ehindbay ere.”thay

Anday inay isthay ayway, alkingtay anday anglingwray anday ashingsplay oughthray ethay iversray,
eythay ademay eirthay irstfay archmay otay aay ortsay ofay eceivingray ampcay orfay ethay ewnay
elephantsay. Utbay eythay ostlay eirthay emperstay onglay eforebay eythay otgay erethay.

Enthay ethay elephantsay ereway ainedchay ybay eirthay indhay egslay otay eirthay igbay umpsstay
ofay icketspay, anday extraay opesray ereway ittedfay otay ethay ewnay elephantsay, anday ethay
odderfay asway iledpay eforebay emthay, anday ethay illhay iversdray entway ackbay otay Etersenpay
Ahibsay oughthray ethay afternoonay ightlay, ellingtay ethay ainsplay iversdray otay ebay
extraay arefulcay atthay ightnay, anday aughinglay enwhay ethay ainsplay iversdray askeday ethay
easonray.

Ittlelay Oomaitay attendeday otay Alakay Ag’snay uppersay, anday asay eveningay ellfay,
anderedway oughthray ethay ampcay, unspeakablyay appyhay, inay earchsay ofay aay om-tomtay.
Enwhay anay Indianay ild’schay earthay isay ullfay, ehay oesday otnay unray aboutay anday akemay aay
oisenay inay anay irregularay ashionfay. Ehay itssay ownday otay aay ortsay ofay evelray allay ybay
imselfhay. Anday Ittlelay Oomaitay adhay eenbay okenspay otay ybay Etersenpay Ahibsay! Ifay ehay
adhay otnay oundfay atwhay ehay antedway, Iay elievebay ehay ouldway avehay eenbay illay. Utbay ethay
eetmeatsway ellersay inay ethay ampcay entlay imhay aay ittlelay om-tom--atay umdray eatenbay
ithway ethay atflay ofay ethay and--andhay ehay atsay ownday, oss-leggedcray, eforebay Alakay
Agnay asay ethay arsstay eganbay otay omecay outay, ethay om-tomtay inay ishay aplay, anday ehay
umpedthay anday ehay umpedthay anday ehay umpedthay, anday ethay oremay ehay oughtthay ofay ethay
eatgray onorhay atthay adhay eenbay oneday otay imhay, ethay oremay ehay umpedthay, allay aloneay
amongay ethay elephantay odderfay. Erethay asway onay unetay anday onay ordsway, utbay ethay
umpingthay ademay imhay appyhay.

Ethay ewnay elephantsay ainedstray atay eirthay opesray, anday uealedsqay anday umpetedtray
omfray imetay otay imetay, anday ehay ouldcay earhay ishay othermay inay ethay ampcay uthay uttingpay
ishay allsmay otherbray otay eepslay ithway anay olday, olday ongsay aboutay ethay eatgray Odgay
Ivshay, owhay onceay oldtay allay ethay animalsay atwhay eythay ouldshay eatay. Itay isay aay eryvay
oothingsay ullabylay, anday ethay irstfay ersevay ays:say

Ivshay, owhay ouredpay ethay arvesthay anday ademay ethay indsway otay owblay,
Ittingsay atay ethay oorwaysday ofay aay ayday ofay onglay agoay,
Avegay otay eachay ishay ortionpay, oodfay anday oiltay anday atefay,
Omfray ethay Ingkay uponay ethay uddee__gay otay ethay Eggarbay atay ethay ategay.
Allay ingsthay ademay e--Shivahay ethay Eserverpray.
Ahadeomay! Ahadeomay! Ehay ademay all--ay
Ornthay orfay ethay amelcay, odderfay orfay ethay inekay,
Anday other’smay earthay orfay eepyslay eadhay, Oay ittlelay onsay ofay inemay!

Ittlelay Oomaitay amecay inay ithway aay oyousjay unk-a-tunktay atay ethay enday ofay eachay
ersevay, illtay ehay eltfay eepyslay anday etchedstray imselfhay onay ethay odderfay atay Alakay
Ag’snay idesay. Atay astlay ethay elephantsay eganbay otay ielay ownday oneay afteray anotheray
asay isay eirthay ustomcay, illtay onlyay Alakay Agnay atay ethay ightray ofay ethay inelay asway
eftlay andingstay up;ay anday ehay ockedray owlyslay omfray idesay otay idesay, ishay earsay utpay
orwardfay otay istenlay otay ethay ightnay indway asay itay ewblay eryvay owlyslay acrossay ethay
illshay. Ethay airay asway ullfay ofay allay ethay ightnay oisesnay atthay, akentay ogethertay,
akemay oneay igbay ilence--thesay ickclay ofay oneay amboobay emstay againstay ethay otheray,
ethay ustleray ofay omethingsay aliveay inay ethay undergrowthay, ethay atchscray anday uawksqay
ofay aay alf-wakedhay irdbay irds(bay areay awakeay inay ethay ightnay uchmay oremay oftenay anthay
eway imagine)ay, anday ethay allfay ofay aterway everay osay arfay awayay. Ittlelay Oomaitay eptslay
orfay omesay imetay, anday enwhay ehay akedway itay asway illiantbray oonlightmay, anday Alakay
Agnay asway illstay andingstay upay ithway ishay earsay ockedcay. Ittlelay Oomaitay urnedtay,
ustlingray inay ethay odderfay, anday atchedway ethay urvecay ofay ishay igbay ackbay againstay
alfhay ethay arsstay inay eavenhay, anday ilewhay ehay atchedway ehay eardhay, osay arfay awayay
atthay itay oundedsay onay oremay anthay aay inholepay ofay oisenay ickedpray oughthray ethay
illnessstay, ethay oot-toot”“hay ofay aay ildway elephantay.

Allay ethay elephantsay inay ethay ineslay umpedjay upay asay ifay eythay adhay eenbay otshay, anday
eirthay untsgray atay astlay akedway ethay eepingslay ahoutsmay, anday eythay amecay outay anday
ovedray inay ethay icketpay egspay ithway igbay alletsmay, anday ightenedtay isthay operay anday
ottedknay atthay illtay allay asway uietqay. Oneay ewnay elephantay adhay earlynay ubbedgray upay
ishay icketpay, anday Igbay Oomaitay ooktay offay Alakay Ag’snay eglay ainchay anday ackledshay
atthay elephantay ore-footfay otay ind-foothay, utbay ippedslay aay ooplay ofay assgray ingstray
oundray Alakay Ag’snay eglay, anday oldtay imhay otay ememberray atthay ehay asway iedtay astfay. Ehay
ewknay atthay ehay anday ishay atherfay anday ishay andfathergray adhay oneday ethay eryvay amesay
ingthay undredshay ofay imestay eforebay. Alakay Agnay idday otnay answeray otay ethay orderay
ybay urglinggay, asay ehay usuallyay idday. Ehay oodstay illstay, ookinglay outay acrossay ethay
oonlightmay, ishay eadhay aay ittlelay aisedray anday ishay earsay eadspray ikelay ansfay, upay otay
ethay eatgray oldsfay ofay ethay Arogay illshay.

end“Tay otay imhay ifay ehay owsgray estlessray inay ethay ight,”nay aidsay Igbay Oomaitay otay
Ittlelay Oomaitay, anday ehay entway intoay ethay uthay anday eptslay. Ittlelay Oomaitay asway
ustjay oinggay otay eepslay, ootay, enwhay ehay eardhay ethay oircay ingstray apsnay ithway aay
ittlelay ang,”“tay anday Alakay Agnay olledray outay ofay ishay icketspay asay owlyslay anday asay
ilentlysay asay aay oudclay ollsray outay ofay ethay outhmay ofay aay alleyvay. Ittlelay Oomaitay
atteredpay afteray imhay, arefootedbay, ownday ethay oadray inay ethay oonlightmay, allingcay
underay ishay eathbray, ala“Kay Agnay! Alakay Agnay! Aketay emay ithway youay, Oay Alakay Ag!”nay
Ethay elephantay urnedtay, ithoutway aay oundsay, ooktay eethray idesstray ackbay otay ethay
oybay inay ethay oonlightmay, utpay ownday ishay unktray, ungsway imhay upay otay ishay ecknay,
anday almostay eforebay Ittlelay Oomaitay adhay ettledsay ishay eesknay, ippedslay intoay ethay
orestfay.

Erethay asway oneay astblay ofay uriousfay umpetingtray omfray ethay ineslay, anday enthay ethay
ilencesay utshay ownday onay everythingay, anday Alakay Agnay eganbay otay ovemay. Ometimessay
aay ufttay ofay ighhay assgray ashedway alongay ishay idessay asay aay aveway ashesway alongay ethay
idessay ofay aay ipshay, anday ometimessay aay usterclay ofay ild-pepperway inesvay ouldway
apescray alongay ishay ackbay, oray aay amboobay ouldway eakcray erewhay ishay ouldershay
ouchedtay itay. Utbay etweenbay osethay imestay ehay ovedmay absolutelyay ithoutway anyay
oundsay, iftingdray oughthray ethay ickthay Arogay orestfay asay oughthay itay adhay eenbay
okesmay. Ehay asway oinggay uphillay, utbay oughthay Ittlelay Oomaitay atchedway ethay arsstay
inay ethay iftsray ofay ethay eestray, ehay ouldcay otnay elltay inay atwhay irectionday.

Enthay Alakay Agnay eachedray ethay estcray ofay ethay ascentay anday oppedstay orfay aay inutemay,
anday Ittlelay Oomaitay ouldcay eesay ethay opstay ofay ethay eestray yinglay allay eckledspay anday
urryfay underay ethay oonlightmay orfay ilesmay anday ilesmay, anday ethay ue-whiteblay istmay
overay ethay iverray inay ethay ollowhay. Oomaitay eanedlay orwardfay anday ookedlay, anday ehay
eltfay atthay ethay orestfay asway awakeay elowbay im--awakehay anday aliveay anday owdedcray.
Aay igbay ownbray uit-eatingfray atbay ushedbray astpay ishay ear;ay aay orcupine’spay uillsqay
attledray inay ethay icket;thay anday inay ethay arknessday etweenbay ethay eetray emsstay ehay
eardhay aay og-bearhay iggingday ardhay inay ethay oistmay armway earthay, anday uffingsnay asay
itay iggedday.

Enthay ethay anchesbray osedclay overay ishay eadhay againay, anday Alakay Agnay eganbay otay ogay
ownday intoay ethay alley--notvay uietlyqay isthay imetay, utbay asay aay unawayray ungay oesgay
ownday aay eepstay ank--inbay oneay ushray. Ethay ugehay imbslay ovedmay asay eadilystay asay
istonspay, eightay eetfay otay eachay idestray, anday ethay inkledwray inskay ofay ethay elboway
ointspay ustledray. Ethay undergrowthay onay eitheray idesay ofay imhay ippedray ithway aay
oisenay ikelay orntay anvascay, anday ethay aplingssay atthay ehay eavedhay awayay ightray anday
eftlay ithway ishay ouldersshay angspray ackbay againay anday angedbay imhay onay ethay ankflay,
anday eatgray ailstray ofay eeperscray, allay attedmay ogethertay, unghay omfray ishay uskstay
asay ehay ewthray ishay eadhay omfray idesay otay idesay anday owedplay outay ishay athwaypay. Enthay
Ittlelay Oomaitay aidlay imselfhay ownday oseclay otay ethay eatgray ecknay estlay aay ingingsway
oughbay ouldshay eepsway imhay otay ethay oundgray, anday ehay ishedway atthay ehay ereway ackbay inay
ethay ineslay againay.

Ethay assgray eganbay otay etgay uashysqay, anday Alakay Ag’snay eetfay uckedsay anday uelchedsqay
asay ehay utpay emthay ownday, anday ethay ightnay istmay atay ethay ottombay ofay ethay alleyvay
illedchay Ittlelay Oomaitay. Erethay asway aay ashsplay anday aay ampletray, anday ethay ushray ofay
unningray aterway, anday Alakay Agnay odestray oughthray ethay edbay ofay aay iverray, eelingfay
ishay ayway atay eachay epstay. Aboveay ethay oisenay ofay ethay aterway, asay itay irledsway oundray
ethay elephant’say egslay, Ittlelay Oomaitay ouldcay earhay oremay ashingsplay anday omesay
umpetingtray othbay upstreamay anday own--greatday untsgray anday angryay ortingssnay, anday
allay ethay istmay aboutay imhay eemedsay otay ebay ullfay ofay ollingray, avyway adowsshay.

Ai!”“ay ehay aidsay, alfhay alouday, ishay eethtay atteringchay. e“Thay elephant-folkay areay
outay onighttay. Itay isay ethay anceday, en!”thay

Alakay Agnay ashedsway outay ofay ethay aterway, ewblay ishay unktray earclay, anday eganbay
anotheray imbclay. Utbay isthay imetay ehay asway otnay aloneay, anday ehay adhay otnay otay akemay
ishay athpay. Atthay asway ademay alreadyay, ixsay eetfay ideway, inay ontfray ofay imhay, erewhay
ethay entbay ungle-grassjay asway yingtray otay ecoverray itselfay anday andstay upay. Anymay
elephantsay ustmay avehay onegay atthay ayway onlyay aay ewfay inutesmay eforebay. Ittlelay
Oomaitay ookedlay ackbay, anday ehindbay imhay aay eatgray ildway uskertay ithway ishay ittlelay
ig’spay eyesay owingglay ikelay othay oalscay asway ustjay iftinglay imselfhay outay ofay ethay
istymay iverray. Enthay ethay eestray osedclay upay againay, anday eythay entway onay anday upay,
ithway umpetingstray anday ashingscray, anday ethay oundsay ofay eakingbray anchesbray onay
everyay idesay ofay emthay.

Atay astlay Alakay Agnay oodstay illstay etweenbay otway ee-trunkstray atay ethay eryvay optay
ofay ethay illhay. Eythay ereway artpay ofay aay irclecay ofay eestray atthay ewgray oundray anay
irregularay acespay ofay omesay eethray oray ourfay acresay, anday inay allay atthay acespay, asay
Ittlelay Oomaitay ouldcay eesay, ethay oundgray adhay eenbay ampledtray ownday asay ardhay asay
aay ickbray oorflay. Omesay eestray ewgray inay ethay entercay ofay ethay earingclay, utbay eirthay
arkbay asway ubbedray awayay, anday ethay itewhay oodway eneathbay owedshay allay inyshay anday
olishedpay inay ethay atchespay ofay oonlightmay. Erethay ereway eeperscray anginghay omfray
ethay upperay anchesbray, anday ethay ellsbay ofay ethay owersflay ofay ethay eeperscray, eatgray
axyway itewhay ingsthay ikelay onvolvulusescay, unghay ownday astfay asleepay. Utbay
ithinway ethay imitslay ofay ethay earingclay erethay asway otnay aay inglesay adeblay ofay
een--nothinggray utbay ethay ampledtray earthay.

Ethay oonlightmay owedshay itay allay ironay aygray, exceptay erewhay omesay elephantsay
oodstay uponay itay, anday eirthay adowsshay ereway inkyay ackblay. Ittlelay Oomaitay ookedlay,
oldinghay ishay eathbray, ithway ishay eyesay artingstay outay ofay ishay eadhay, anday asay ehay
ookedlay, oremay anday oremay anday oremay elephantsay ungsway outay intoay ethay openay omfray
etweenbay ethay eetray unkstray. Ittlelay Oomaitay ouldcay onlyay ountcay upay otay entay, anday
ehay ountedcay againay anday againay onay ishay ingersfay illtay ehay ostlay ountcay ofay ethay
enstay, anday ishay eadhay eganbay otay imsway. Outsideay ethay earingclay ehay ouldcay earhay
emthay ashingcray inay ethay undergrowthay asay eythay orkedway eirthay ayway upay ethay
illsidehay, utbay asay oonsay asay eythay ereway ithinway ethay irclecay ofay ethay eetray unkstray
eythay ovedmay ikelay ostsghay.

Erethay ereway ite-tuskedwhay ildway alesmay, ithway allenfay eaveslay anday utsnay anday
igstway yinglay inay ethay inkleswray ofay eirthay ecksnay anday ethay oldsfay ofay eirthay ears;ay
atfay, ow-footedslay e-elephantsshay, ithway estlessray, ittlelay inkypay ackblay
alvescay onlyay eethray oray ourfay eetfay ighhay unningray underay eirthay omachs;stay youngay
elephantsay ithway eirthay uskstay ustjay eginningbay otay owshay, anday eryvay oudpray ofay
em;thay ankylay, aggyscray old-maiday elephantsay, ithway eirthay ollowhay anxiousay
acesfay, anday unkstray ikelay oughray ark;bay avagesay olday ullbay elephantsay, arredscay
omfray ouldershay otay ankflay ithway eatgray ealsway anday utscay ofay ygonebay ightsfay,
anday ethay akedcay irtday ofay eirthay olitarysay udmay athsbay oppingdray omfray eirthay
oulders;shay anday erethay asway oneay ithway aay okenbray usktay anday ethay arksmay ofay ethay
ull-strokefay, ethay erribletay awingdray apescray, ofay aay iger’stay awsclay onay ishay
idesay.

Eythay ereway andingstay eadhay otay eadhay, oray alkingway otay anday ofray acrossay ethay oundgray
inay ouplescay, oray ockingray anday ayingsway allay ybay emselves--scoresthay anday oresscay
ofay elephantsay.

Oomaitay ewknay atthay osay onglay asay ehay aylay illstay onay Alakay Ag’snay ecknay othingnay
ouldway appenhay otay imhay, orfay evenay inay ethay ushray anday amblescray ofay aay Eddahkay ivedray
aay ildway elephantay oesday otnay eachray upay ithway ishay unktray anday agdray aay anmay offay ethay
ecknay ofay aay ametay elephantay. Anday esethay elephantsay ereway otnay inkingthay ofay enmay
atthay ightnay. Onceay eythay artedstay anday utpay eirthay earsay orwardfay enwhay eythay eardhay
ethay inkingchay ofay aay eglay ironay inay ethay orestfay, utbay itay asway Udminipay, Etersenpay
Ahib’ssay etpay elephantay, erhay ainchay appedsnay ortshay offay, untinggray, ufflingsnay
upay ethay illsidehay. Eshay ustmay avehay okenbray erhay icketspay anday omecay aightstray omfray
Etersenpay Ahib’ssay amp;cay anday Ittlelay Oomaitay awsay anotheray elephantay, oneay atthay
ehay idday otnay owknay, ithway eepday operay allsgay onay ishay ackbay anday eastbray. Ehay, ootay,
ustmay avehay unray awayay omfray omesay ampcay inay ethay illshay aboutay.

Atay astlay erethay asway onay oundsay ofay anyay oremay elephantsay ovingmay inay ethay orestfay,
anday Alakay Agnay olledray outay omfray ishay ationstay etweenbay ethay eestray anday entway intoay
ethay iddlemay ofay ethay owdcray, uckingclay anday urglinggay, anday allay ethay elephantsay
eganbay otay alktay inay eirthay ownay onguetay, anday otay ovemay aboutay.

Illstay yinglay ownday, Ittlelay Oomaitay ookedlay ownday uponay oresscay anday oresscay ofay
oadbray acksbay, anday aggingway earsay, anday ossingtay unkstray, anday ittlelay ollingray
eyesay. Ehay eardhay ethay ickclay ofay uskstay asay eythay ossedcray otheray uskstay ybay
accidentay, anday ethay ydray ustleray ofay unkstray inedtway ogethertay, anday ethay afingchay
ofay enormousay idessay anday ouldersshay inay ethay owdcray, anday ethay incessantay ickflay
anday isshhay ofay ethay eatgray ailstay. Enthay aay oudclay amecay overay ethay oonmay, anday ehay
atsay inay ackblay arknessday. Utbay ethay uietqay, eadystay ustlinghay anday ushingpay anday
urglinggay entway onay ustjay ethay amesay. Ehay ewknay atthay erethay ereway elephantsay allay
oundray Alakay Agnay, anday atthay erethay asway onay ancechay ofay ackingbay imhay outay ofay ethay
assembly;ay osay ehay etsay ishay eethtay anday iveredshay. Inay aay Eddahkay atay eastlay erethay
asway orchlighttay anday outingshay, utbay erehay ehay asway allay aloneay inay ethay arkday, anday
onceay aay unktray amecay upay anday ouchedtay imhay onay ethay eeknay.

Enthay anay elephantay umpetedtray, anday eythay allay ooktay itay upay orfay ivefay oray entay
erribletay econdssay. Ethay ewday omfray ethay eestray aboveay atteredspay ownday ikelay ainray
onay ethay unseenay acksbay, anday aay ullday oomingbay oisenay eganbay, otnay eryvay oudlay atay
irstfay, anday Ittlelay Oomaitay ouldcay otnay elltay atwhay itay asway. Utbay itay ewgray anday
ewgray, anday Alakay Agnay iftedlay upay oneay orefootfay anday enthay ethay otheray, anday
oughtbray emthay ownday onay ethay ound--one-twogray, one-twoay, asay eadilystay asay
ip-hammerstray. Ethay elephantsay ereway ampingstay allay ogethertay ownay, anday itay
oundedsay ikelay aay arway umdray eatenbay atay ethay outhmay ofay aay avecay. Ethay ewday ellfay omfray
ethay eestray illtay erethay asway onay oremay eftlay otay allfay, anday ethay oomingbay entway onay,
anday ethay oundgray ockedray anday iveredshay, anday Ittlelay Oomaitay utpay ishay andshay upay
otay ishay earsay otay utshay outay ethay oundsay. Utbay itay asway allay oneay iganticgay arjay atthay
anray oughthray im--thishay ampstay ofay undredshay ofay eavyhay eetfay onay ethay awray earthay.
Onceay oray icetway ehay ouldcay eelfay Alakay Agnay anday allay ethay othersay urgesay orwardfay
aay ewfay idesstray, anday ethay umpingthay ouldway angechay otay ethay ushingcray oundsay ofay
uicyjay eengray ingsthay eingbay uisedbray, utbay inay aay inutemay oray otway ethay oombay
ofay eetfay onay ardhay earthay eganbay againay. Aay eetray asway eakingcray anday oaninggray
omewheresay earnay imhay. Ehay utpay outay ishay armay anday eltfay ethay arkbay, utbay Alakay Agnay
ovedmay orwardfay, illstay ampingtray, anday ehay ouldcay otnay elltay erewhay ehay asway inay ethay
earingclay. Erethay asway onay oundsay omfray ethay elephantsay, exceptay onceay, enwhay otway
oray eethray ittlelay alvescay ueakedsqay ogethertay. Enthay ehay eardhay aay umpthay anday aay
uffleshay, anday ethay oomingbay entway onay. Itay ustmay avehay astedlay ullyfay otway ourshay,
anday Ittlelay Oomaitay acheday inay everyay ervenay, utbay ehay ewknay ybay ethay ellsmay ofay ethay
ightnay airay atthay ethay awnday asway omingcay.

Ethay orningmay okebray inay oneay eetshay ofay alepay yelloway ehindbay ethay eengray illshay,
anday ethay oomingbay oppedstay ithway ethay irstfay ayray, asay oughthay ethay ightlay adhay
eenbay anay orderay. Eforebay Ittlelay Oomaitay adhay otgay ethay ingingray outay ofay ishay eadhay,
eforebay evenay ehay adhay iftedshay ishay ositionpay, erethay asway otnay anay elephantay inay
ightsay exceptay Alakay Agnay, Udminipay, anday ethay elephantay ithway ethay ope-gallsray,
anday erethay asway eithernay ignsay ornay ustleray ornay isperwhay ownday ethay illsideshay otay
owshay erewhay ethay othersay adhay onegay.

Ittlelay Oomaitay aredstay againay anday againay. Ethay earingclay, asay ehay ememberedray itay,
adhay owngray inay ethay ightnay. Oremay eestray oodstay inay ethay iddlemay ofay itay, utbay ethay
undergrowthay anday ethay unglejay assgray atay ethay idessay adhay eenbay olledray ackbay.
Ittlelay Oomaitay aredstay onceay oremay. Ownay ehay understooday ethay amplingtray. Ethay
elephantsay adhay ampedstay outay oremay oom--hadray ampedstay ethay ickthay assgray anday
uicyjay anecay otay ashtray, ethay ashtray intoay iversslay, ethay iversslay intoay inytay
ibersfay, anday ethay ibersfay intoay ardhay earthay.

ah!”“Way aidsay Ittlelay Oomaitay, anday ishay eyesay ereway eryvay eavyhay. ala“Kay Agnay, ymay
ordlay, etlay usay eepkay ybay Udminipay anday ogay otay Etersenpay Ahib’ssay ampcay, oray Iay allshay
opdray omfray ythay eck.”nay

Ethay irdthay elephantay atchedway ethay otway ogay awayay, ortedsnay, eeledwhay oundray, anday
ooktay ishay ownay athpay. Ehay aymay avehay elongedbay otay omesay ittlelay ativenay ing’skay
establishmentay, iftyfay oray ixtysay oray aay undredhay ilesmay awayay.

Otway ourshay aterlay, asay Etersenpay Ahibsay asway eatingay earlyay eakfastbray, ishay
elephantsay, owhay adhay eenbay oubleday ainedchay atthay ightnay, eganbay otay umpettray, anday
Udminipay, iredmay otay ethay ouldersshay, ithway Alakay Agnay, eryvay ootsorefay, ambledshay
intoay ethay ampcay. Ittlelay Oomai’stay acefay asway aygray anday inchedpay, anday ishay
airhay asway ullfay ofay eaveslay anday encheddray ithway ewday, utbay ehay iedtray otay alutesay
Etersenpay Ahibsay, anday iedcray aintly:fay e“Thay ance--theday elephantay anceday! Iay
avehay eensay itay, and--Iay ie!”day Asay Alakay Agnay atsay ownday, ehay idslay offay ishay ecknay inay
aay eadday aintfay.

Utbay, incesay ativenay ildrenchay avehay onay ervesnay orthway eakingspay ofay, inay otway
ourshay ehay asway yinglay eryvay ontentedlycay inay Etersenpay Ahib’ssay ammockhay ithway
Etersenpay Ahib’ssay ooting-coatshay underay ishay eadhay, anday aay assglay ofay armway ilkmay,

ow“Nay, ifay Iay ielay inay oneay ordway, endsay enmay otay eesay, anday eythay illway indfay atthay ethay

Agnay ooktay emay, anday Iay awsay. Alsoay Alakay Agnay isay eryvay eg-weary!”lay

Ittlelay Oomaitay aylay ackbay anday eptslay allay oughthray ethay onglay afternoonay anday intoay
ethay ilighttway, anday ilewhay ehay eptslay Etersenpay Ahibsay anday Achuamay Appaay ollowedfay
ethay acktray ofay ethay otway elephantsay orfay ifteenfay ilesmay acrossay ethay illshay.
Etersenpay Ahibsay adhay entspay eighteenay yearsay inay atchingcay elephantsay, anday ehay
adhay onlyay onceay eforebay oundfay uchsay aay ance-placeday. Achuamay Appaay adhay onay eednay
otay ooklay icetway atay ethay earingclay otay eesay atwhay adhay eenbay oneday erethay, oray otay
atchscray ithway ishay oetay inay ethay ackedpay, ammedray earthay.

e“Thay ildchay eaksspay uth,”tray aidsay ehay. All“ay isthay asway oneday astlay ightnay, anday

Eythay ookedlay atay oneay anotheray anday upay anday ownday, anday eythay onderedway. Orfay ethay

athomfay.

orty“Fay yearsay anday ive,”fay aidsay Achuamay Appaay, ave“hay Iay ollowedfay ymay ordlay, ethay

Enwhay eythay otgay ackbay otay ampcay itay asway imetay orfay ethay eveningay ealmay. Etersenpay
Ahibsay ateay aloneay inay ishay enttay, utbay ehay avegay ordersay atthay ethay ampcay ouldshay
avehay otway eepshay anday omesay owlsfay, asay ellway asay aay oubleday ationray ofay ourflay anday
iceray anday altsay, orfay ehay ewknay atthay erethay ouldway ebay aay eastfay.

Igbay Oomaitay adhay omecay upay otfoothay omfray ethay ampcay inay ethay ainsplay otay earchsay orfay
ishay onsay anday ishay elephantay, anday ownay atthay ehay adhay oundfay emthay ehay ookedlay atay
emthay asay oughthay ehay ereway afraiday ofay emthay othbay. Anday erethay asway aay eastfay ybay
ethay azingblay ampfirescay inay ontfray ofay ethay ineslay ofay icketedpay elephantsay,
anday Ittlelay Oomaitay asway ethay erohay ofay itay allay. Anday ethay igbay ownbray elephantay
atcherscay, ethay ackerstray anday iversdray anday opersray, anday ethay enmay owhay owknay allay
ethay ecretssay ofay eakingbray ethay ildestway elephantsay, assedpay imhay omfray oneay otay
ethay otheray, anday eythay arkedmay ishay oreheadfay ithway oodblay omfray ethay eastbray ofay aay
ewlynay illedkay ungle-cockjay, otay owshay atthay ehay asway aay oresterfay, initiateday anday
eefray ofay allay ethay unglesjay.

Anday atay astlay, enwhay ethay amesflay iedday ownday, anday ethay edray ightlay ofay ethay ogslay
ademay ethay elephantsay ooklay asay oughthay eythay adhay eenbay ippedday inay oodblay ootay,
Achuamay Appaay, ethay eadhay ofay allay ethay iversdray ofay allay ethay Eddahs--Machuakay
Appaay, Etersenpay Ahib’ssay otheray elfsay, owhay adhay evernay eensay aay ademay oadray inay
ortyfay years:ay Achuamay Appaay, owhay asway osay eatgray atthay ehay adhay onay otheray amenay
anthay Achuamay Appa,--leapeday otay ishay eetfay, ithway Ittlelay Oomaitay eldhay ighhay inay
ethay airay aboveay ishay eadhay, anday outed:shay isten“Lay, ymay othersbray. Istenlay, ootay,
youay ymay ordslay inay ethay ineslay erethay, orfay Iay, Achuamay Appaay, amay eakingspay! Isthay
ittlelay oneay allshay onay oremay ebay alledcay Ittlelay Oomaitay, utbay Oomaitay ofay ethay
Elephantsay, asay ishay eat-grandfathergray asway alledcay eforebay imhay. Atwhay evernay
anmay ashay eensay ehay ashay eensay oughthray ethay onglay ightnay, anday ethay avorfay ofay ethay
elephant-folkay anday ofay ethay Odsgay ofay ethay Unglesjay isay ithway imhay. Ehay allshay

ains,”--hechay irledwhay upay ethay inelay ofay ickets--“herepay isay ethay ittlelay oneay

Anday atay atthay astlay ildway yellay ethay olewhay inelay ungflay upay eirthay unkstray illtay ethay
ipstay ouchedtay eirthay oreheadsfay, anday okebray outay intoay ethay ullfay alute--thesay
ashingcray umpet-pealtray atthay onlyay ethay Iceroyvay ofay Indiaay earshay, ethay Alaamutsay
ofay ethay Eddahkay.

Utbay itay asway allay orfay ethay akesay ofay Ittlelay Oomaitay, owhay adhay eensay atwhay evernay
anmay adhay eensay efore--thebay anceday ofay ethay elephantsay atay ightnay anday aloneay inay
ethay earthay ofay ethay Arogay illshay!

Erhay Ajesty’smay Ervantssay

Youay ancay orkway itay outay ybay Actionsfray oray ybay implesay Uleray ofay Eethray,
Utbay ethay ayway ofay Eedle-dumtway isay otnay ethay ayway ofay Eedle-deetway.
Youay ancay isttway itay, youay ancay urntay itay, youay ancay aitplay itay illtay youay opdray,
Utbay ethay ayway ofay Illypay Inky’sway otnay ethay ayway ofay Inkieway Oppay!

Itay adhay eenbay ainingray eavilyhay orfay oneay olewhay onth--rainingmay onay aay ampcay
ofay irtythay ousandthay enmay anday ousandsthay ofay amelscay, elephantsay, orseshay,
ullocksbay, anday ulesmay allay atheredgay ogethertay atay aay aceplay alledcay Awalray Indipay,
otay ebay eviewedray ybay ethay Iceroyvay ofay Indiaay. Ehay asway eceivingray aay isitvay omfray
ethay Amiray ofay Afghanistan--aay ildway ingkay ofay aay eryvay ildway ountrycay. Ethay Amiray
adhay oughtbray ithway imhay orfay aay odyguardbay eightay undredhay enmay anday orseshay owhay
adhay evernay eensay aay ampcay oray aay ocomotivelay eforebay inay eirthay ives--savagelay
enmay anday avagesay orseshay omfray omewheresay atay ethay ackbay ofay Entralcay Asiaay. Everyay
ightnay aay obmay ofay esethay orseshay ouldway ebay uresay otay eakbray eirthay eelhay opesray anday
ampedestay upay anday ownday ethay ampcay oughthray ethay udmay inay ethay arkday, oray ethay amelscay
ouldway eakbray ooselay anday unray aboutay anday allfay overay ethay opesray ofay ethay entstay,
anday youay ancay imagineay owhay easantplay atthay asway orfay enmay yingtray otay ogay otay eepslay.
Ymay enttay aylay arfay awayay omfray ethay amelcay ineslay, anday Iay oughtthay itay asway afesay.
Utbay oneay ightnay aay anmay oppedpay ishay eadhay inay anday outedshay, et“Gay outay, uickqay!
Ey’rethay omingcay! Ymay ent’stay one!”gay

Iay ewknay owhay ey”“thay ereway, osay Iay utpay onay ymay ootsbay anday aterproofway anday uttledscay
outay intoay ethay ushslay. Ittlelay Ixenvay, ymay oxfay erriertay, entway outay oughthray ethay
otheray ide;say anday enthay erethay asway aay oaringray anday aay untinggray anday ubblingbay,
anday Iay awsay ethay enttay avecay inay, asay ethay olepay appedsnay, anday eginbay otay anceday
aboutay ikelay aay admay ostghay. Aay amelcay adhay underedblay intoay itay, anday etway anday angryay
asay Iay asway, Iay ouldcay otnay elphay aughinglay. Enthay Iay anray onay, ecausebay Iay idday otnay
owknay owhay anymay amelscay ightmay avehay otgay ooselay, anday eforebay onglay Iay asway outay ofay
ightsay ofay ethay ampcay, owingplay ymay ayway oughthray ethay udmay.

Atay astlay Iay ellfay overay ethay ail-endtay ofay aay ungay, anday ybay atthay ewknay Iay asway
omewheresay earnay ethay artilleryay ineslay erewhay ethay annoncay ereway ackedstay atay
ightnay. Asay Iay idday otnay antway otay owterplay aboutay anyay oremay inay ethay izzledray anday
ethay arkday, Iay utpay ymay aterproofway overay ethay uzzlemay ofay oneay ungay, anday ademay aay
ortsay ofay igwamway ithway otway oray eethray ammersray atthay Iay oundfay, anday aylay alongay ethay
ailtay ofay anotheray ungay, onderingway erewhay Ixenvay adhay otgay otay, anday erewhay Iay ightmay
ebay.

Ustjay asay Iay asway ettinggay eadyray otay ogay otay eepslay Iay eardhay aay inglejay ofay arnesshay
anday aay untgray, anday aay ulemay assedpay emay akingshay ishay etway earsay. Ehay elongedbay otay
aay ew-gunscray atterybay, orfay Iay ouldcay earhay ethay attleray ofay ethay apsstray anday ingsray
anday ainschay anday ingsthay onay ishay addlesay adpay. Ethay ew-gunsscray areay inytay ittlelay
annoncay ademay inay otway iecespay, atthay areay ewedscray ogethertay enwhay ethay imetay omescay
otay useay emthay. Eythay areay akentay upay ountainsmay, anywhereay atthay aay ulemay ancay indfay
aay oadray, anday eythay areay eryvay usefulay orfay ightingfay inay ockyray ountrycay.

Ehindbay ethay ulemay erethay asway aay amelcay, ithway ishay igbay oftsay eetfay uelchingsqay
anday ippingslay inay ethay udmay, anday ishay ecknay obbingbay otay anday ofray ikelay aay
ayedstray en’shay. Uckilylay, Iay ewknay enoughay ofay eastbay anguage--notlay ild-beastway
anguagelay, utbay amp-beastcay anguagelay, ofay ourse--fromcay ethay ativesnay otay owknay
atwhay ehay asway ayingsay.

Ehay ustmay avehay eenbay ethay oneay atthay oppedflay intoay ymay enttay, orfay ehay alledcay otay
ethay ulemay, at“Whay allshay Iay oday? Erewhay allshay Iay ogay? Iay avehay oughtfay ithway aay itewhay
ingthay atthay avedway, anday itay ooktay aay ickstay anday ithay emay onay ethay eck.”nay at(Thay asway
ymay okenbray enttay olepay, anday Iay asway eryvay adglay otay owknay it.ay) all“Shay eway unray on?”ay

uchmay otay unray away--ifay Iay asway ikelay imhay Iay ouldcay ullpay ethay unsgay. Utbay ifay Iay ereway
asay iseway asay allay atthay Iay ouldshay evernay ebay erehay. Iay ouldshay ebay aay ingkay inay ethay
orestfay, asay Iay useday otay ebay, eepingslay alfhay ethay ayday anday athingbay enwhay Iay ikedlay.

Ethay igbay aradepay ofay allay ethay irtythay ousandthay enmay asway eldhay atthay afternoonay,
